Ol lain i lukim ol blakpela klaut we i no save kamap long taim bilong volkeno pairap long as bilong maunten.

Luno i gat 120-160 'cubic metre' bilong 'fuel' i stap long em taim i stop long ron na ol strongpela win na sibruk i pusim em i go insait long 'breakwater'.

Dispela 100-mita sip i wok long go long kisim 'fertiliser' kago we em i save kisim long olgeta taim na pastaim ol ofisa i pret olsem dispela sip i ken kapsaitim wanpela 'load'.
Dispela senis long lo em tupela haus wantaim i bin wanbel long em long 2011.
Ol i bin mekim wanpela senis long dispela 'legislative session' taim House of Representatives i rausim namba tu sentens pastaim na bihain Senate i wanbel long dispela long Mande.
Dispela samting we i no stret long namba tu sentens, we i tok olsem ol i mas tok tambu long tupela man i marit o tupela meri i marit, na dispela i ken opim dua long ol dispela kain marit long kamap long bihaintaim.
Bihain long dispela proses (process), narapela 'legislature' we ol i makim long 2015 o 2016 bai i lukluk gen long HJR-3 long mekim em i stap insait long proses.

Karno em i wanpela tisa bilong English we planti lain i save long em na tu i no save wanbel long sampela wok bilong em we i bin tis aninit long Modern Education na King's Glory na em i bin tok olsem em i gat 9,000 sumatin taim wok bilong em kamap gut tru.
Long ol 'notes' bilong em we em i yusim sampela ol toktok we ol papamama i ting olsem ol i strong tumas, na ol i ripot olsem em i save yusim tok nogut insait long klas (class).

Na tu, ol i sutim tok long em long brukim lo bilong 'copyright infringement', tasol ol i no sasim em long dispela.

Long tripela ten yia i go pinis, maski em i stap olsem wanpela 'communist state', China i kamapim wanpela 'market economy'.

Tropical Storm Danielle, we ol i kolim olsem namba foa 'storm' bilong 2010 Hurricane sisen (season), em i wok long redi long kirap long 'eastern' Atlantic Ocean.

Bobek i bon long kapitel bilong Croatia, Zagreb, na planti lain i save long em taim em i pilai long Partizan Belgrade.

No gat narapela lain i bin pilai long dispela namba bilong ol geim (game) o skorim (score) moa gol long dispela klab olsem Bobek.
Long 1995 ol i votim (vote) em olsem nambawan pleiya (player) insait long histori bilong Partizan.

Ol helt wokmanmeri i hariap long wok long em na ol i kisim em i go long wanpela lokel haus sik we em i stap long en na bihain em i dai.
Zayat i no kisim wanpela bagarap insait long dispela eksiden.
Long sait bilong dispela hevi bilong fainens (finance) long graun, Zapatero i kontinu (continue) na i tok olsem "'financial system' em i wanpela pat bilong ekonomi (economy), wanpela impoten pat.
Mipela i gat wanpela longpela yia bilong 'financial crises', we nogut bilong em i kamap long tupela mun i go pinis, na mi ting olsem nau ol 'financial market' i wok long kamap orait gen."
Long wik i go pinis, Naked News i tokaut olsem em i bai i apim oda bilong em long mekim 'news reporting' insait ol intanesinol tok ples ', wantaim tripela nupela 'broadcast'.
Em i wok long mekim 'reporting' long English na Japanese, dispela 'global organization' i presentim ol progren long tok ples Spanish, Italian, na Korean, long televisen, long intanet, na long ol mobail divais (mobile device).
Laki (lucky) na no gat samting i kamap long mi, tasol mi lukim wanpela samting we i mekim mi pret, taim ol manmeri i wok long traim long brukim windua na kam autsait.
Ol manmeri i wok long paitim ol glas wantaim ol sia, tasol ol windua i no inap long bruk.
"Wanpela bilong ol glas i bruk, na ol i stat long kam autsait long windua," man we i bin stap insait long dispela hevi Franciszek Kowal i tok.
Ol sta i save givim lait na hot bikos long eneji (enegry) we i kamap taim ol 'hydrogen atom' i pas (o 'fuse') wantaim long kamap ol narapela 'element' we i hevi moa.
Ol saintis i wok long kamapim wanpela 'reactor' we i ken kamapim eneji (energy) long wankain we.
Dispela, em i wanpela hatpela problem tru long painim ansa bilong em na em bai i kisim planti yia bipo long mipela i ken lukim ol lain i bildim ol 'fusion reactor'.
Dispela 'steel needle' i trip anatp long wara bikos long 'surface tension'.
'Surface tension' i save kamap taim ol 'water molecule' long antap bilong wara i 'attract' long ol yet moa long ol i 'attract' i go long ol 'air molecules' i stap antap long ol.
Dispela ol 'water molecule' i mekim wanpela skin antap long wara we ai bilong yumi i no inap long lukim na ol i mekim ol kain ol samting olsem ol 'needle' long trip antap long wara.
Dispela 'blade' i satp long wanpela 'ice skate' bilong tude i gat 'double edge' na i gat wanpela hol i stap namellong dispela tuple 'edge'. Dispela tupela 'edge' i save mekim isi long 'blade' i holimpasim ais, maski taim em i tanim liklik.
Bikos aninit bilong dispela 'blade' em i 'curve' liklik, taim 'blade' i tanim liklik i go long wanpela sait, 'edge' bilong em i pas yet wantaim ais na i tanim.
Dispela i save mekim 'skater' i tanim. Sapos ol 'skate' i tanim i go long rait sait, 'skater' bai tanim i go long rait sait, na sapos ol 'skates' i tanim i go long lep sait, 'skater' bai tanim i go long lep sait.
Long go bek long level bilong eneji (energy) we ol i bin stap long en, ol i mas rausim ol narapela eneji we ol i kisim long lait.
Ol bai mekim dispela taim ol salim wanpela liklik patikel (particle) bilong lait we ol i kolim olsem wanpela "photon".
Ol saintis i kolim dispela proses (process) olsem "'stimulated emission of radiation'" bikos lait i mekim ol 'atom' i senis na i kamapim 'emission' bilong wanpela 'photon' bilong lait, na lait em i wanpela kain 'radiation'.
Dispela narapela piksa i soim ol 'atom' i rausim ol 'photon'. Na, trutru ol 'photon' i liklik moa long ol dispela i stap insait long piksa.
Ol 'photon' i liklik moa long ol samting we i mekim ol 'atom'!
Taim em i wok long planti handret aua, 'filament' insait long balb (bulb) i save kuk na lait balb i no save wok.
Yumi nid long senisim dispela lait balb (bulb). Em i impoten olsem yumi mas was gut taim yumi senisim lait balb.
Pastaim, 'switch' bilong dispela lait em yumi mas ofim o yumi mas diskonektim (disconnect) 'cable'.
Dispela em bikos ilektrisiti (electricity) i wok long ron i go insait long 'socket' we hap bilong balb (bulb) i gat metel (metal) long em i save sindaun na dispela i ken givim yu bikpela 'electric shock' sapos yu tasim insait bilong 'socket' o metel hap bilong balb taim em i pas liklik yet long 'socket'.
Dispela impoten hap bilong 'circulatory system' em i hat, we i save pamim blut.
Blut i save lusim hat long ol tiub (tube) ol i kolim ol 'artery' na ol i save kam bek long hat long ol tiub (tube) ol i kolim 'veins'. Ol liklik tiub tru em ol i kolim 'capillaries'.
Tit bilong wanpela 'triceratop' em bai inap long kaikai ol lip na ol stronpela han na rut (root) bilong diwai.
Sampela saintis i ting olsem ol Triceratop i bin kaikai ol 'cycad', wanpela kain plent (plant) we i save gro long planti hap long Cretaceous.
Ol dispela plent (plant) i luk olsem ol liklik pam (palm) diwai we i gat 'crown' we ol longpela sap lip i kamapim.
Wanpela Triceratopo i inap long yusim strongpela bik (beak) bilong em long rausim ol lip bipo long em i kaikai namel bilong dispela diwai.
Ol narapela saintis i tok pait olsem dispela ol plent (plant) ol i pulap long poisin olsem na ol dainaso i no inap long kaikaim ol, maski long tude, ol 'sloth' na ol narapela animal olsem ol 'parrot' (wanpela tumbuna bilong ol dainaso) i ken kaikai ol lip o frut we i gat poisin long en.
Wanem kain we bai 'gravity' bilong 'lo' i pulim mi? Sapos yu sanap antap long graun bilong 'lo', hevi bilong yu bai i liklik moa long hevi bilong yu long Earth.
Wanpela man we i hevi bilong em i 200 paun (90kg) long Earth em bai hevi bilong em i kamap olsem 36 paun (16kg) antap long 'lo'. Olsem na 'gravity', em nau, bai i pulim yu long mak we i liklik moa.
Sun i no gat wanpela 'crust' olsem Earth we yu ken sanap long em. Olgeta hap bilong Sun em ol ges (gas), paia, na 'plasma'.
Mak bilong ol ges (gas) i kamap liklik moa taim yu go longwe long namel bilong Sun.
Autsait hap we yumi save lukim taim yumi lukluk long Sun em ol i save kolim 'photosphere', dispela em i min olsem "bal we i lait".
Kain olsem tri tausen yia bihain, long 1610, wanpela 'astronomer' bilong Italu Galileo Galilei i yusim wanpela 'telescope' long lukim olsem Venus em i gat ol 'phase' bilong em, wankain olsem mun i gat.
Ol 'phase' i save kamap bikos dispela sait bilong Venus (o bilong Moon) we i tanim i kam long Sun em lait i save kisim. Dispela 'phase' bilong Venus em i sapotim tingting bilong Copernicus olsem ol plenet (planet) i save go raunim Sun.
Orait, bihain long sampela yia long 1639, wanpela 'astronomer' bilong England nem bilong em Jeremiah Harrocks i lukim wanpela samting ol i kolim 'transit of Venus'.
Taim ol i winim Danelaw long namba tu taim, no gat pait i kamap long England na ol i stap gut longpela taim.
Tasol long yia 991, Ethelred i bungim bikpela namba bilong ol Viking sip we i bikpela moa long olgeta narapela grup sip i bin i stap bihain long taim bilong Guthrum 100 yia i go pinis.
Dispela ol sip bilong pait em Olaf Trygvasson, wanpela man bilong Norway i go pas long ol. Olaf i laik kisim bek kantri bilong em long ol Danes, husat i wok long bosim i stap long dispela taim.
Bihain long ol samting i no kamap gut long ol soldia, Ethelred i wanbel long wanem ol samting Olaf i tok long en, na Olaf i go bek long Norway long traim na kisim bek kingdom bilong em. Em i winim sampela samting, tasol sampela samting i no kamap gut long em.
Hanguel em i wanpela 'alphabet' we ol i wokim na planti lain i bin yusim long olgeta de. Dispela 'alphabet' em ol i bin kamapim long 1444 long taim King Sejong (1418 – 1450) i bin king.
King Sejong em i namba foa king bilong Joseon Dynasty na em i wanpela bilong ol king ol lain i save givim bikpela rispek long em.
Em i bin kolim Hangeul alphabet olsem Hunmin Jeongeum, dispela em i min olsem "ol stretpela saun bilong givim tok skul long ol manmeri".
I gat planti tingting long wanem we Sanskrit i kamap. Wanpela bilong ol em i toktok long wanpela lain Aryan long hap wes i go insait long India na i karim dispela tok ples i go wantaim ol.
Sanskrit em i wanpela tok ples bilong bipo na em i klostu wankain olsem tok ples Latin we ol i save yusim long Europe.
Olpela buk tru long olgeta hap bilong graun em ol i raitim long tok ples Sanskrit. Bihain long ol i raitim Upanishads, no gat lain i yusim Sanskrit moa bikos ol bikman we i gat pawa na atoriti tasol i bin yusim.
Sanskrit em i wanpela tok ples we i narakain na i gat planti bikpela hap tok, we i bin stap olsem mama bilong ol narapela tok ples bilong tude long India, wankain olsem Latin em i mama bilong ol tok ples olsem French na Spanish.
Taim pait bilong France i pinis, Germany i stat long redi long kisim ailan bilong Britain.
Germany i givim 'code-name' long dispela pait olsem “Operation Sealion”. Planti bilong ol bikpela wepon (weapon) bilong British Army em ol i bin lus taim ol i lusim Dunkirk, olsem na ami bilong ol i no gat strong bilong pait.
Tasol Royal Navy bilong ol em i strong moa long German Navy (“Kriegsmarine”) na ol i inap long bagarapim ol lain bilong pait we i kam long English Channel.
Tasol, wanwan bilong ol sip bilong Royal Navy i stap klostu long ol dispela rot bilong ol birua long kam bikos ol 'admiral' i pret olsem ol balus bilong Germany bai i bagarapim ol.
Yumi bai stat wantaim stori bilong plen bilong Italy. Italy em i stap olsem "liklik brata" bilong Germany na Japan.
Ami bilong em i no strong na navy bilong em i no strong, maski nau tasol i bildim foapela nupela sip bipo long woa i stat.
Namba wan as tingting bilong Italy em long kisim ol kantri long Africa. Long holimpasim ol dispela kantri, ol i mas i gat hap bilong salim ol man bilong pait, olsem na ol man bilong pait bai i sel long Mediterranean Sea na kisim Africa.
Long mekim dispela, ol i mas rausim ol senta bilong ol sip bilong Britain we i stap long Egypt. Wantaim dispela, ol 'battleship' bilong Italy i no sapos long mekim narapela samting moa.
Nau long Japan. Japan em wanplela ailan kantri, wankain olsem Britain.
Ol 'Submarines' em ol sip we ol i disainim (design) long em i ken ron aninit long wara, na i stap long hap long longpela taim.
Ol lain i bin yusim ol 'submarine' long World War I na World War II. Long dispela taim ol i save ron isi isi tru na i no save sutim samting we i stap longwe long ol.
Long stat bilong woa ol i save ron klostu tru long antap bilong solwara, tasol taim ol lainim ol 'radar' bilong painim ol sip na balus na ol dispela 'radar' i wok long kamap gut, ol 'submarine i mas i go aninit long wara na ol bai i no inap long lukim ol.
Ol 'submarine' bilong German em ol i kolim ol U-Boats. Ol German i save gut tru long mekim 'navigation' na 'operation' long ol 'submarine' bilong ol.
Bikos ol i wok gut wantaim ol 'submarine', bihain long woa ol i no trastim ol German long i gat ol 'submarine'.
Yes! King Tutankhamun, sampela taim ol i save kolim em olsem "King Tut" o "The Boy King", em i wanpela bilong ol king bilong Egypt long bipotaim we planti manmeri i save long em long tude.
Wanpela samting we i narakain em i olsem, ol lain bilong bipo i no ting olsem em i impoten tumas na ol i no putim nem bilong em insait long planti bilong ol list bilong ol king bilong bipotaim.
Tasol, ol i bin painim 'tomb' bilong em long 1922 na dispela i mekim na planti manmeri i save long em. Taim planti bilong ol 'tomb' bilong bipo em ol lain i bin i go insait long em na stilim ol samting, dispela 'tomb' em ol i no bin tasim.
Planti bilong ol samting we ol i putim wantaim Tutankhamun em ol i bin stap gut, wantaim tausim ol 'artefact' we ol i mekim long ol 'precious metals' na ol ston we i dia tumas.
Dispela 'spoke wheel' i mekim ol 'chariot' bilong Assyria i no gat hevi, i ron hariap moa, na i redi long winim ol soldia na ol narapela 'chariot'.
Ol spia bilong ol bunara bilong kilim man i ken go insait long klos pait bilong ol birua soldia. Long kain olsem 1000 B.C., ol Assyria i gat namba wan 'calvary'.
Wanpela 'calvary' em i wanpela ami we i save sindaun long hos na pait. Long dispela taim, ol i no bin wokim ol 'saddle' yet, olsem na ol Assyria i save sindaun antap nating long baksait bilong ol hos bilong ol taim ol i pait.
Yumi save long planti ol 'politician', saintis, na ol 'artist' bilong ol Greece. I luk olsem wanpela man bilong dispela kalsa we planti manmeri i save long en em i Homer, dispela 'poet' we i aipas, husat i kamapim tupela 'masterpieces' bilong 'Greek literature: dispela tupela 'poem' Iliad na Odyssey.
Sophocles na Aristophanes em ol 'playwrites' we planti lain i save long en na ol drama bilong ol em ol save lain i save tok olsem ol i wanpela bilong ol nambawan wok insait long 'world literatue'.
Wanpela narapela man long Greek we planti lain i save long en em Pythagoras, planti lain i save long em bikos long 'theorem' bilong em long ol sait bilong ol 'right triangles'.
I gat kainkain namba bilong ol lain i save toktok long Hindi. Ol i estimetim (estimate) olsem em i stap namel long namba tu na namba foa tok ples we planti manmeri long graun i save yusim.
Namba bilong ol 'native speaker' em i bihainim sapos ol i wankain ol i no wankain long ol 'dialect' we ol i wok long kaunim.
Ol i estimet (estimate) namba i stap namel long 340 milien i go long 500 milien manmeri we i save toktok long dispela tok ples, na kain olsem 800 milien manmeri i ken harim na save long dispela tok ples.
Hindi na Urdu em ol i wankain long toktok tasol we ol i raitim em i narakain; long olgeta de, ol lain i save toktok long dispela tupela tok ples i save harim wanpela narapela.
Long kain taim olsem 15th century, long hap not bilong Estonia i bin stap aninit long Germany na i bihainim kalsa bilong em.
Sampela bilong ol bruder bilong ol Germany i laik bringim God i kam klostu long ol manmeri bilong dispela ples, olsem na ol i kamapim tok ples bilong Estonia na dispela tok ples i no gat tok piksa insait long en.
Dispela tok ples em i gat 'alphbet' bilong Germany na wanpela 'character' moa "Õ/õ" em ol i putim.
Bihain long sampela taim, planti wod we ol i kisim long tok ples i bung wantaim. Dispela em i stat bilong 'enlightenment'.
Long pasin bilong bipo, dispela man husat bai i kisim sia king i mas i go long 'military' bihain long em i pinisim skul.
Tasol, Charles i go long univesiti long Trinity College, long Cambridge we em i stadim Anthropology na Archaeology, na bihain History, na em i kisim 2:2 (wanpela 'lower second class degree).
Charles em i namba wan memba bilong British Royal Family long kisim wanpela 'degree' pepa.
European Turkey (eastern Thrace o Rumelia insait long Balkan peninsula) i kamapim 3% bilong dispela kantri.
Dispela teritori (territory) longpela bilong em i moa long 1,600 kilomita (1,000 mi) na bikpela bilong em i 800 km (500 mi), na seip (shape) bilong i klostu wankain olsem wanpela 'rectangle'.
'Area' bilong Turkey, wantaim ol raunwara, i karamapim 783,562 'square kilometres' (300,948 sq mi), insait long dispela 755,688 'square kilometres' (291,773 sq mi) i stap long 'south west' Asia na 23,764 'square kilometres' (9,174 sq mi) i stap long Europe.
'Area' bilong Turkey i mekim em i stap olsem namba 37 bikpela kantri, na sais bilong em i olsem sais bilong Metropolitan France na United Kingdom taim tupela i bung wantaim.
Ol solwara i raunim ol tripela sait bilong Turkey: Aegean Sea i stap long wes, Black Sea i stap long not na Mediterranean Sea i stap long saut.
Luxembourg i gat longpela histori, tasol indipendens (independence) bilong em i stat long 1839.
Ol sampelaa hap bilong Belgiun long tude i bin stap olsem hap bilong Luxembourg long bipo, tasol em i kamap ol hap bilong Belgium bihain long Belgian Revolution we i kamap long ol yia insait long 1830.
Luxembourg i save traim long stap olsem wanpela 'neutral' kantri, tasol Germany i bin holimpasim em na kisim em long World War I na World War II.
Long 1957 Luxembourge i kamap olsem wanpela memba we i kamapim dispela oganaisesen we tude yumi save long em olsem European Union.
Drukgyal Dzong em i wanpela 'fortress' bilong bipo we i bagarap na i stap na em i wanpela Buddhist 'monastery' long hap antap bilong Paro District (long Phondey Village).
Ol i tok olsem long 1649, Zhabdrung Ngawang Namgyel i wokim wanpela 'fortress' long makim taim em i winim pait agensim ol soldia bilong Tibetan-Mongol.
Long 1951, wanpela paia i mekim sampela ol 'relic' bilong Drukgyal Dzong tasol i stap, kain olsem piksa bilong Zhabdrung Ngawang Namgyal.
Bihain long dispela paia, ol i lukautim na banisim dispela 'fortress', na em i stap olsem wanpela bilong ol narakain samting insait long Bhutan.
Long '18 century' Cambodia i stap namel long tupela kantri i stap klostu long em we i gat pawa, dispela tupela kantri em Thailand na Vietnam.
Ol lain long Thailand i holimpasim na kisim Cambodia long moa long wanpela taim long '18 century' na long 1772 ol i bagarapim Phnom Phen.
Long ol laspela yia bilong '18th century' ol Vietnam tu i holimpasim na kisim Cambodia.
Etin pesen (percent) bilong ol Venezuela i no gat wok, na planti bilong ol lain i wok em ol wok insait long 'informal economy'.
'Two thirds' bilong ol Venezuela husat i wok em ol i save wok insait long 'services sector', klostu wanpela 'quater' i wok insait long indastri (industry) na wanpela 'fifth' i wok insait long 'agriculture'.
Wanpela impoten indastri (industry) bilong ol Venezuela em i oil, dispela kantri em i wanpela 'net exporter', maski wanpela pesen (percent) tasol i wok insait long oil indastri.

Pasin bilong lainim long kamapim 'interactive media' em i nidim 'conventional' na 'traditional' save bilong mekim wok, na tu ol tul (tool) bilong save long en insait long 'interactive class' em ('storyboarding', 'audio', na 'video editing', 'storytelling' na sampela moa.)
Ol 'interactive design' i nidim yu long skelim bek gen ol tingting bilong yu long 'media production' na lainim long tingting long 'non-linear' we.
'Interactive design' em i nisim ol komponen (component) bilong wanpela projek long konek gut wantaim wanpela narapela, tasol ol i mas i gat mining taim ol i stap ol yet tu.
Ol samting we i no gutpela long ol 'zoom lenses' em i olsem 'focla complexity' na namba bilong 'lens elements' we ol i nidim long kisim wanpela 'range of focal lengths, em i ikpela moa long namba bilong 'prime lenses'.
Dispela em i no kamap olsem wanpela hevi moa bikos ol lain bilong wokim ol 'lens' i kamapim ol stendet we i antap moa insait long prodaksen (production) bilong ol.
Dispela i mekim ol 'zoom lenses' long kamapim ol piksa we i gat gutpela kwaliti we i wankain olsem piksa we ol i kisim wantaim ol 'lens' we i gat 'fixed focal length'.
Narapela samting we i no gutpel long ol 'zoom lenses' em 'maximum aperture' (spit) bilong 'lens' i save daunbilo moa.
Dispela i mekim ol 'zoom lens' we i no ekspesif (expensive) i hat long yusim ol long ol ples we i gat 'low-light' na i no wantaim 'flash'.
Wanpela bilong ol problem we i save kamap taim ol i traim long senisim wanpela vidio i go long DVD fomet (format) em 'overscan'.
Planti ol televisen em ol i wokim bilong mekim ol manmeri i amamas.
Long dispela as, olgeta samting yu save lukim long TV, sait sait bilong en, em ol i katim, long antap, daunbilo, na tupela sait.

Dispela kasol bilong bipo i bin kirapim tingting bilong planti manmeri. Em i bin mekim ol i tingim ol soldia i sindaun long hos na pilai, ol bikpela bung kaikai na ol pasin we ol lain long taim bilong King Authur i save bihainim.
Taim yu sanap namel long ol samting we i bagarap na i stap long taunsen yia i go pinis, yu ken tingim saun na smel bilong ol bikpela pait we i bin kamap long taim bipo. Yu ken pilim olsem yu inap harim lek bilong ol wel animal i ron antap long graun na tingim pret bilong ol lain i stap long kalabus.
Tasol yumi save tingim ol samting we i trutru, o nogat? Bilong wanem na ol i wokim ol kasol (castle), dispela bikpela haus bilong ol king na kwin long i stap long en? Ol i bin disainim ol na bildim ol long wanem kain we?
Em i pasin bilong planti lain long dispela taim, Kirby Muxloe Castle em i wanpela strongpela haus bilong hait na i no wanpela trupela kasol (castle).
Ol bikpela glas windua na ol wol we i no bikpela ol i no inap long stopim ol lain i kam long pait.

Dispela balens bilong pawa em i bin wanpela sistem we ol kantri bilong Europe i bin laikim long mekim olgeta steit (state) bilong Europe i kontinu (continue) long holim yet wanwan pawa bilong ol.
Dispela tingting em i olsem olgeta kantri bilong Europe i mas traim long stopim wanpela kantri long i gat moa pawa long ol narapela, olsem na ol nesinel gavman i save senisim ol lain we ol i ken wok bung wantaim long mekim na dispela balens i mas i stap.

Dispela em i makim wanpela impoten senis, bikos ol kantri bilong Europe i no inap moa long pait bikos long lotu. Olsem na, dispela Thirty Years' War em bai i stap olsem laspela woa we ol i kolim olsem 'religious war'.
Tempel bilong Artemis long Ephesus em ol i bin bagarapim long Julai 21, 356 BCE taim Herostratus. i putim paia long em.
Stori i tok olsem, as tingting bilong em i olsem em i laik kisim biknem. Ol lain bilong Ephesia, ol i belhat nogut tru, ol i tok olsem bai i nogat rekod bilong nem bilong Herostratus.
Bihain Strabo wanpela 'historian' bilong Greece i raitim nem bilong em, na tude yumi save long en. Tempel em ol i bin bagarapim long seim (same) nait we Alexander the Great i bin bon.
Alexander, taim em i king, i tok long baim ol lain long bildim gen dispela tempel, tasol ol i no larim em. Bihain, taim Alexander i dai pinis, ol i bildim gen dispela tempel long 323 BCE.
Yu mas sekim na lukim olsem han bilong yu em i stap isi taim yu pilai ol dispela 'note' stret - na tu traim long no muvim nating pinga bilong yu.
Long dispela we, yu bai no inap mekim yu yet i pilim tait tumas. Tingim olsem i no gat nid long paitim ol ki wantaim bikpela strong long mekim volum (volume) i go antap kain olsem long piano.
Long 'accordion', long kisim moa volum (volume), yu yusim ol 'bellow' wantaim moa presa (pressure) o spit.
'Mysticism' em i wanpela rot bilong stap wantaim 'ultimate reality', 'divinity', 'spiritual truth', o God.
Dispela man o meri we i bilip i laik i gat ekspiriens o save long 'divine realiy'/god o ol god.
Ol lain we i save bihainim wanpela bilip i save bihainim wanpela kain we bilong stap, o mekim ol samting we bai mekim ol dispela ekspiriens i kamap gutpela moa.
'Mysticism' em i narakain long ol narapela kain bilip na pasin bilong lotu bikos em i toktok moa long pasin bilong i gat wampela ekspirens wantaim 'unique state of conciousness', bikpela moa long sait bilong i stap bel isi, i gat gutpela tingting, i stap amamas.
Sikhism em i wanpela lotu bilong India. Em i stat long Punjap rijen long '15th century' taim wanpela bruk i kamap insait long tredisen (tradition) bilong ol Hindu.
Ol Sikh i save lukim bilip bilong ol olsem em i wanpela narapela lotu long Hinduism, maski ol i tokaut olsem em i kam long Hindu na sampela ol tredisen (tradition) bilong em i olsem bilong ol Hindu.
Ol Sikh i save kolim lotu bilong ol olsem Gurmat, long tok ples Punjabi dispela em i min olsem "pasin bilong 'guru'". 'Guru' em i wanpela bikpela samting insait long olgeta ol lotu bilong India, tasol insait long Sikhism 'guru' em impoten long wanem em i kamapim ol nambawan samting insait long bilip bilong ol Sikh.
Guru Nanak (1469–1539) i kamapim dispela lotu long '15 century'. Bihain long em i gat nainpela 'guru' moa i bin kamap.
Tasol, long June 1956, ol protes (protest) we i kamap long Poland i testim ol promis bilong Krushchev, we ol wokmanmeri i protes long kaikaini save sot na ol i katim pwl bilong ol, na dispela i tanim na kamap olsem wanpela protes long Communism.
Mekim i go na, Krushchev i salim ol 'tank' long kamapim oda, em i tok orait long sampela askim bilong ol long sait bilong mani na i wanbel long makim Wladyslaw Gomulka we planti man i laikim long kamap olsem nupela praim minista.
Indus Vally Civilization em i wanpela 'civilization' we i kamap long taim bilong Bronz Age long 'northwest' hap bilong India na i karamapim bikpela hap bilong Pakistan long tude na sampela rijen insait long 'northest' India na 'northeast' Afghanistan.
Dispela 'civilisation' i stap long ol arere bilong Indus River we em i kisim nem bilong em long en.
Maski sampela saveman i ting olsem bikos dispela 'civilization' i stap tu long arere bilong Saravati River we i drai pinis, ol i mas kolim dispela 'civilization' olsem Indus-Sarasvati Civilization, sampela i kolim em olsem Harappan Civilization bihainim Harappa, dispela em i nem bilong namba wan hap we ol i bin eksevetim (excavate) long ol yia insait long 1920.
Roman empire i gat bikpela militeri (miltary) na dispela i mekim save bilong ol long marasin na bodi i kamap bikpela moa.

Ol 'surgeon' i gat save bilong ol kainkain marasin bilong mekim ol man i slip na ol i save long 'morphine' we ol i save kisim long ol 'poppy seed' na ol 'scopolamine' we ol i save kisim long ol 'herbane seed'.
Ol i save gut tru long katim hap lek o hap han bilong ol man long seivim (save) ol bai ol i no ken kisim 'gangrene' na ol i save tu long 'tourniquet' na 'arterial clamps' we i save stopim blut long ron.

Attention Deficit Disorder "em i wanpela 'neurological syndrome' na ol nambawan sain em 'impulsivity', 'distractibility', na 'hyperactivity' o 'excess energy'".
Em i no wanpela 'learning disability', em i wanpela 'learning disorder', em i save "kamap long 3 i go long 5 pesen (percent) bilong olgeta pikinini, ating kain olsem 2 milien pikinini long America".
Ol pikinini we i gat ADD i save painim hat long 'focus' long ol samting olsem skul wok, tasol ol i ken konsentret (concerntrate) long ol samting we ol i save amamas long mekim kain olsem pilai ol geim (game) o lukim katun (cartoon) we ol i save laikim o raitim ol sentens we i no gat 'punctuation'.
Ol dispela pikinini i save laik long i stap insait long planti trabel, bikos ol i save "mekim ol 'risky behavior', stap insait long ol pait, salensim atoriti" long kirapim brein (brain) bilong ol, bikos ol nomol samting i no save kirapim brein bilong ol.
ADD i save mekim senis i kamap long ol rilesensip we ol i gat wantaim ol narapela pikinini bikos ol i no inap long klia gut long wanem as na ol i save ekt olsem o bilong wanem na ol i spelim ol wod long dispela kain we o level bilong 'maturity' bilong ol em i narapela.
Taim dispela pasin bilong kisim save na lainim samting em i senis long dispela kain we mipela i tok long en 'base rate' we yumi save kisim save em tu i senis.
Rot bilong kisim infomesen em i narapela kain. Dispela presa (pressure) bilong tingim bek samting em i no stap long wanpela man long tingim bek, tasol em i stap long ol lain husat i inap long tingim wanem samting ol i raitim long pepa.
Bikpela tru, Renaissance i mekim wanpela bikpela senis long pasin bilong lainim samting na givim save.
I no olsem ol narapela 'primates', ol 'hominid' i no yusim han bilong ol long muv o karim hevi o swing namel long ol diwai.

Sampela manmeri i bilip olsem taim yu lukim planti driman we i no tru long planti taim dispela i ken mekim yu i pilim tait nogut tru.

Taim i no gat inap REM long wanpela nait, dispela em mak we bodi bilong yu i save slip na bodi bilong yu i no malolo gut na dispela em bai kamap wanpela problem.
Dispela em bai mekim yu i pilim tait tru wankain olsem sapos yu kirap long olgeta twenti o teti minit na lukim TV.

Wanpela 'sport' bilong tude ol i kolim 'fencing' em ol i save pilai long planti level, stat long ol sumatin long univesiti (university) na i go long Olympic kompetisien (competition).
Dispela 'sport' em ol i save pilai tupela tupela, wanpela 'fencer' i save pilai agensim narapela 'fencer'.
Golf em i wanpela geim (game) we tupela pleiya (player) i save yusim ol 'club' long paitim ol bal i go insait long ol hol.
ol i save pilai long etinpela hol long wanpela 'regualr round', we ol plaiya (player) i stat long namba wan hol bilong 'course' na pinis long namba etin hol.
Dispela pleiya (player) husat i yusim liklik namba bilong ol 'strokes', o 'swings' long 'club' bilong em insait long dispela 'course' em i save win.
Dispela geim (game) em ol i save pilai long gras, na ol i gras ww i raunim hol em ol i save katim em i go got moa na ol i save kolim em olsem 'green'.
Ating wanpela bilong ol 'tourism' we planti lain i save long en em pasin bilong raun i go long narapela ples: 'Recreation tourisim'.
Dispela em i taim we ol manmeri i go long wanpela ples wei narakain long ples we ol i stap long en na ol i save lukluk raun na amamas.
Ol nambis, ol 'theme park' na ol 'camp ground' em ol ples we planti ol 'recreation tourist' i save go long en.
Sapos as tingting bilong wanpela man o meri long i go long wanpela ples long save long histori na kalsa orait dispela kain 'tourism' em ol save kolim olsem 'cultural tourism'.

Ol Colonist, taim ol i lukim dispela samting, ol tu i salim tok long sampela moa soldia long kam.
