Sampela kantri 'cross running' long winta (winter), em ol i bungim wantaim 'gymnasium work' bilong antap bilong bodi, dispela em i nambawan rot bilong redi long 'running season'.
Gutpela kaikai tasol i no inap long mekim ol gutpela pefomens (performance) i kamap, tasol em i ken mekim yanpela 'athlete' i stap gut.
Stap long wanpela helti eneji balens, prektisim pasin bilong dring wara, ol save long ol kainkain rot we ol narapela prektis i ken helpim 'athlete' i ken mekim pefomens (performance) bilong ol i kamap gut na mekim ol i amamas long pilai dispela 'sport'.
'Middle distance running' em i wanpela 'sport' we i no yusim planti mani; tasol, i gat ol kainkain rong tingting long ol sampela ikwipmen (equipment) we ol lain i mas i gat long stap insait long dispela 'sport'.
Ol i ken baim ol dispela prodak sapos ol i nidim, tasol planti bai i gat liklik o no gat senis i kamap long pefomens (performance).
Ol 'athlete' i ken pilim olsem ol i laikim wanpela prodak taim em i no givim gutpela samting.
Ol 'atom' em ol wanpela bilong ol nambawan samting we i kamapim olgeta 'matter'.
Em i wanpela narapela kain 'entity', we liklik model bilong Bohr i tok, em i gat wanpela 'central nucleus' we ol 'electron' i save raunim, wankain olsem ol plenet (planet) i save raunim san-lukim Piksa 1.1.
Ol 'nucleus' i gat tupela 'particle'- 'neutrons' na 'protons'.
Ol 'proton' i gat 'positive electric charge' na ol 'neutron' i no gat 'charge'. Ol 'electron' i gat wanpela 'negative electric charge'.
Long sekim dispela man o meri i stap long hevi, pastaim yu mas mekim sevei long ples we hevi i kamap long lukim olsem yu i stap seif.
Yu nid long luksave long posisen bilong man o meri we i stap long hevi taim yu wok long i go long em na luksave tu long ol samting we i no stret.
Sapos yu kisim bagarap taim yu traim long helpim, yu bai mekim ol samting i kamap nogut moa.
Dispela stadi i painimaut olsem 'depression', pret na 'catastrophising' i gat rilesensip namel long pen na 'disability' long ol lain i gat pen long daunbilo long baksait bilong ol.
Insait long ol 'structured PA session' we i wok long kamap long olgeta wik, ol i lukim olsem dispela senis i kamap bikos long 'catastrophizing', na i no long 'depression' na pasin bilong pret.
Ol lain we i stap insait long ol dispela ektiviti i nidim moa sapot long wanem we ol i lukim pain na save long wanem em i 'chronic pain' na wanem em i 'discomfort' tasol we i kamap long nomol muvmen bilong bodi.
'Vision', o inap long lukim ol samting em i kamap bikos long 'visual system sensory organs' o ol ai.
I gat ol planti kainkain konstraksen bilong ol ai, we i bihainim wanwan samting i stap insait long wanpela animal o bihainim wanem samting dispela animal i nidim.
Ol dispela kainkain konstraksen (construction) i gat kainkain samting ol i ken mekim, sampela em ol i ken save long ol kainkain 'wave-length' na ol i gat ol kainkain level bilong strong bilong ol, na tu ol i nidim ol kainkain proses (process) long mekim mining long ol samting i kam insait long ai na ol i nidim ol kainkain namba bilong samting long wok gut.
Wanpela populesen (population) em wanpela grup bilong wanpela 'specie' we i stap insait long wanpela eria.
Taim olgeta wanwan insait long wanpela populesen (population) i gat wankain 'phenotypic trait' ol i save kolim ol olsem 'monomorphic'.
Taim wanwan bilong ol i soim sampela 'variant' bilong wanpela 'trait' ol i save kolim olsem 'polymorphic'.
Ol 'army colony' bilong ol anis tu i save mas na mekim haus long ol kainkain 'phase'.
Insait long 'nomadic phase', ol 'army' anis i save mas long nait na stop long kem long de.
'Colony' i save statim wanpela 'nomadic phase' taim kaikai i go daun. Long dispela 'phase', 'colony' i save mekim ol haus bilong sotpela taim we ol i save senisim long olgeta de.
Wanwan bilong ol dispela pasin bilong raun o mas long wanpela ples i go long narapela em i save stap inap long kain olsem 17-pela de.
Wanem samting i stap insait long wanpela 'cell'? Dispela wod 'cell' em i kam long Latin wod "'cella'", mining bilong en em "liklik rum", na man we i kamapim dispela wod em i wanpela 'microscopist' we i wok long stadim straksa (structure) bilong 'cork'.
'Cell' em i wanpela liklik samting we i karim laip na i stap insait long olgeta samting i gat laip, na olgeta samting i gat laip em ol i gat wanpela o moa long wanpela 'cell'.
Ol 'cell' em ol nambawan samting tru na ol i impoten long stadi bilong laip, em i tru olsem, planti taim ol lain i save kolim ol olsem "ol samting we i bildim laip".
Nervous System i save mentenim 'homeostasis' taim em i salim ol 'nerve impulses' i go long olgeta hap bilong bodi na mekim blut i ron na tu, em i mekim blut i go gut long olgeta hap bilong bodi.
Ol dispela 'nerve impulses' em ol i save go aut hariap tru long olgeta hap bilong bodi we i save helpim long mekim bodi i stap seif long ol samting we i ken bagarapim em.
Ol 'tornado' i save kamap long wanpela liklik eria taim yu skelim ol wantaim ol narapela strongpela win na ren, tasol em i save bagarapim tru olgeta samting we i stap long rot bilong em.
Ol 'tornado' i save kamautim ol diwai, rausim ruf bilong ol bilding, na apim na tromoi ol kar i go antap long skai. Ol 'tornado' nogut we i kamapim tupela pesen (percent) bilong olgeta 'tornado' em ol save stap moa long tripela aua.
Ol dispela 'monster storm' i gat win we i spit i go long mak bilong 480 km/h (133 m/s; 300 mph).
Ol manmeri i bin mekim na yusim ol 'lenses' long mekim ol samting i kamap bikpela long planti tausen yia.
Tasol, ol trupela 'telescope' ol i bin wok long Europe long klostu pinis bilong '16th century'.
Ol dispela 'telescope' we ol i yusim em ol i gat tuplela 'lens' we ol i bungim wantaim long mekim ol samting i luk olsem ol i stap klostu na ol i bikpela.
Pasin bilong gridi na tingim yumi yet em bai i stap wantaim mipela olgeta taim na wanpela samting long pasin bilong wok bung em i olsem, olgeta manmeri i ken kisim gutpela samting tasol wanpela i ken kisim moa samting long sotpela taim sapos em i tingim em yet.
Em bai i gutpela moa, planti manmeri bai luksave olsem em i gutpela long longpela taim bihain sapos ol i wok bung wantaim ol narapela.
Planti manmeri i driman i long dispela de we ol manmeri i ken i go long narapela sta na lukim ol narapela wol, sampela manmeri i tingting long wanem samting i stap longwe na sampela i bilip olsem ol 'alien' o ol narapela samting i gat laik i stap long ol narapela plenet (planet).
Tasol, sapos dispela bai kamp em bai no inap long kamap i go inap longpela taim bihain. Ol sta i stap long olgeta hap na i gat trilien (trillion) 'mile' i stap namel long ol sta we i stap "klostu klostu".
Ating long wanpela de, ol tumbuna pikinini bilong yu long sanap antap long wol bilong ol 'alien' na tingting bek long ol tumbuna papamama bilong ol?
Ol planti 'cell' i kamapim ol animal. Ol i save kaikai samting na kaikai i save stap insait long bel bilong ol. Klostu olgeta bilong ol animal i ken muv.
Ol animal tasol i gat ol brein (tasol i no olgeta animal i gat brein; eksampel, em ol jelifis (jellyfish), ol i no gat brein).
Ol animal i stap long olgeta hap bilong graun. Ol i dik i go insait long graun, ol i swim long solwara, ol i flai long skai.
Wanpela 'cell' em i wanpela liklik samting we i gat straka na i save mekim wok insait long wanpela samting ol insait long ol samting i gat laip.
Dispela hap tok 'cell' em i kam long tok ples Latin 'cella' we i min olsem wanpela liklik rum.
Sapos yu lukluk long ol samting i stap aninit long wanpela 'microscope', yu bai lukim olsem ol i gat planti ol samting we i luk olsem ol liklik bal o liklik 'square'.
Robert Hooke, wanpela baiolojist (biologist) bilong England, i lukim ol dispela liklik 'square' insait long wanpela 'cork' wantaim wanpela 'microscope'.
Ol i luk olsem ol rum. Em i namba wan man long lukim ol 'cell' we i dai pinis.
Ol elemen (element) na kompaun (compound) i ken senis long wanpela steit (state) i go long narapela na i stap wankain elemen o kompaun yet.
Nitrogen olsem wanpela ges (gas) em i gat ol wankain propeti (properties) olsem wanpela 'nitrogen' taim em i stap olsem wara. Dispela 'liquid state' em i paspas moa tasol ol 'molecule' i wankain yet.
Wara em i narapela eksampel. Dispela kompaun (compound) i gat tupela 'hydrogen atom' na wanpela 'oxygen atom'.
Em i gat wankain 'molecular structure' maski em i wanpela win, wara, o stronpela samting.
Maski 'physical state' bilong em i ken senis, 'chemical state' i stap wankain yet.
Taim em i samting we i stap long olgeta hap na i raunim mipela, na em i save stap insait long olgeta samting yumi mekim, tasol i hat yet long klia gut long em.
Ol lain bilong lotu, ol saveman bilong skelim ol tingting na pasin, na ol saveman bilong sains (science) i bin stadim taim long planti tausen yia.
Yumi save ol taim i kamap taim ol samting i laik kamap i kamap na i go pinis.
Na tu, taim em i wanem we yumi skelim longpela ('length') bilong ol samting we i kamap.
Yu yet i ken soim olsem taim em i kam i go taim yu lukluk long ol 'cyclic event' we i save kamap olgeta taim. Wanpela 'cyclic event' em i wanpela samting we i save kamap olgeta taim long olgeta taim.
Tude ol i save yusim ol komputa long senisim ol piksa na vidio.
Sampela ol katun we i narakain em ol i ken wokim ol long ol konputa, na dispela kain katun em ol i wok long yusim moa yet insait long ol televisen (television) na muvi.
Planti taim ol i save yusim ol narapela kain komputa long rekodim musik bai em i ken proesesim (process) na miksim ol saun wantaim.
Longpela taim namel long 'nineteenth' na 'twentieth century', ol i bin bilong olsem ol namba wan lain we i stap long New Zealand em ol Maori lain, husat i save kaikai ol bikpela pisim ol i kolim 'moas'.
Ol i kamapim tingting olsem ol Maori lain i stap long Polynesia insait long wanpela Great Fleet we i kisim ol i go long New Zealand na ol i kisim dispela ples long ol Moriori, na kamapim wanpela sosaieti we i save wokim gaden.
Tasol, nupela evidens (evidence) i tok olsem ol Moriori em ol i wanpela grup bilong ol Maori husat i stap long New Zealand na i go long Chatham Islands, na kamapim nupela kalsa bilong ol yet, na em i wanpela kalsa bilong stap isi na stap gut.
I bin i gat wanpela narapela lain i stap long Chatham islands na dispela ol lain em ol Maori husat i lusim New Zealand na i go long hap.
Ol i kolim ol yet olsem ol Moriori na i bin gat sampela pait i kamap i go na bihain, olgeta Moriori i dai.
Ol wanwan manmeri husat i bin mekim dispela wok long sampela ten yia i bin helpim yumi long luksave long ol samting we yumi i inap long mekim na ol samting yumi i save laikim taim ol i skelim ol samting we i bin hat na ol samting we yumi i no mekim.
Taim yumi putim yau na harim ol wanwan manmeri i toktok long stori bilong ol yet, bilong famili na bilong oganaisesen, yumi kisim planti gutpela tingting long wanem samting i bin kamap long bipo na sampela bilong ol impoten lain husat i bin mekim gutpela samting o samting nogut i kamap insait long kalsa bilong oganaisesen.
Taim yumi klia gut long histori bilong wanpela dispela em i no min olsem yumi klia gut long kalsa, em i helpim ol manmeri long save wanem hap ol i stap long en insait long histori bilong oganaisesen.
Taim yumi skelim ol samting yumi bin mekim gut na luksave long ol samting we yumi i no mekim gut, ol wanwan manmeri na olgeta lain we i stap insait long dispela bung i painimaut long ol velu (value), ol misen (mission), na ol samting we i save mekim oganaisesen i wok gut.
Long dispela taim, ol i tingim bek ol taim we ol i bin mekim ol 'entrepreneurial behavior' na ol gutpela samting we i kamap i helpim ol manmeri long mekim ol nupela senis na ol nupela senis bilong lokel sios.
Ol dispela kain 'success story' i daunim ol pret we ol lain i gat long mekim senis, na i kamapim ol gutpela tingting long senis long kamap long bihaintaim.
'Convergent thinking' em i wanpela teknik bilong painim ansa bilong wanpela problem na em i save bungim ol kainkain tingting o ol kainkain save long painim ansa bilong wanpela problem.
As bilong dispela kain tingting em pasin bilong mekim samting hariap, skelim samting gut na mekim samting stret, na pasin bilong luksave long ol trupela samting, yusim gen ol teknik we i stap pinis na kisim infomesen.
Impoten samting tru long dispela kain tingting em i olsem: i gat wanpela stretpela ansa tasol. Yu ken tingim tupela ansa, tasol wanpela em i stret na narapela em i rong.
Dispela kain tingting em i bilong wok wantaim sampela kain sains o stendet prosidia (standard procedure).
Ol manmeri wantaim dispela kain tingting em ol i gat 'logical thinking', na ol i inap long putim ol peten insait long tingting, painim ansa long ol problem na wok long ol test bilong sains.
Ol manmeri em ol i nambawan 'specie' tru we i gat pasin bilong ritim tingting bilong ol narapela.
Dispela em i min olsem yumi i inap long save wanem samting ol narapela manmeri i lukim, i laik mekim, i bilip long en, i save long en o i laik long i gat.
Namel long ol dispela pasin, pasin bilong save long tingting bilong narapela em i impoten. Em i helpim mipela long stretim ol samting we i no klia insait long ol eksen bilong mipela.
Eksampel, sapos yu lukim wanpela i wok long brukim windua bilong kar, yu bai ting olsem em i wok long traim long stil long kar bilong wanpela narapela man.
Yu bai skelim em long narapela kain we sapos em i bin lusim ki bilong kar na dispela em i kar bilong em yet we em i wok long traim na brukim.
MRI em i wanpela samting long sait bilong 'physics' we ol i kolim 'nuclear magnetic resonance' (NMR), we Felix Bloch na Edward Purcell i bin painimaut long 1930s taim (Felix i wok long Stanford University) na (Edward i wok long Havard University).
Insait long 'resonance', dispela 'magnetic field' na ol 'radio waves' i mekim ol 'atom' i givim ol liklik redio siknel (signal).
Long yia 1970, Raymond Damadian, wanpela 'medical doctor' na 'research scientist', i painimaut wanem we bilong yusim 'magnetic resonance imaging' olsem wanpela tul (tool) bilong painimaut sik.
Foapela yia bihain ol i kisim wanpela laisens (licence), na dispela em i namba wan laisen long olgeta hap bilong graun long eria bilong MRI.
Long 1977, Dr. Damadian i pinisim konstraksen (construction) bilong namba wan MRI scanner bilong “olgeta hap bilong bodi”, na em i kolim em ”Indomitable”.
'Asynchronous communication' i save sapotim pasin bilong givim taim long tingting long ol samting na putim ya na toktok long ol narapela.
Em i mekim ol sumating i gat taim long wok long spit na mak bilong ol yet na kontrolim mak we ol i kisim tok skul.
Na tu, i no gat planti mak i stap long taim bilong mekim wok na i mekim isi long wok long taim bilong yu yet. (Bremer, 1998).
Pasin bilong yusim Internet an World Wide Web i mekim ol lain i save lainim samting long kisim infomesen we ol i nidim long olgeta taim.
Ol sumatin i ken salim ol kwesten i go long tisa long kainkain taim bilong de na ol i ken kisim bekim hariap, na ol i no inap long wet inap ol i lukim tisa 'face-to-face'.
'Postmodern' rot bilong lainim samting em i save givim fridom long bihainim wanpela rot tasol. I no gat wanpela gutpela wanpela we bilong lainim samting.
Em i tru olsem, i no gat wanpela gutpela samting long lainim. Pasin bilong lainim samting em i save kamap namel long sumatin na samting ol i givim em long lainim.
Wanem samting yumi save lukim nau long sait bilong 'do-it-yourself' na givim infomesen, na lainim samting long ol 'television show' i soim dispela poin we mipela i toktok long en.
Olsem planti bilong yumi i save lukluk long televisen progrem we i tokim mipela long wanpela samting we mipela bai i no inap long stap insait long en o mipela i no inap long yusim dispela save we mipela i kisim.
Mipela bai i no inap long pulim wanpela kar, wokim wanpela 'fountain' long baksait long haus bilong mipela, go long Peru long lukim ol samting bilong bipo, long mekim nupela stail i kamap long haus bilong mipela.
Tenkyu long ol 'undersea fibre optic cable' we i konektim Europe na 'broadband satellite', Greenland em i konek (connect) gut na 93% bilong populeseen (population) bilong em i ken kisim intanet.
Hotel bilong yu o ol lain i lukautim yu (isapos yu stap insait long wanpela 'guesthouse'o 'private home') yu ken i gat 'wifi' o komputa we i konek long intanet, na olgeta setelmen (settlement) i gat wanpela 'internet cafe' o sampela lokesen we i gat pablik 'wifi'.
Olsem mipela i bin tok pinis long antap, maski dispela wod "Eskimo" em planti lain i save yusim long United States, ol asples manmeri long Artic, na planti moa long Canada i no save laikim dispela tok long wanem em i min olsem ol narapela i no laikim ol.
Maski yu ken harim ol Greenland Natives i yusim dispela tok, ol lain long narapela kantri i mas no ken yusim dispela hap tok.
Ol asples manmeri bilong Greenland i save kolim ol yet olsem ol Inuit long Canada na ol Kalaalleq (moa long wanpela em Kalaallit), na Greenlander, long kantri Greenland.
Sampela bikhet pasin, na sampela pasin nogut long lain i kam long narapela ples, dispela em i no save kamap long Greenland. Maski long ol taun, i no gat ol "ples nogut."
Kolpela weda (weather) ating em tasol em i wanpela trupela birua we ol lain i no redi long en bai i bungim.
Sapos yu go raun na lukim Greenland long taim bilong kol em i impoten olsem yu mas kisim kol klos, (tingim taim yu go moa long hap not, ples bai i kol moa).
Dispela ol lonpela de tru long sama (summer) i ken mekim ol lain i no slip gut na i kamap ol hevi long sait bilong helt.
Long taim bilong sama (summer), yu mas lukaut tu long ol Nordic moskito (mosquito). Maski ol i no save givim sik, ol i ken mekim skin i skrap.
Maski ekonomi (economy) bilong San Francisco em i konek (connect) wantaim 'world-cla tourist attraction', em i save mekim mani long kainkain rot.
Nambawan eria we i save kisim ol manmeri long wok em ol kampani we i save givim profesenol sevis, gavman, fainens, treid (trade), na ol kampani we i save givim sevis long ol turis.
Olgeta taim ol i save soim em insait long musik, muvi, stori, na kalsa bilong tude na dispela i mekim planti manmeri long olgeta hap bilong graun i save long dispela siti.
San Francisco i kamapim wanpela a bikpela namba bilong ol samting we i save sevis long ol turis we i gat planti hotel, 'restaurant', na ol fesiliti (facility) we i gat bihainim ol nambawan stendet.
Na tu, Fransisco em i wanpela bilong ol nambawan ples insait long kantri long painim kaikai bilong Asia: ol i gat Korean, Thai, Indian, and Japanese.
Pasin bilong raun i go long Walt Disney World em i wanpela bikpela raun we planti famili long America i save mekim.
Ol samting "i save kamap olgeta taim" em bai yu flai i go long Orlando International Airport, kalap long bas (bus) i go long wanpela Disney hotel we i stap long dispela hap, stap long wanpela wik na i go autsait long propeti bilong Disney, na go bek long haus.
I gat kainkain senis i ken kamap, tasol dispela em i ol samting we planti manmeri i save mekim taim ol tok olsem ol "i go long Disney World".
Planti tiket we ol i save salim long intanet long ol websait kain olsem eBay o Craigslist em ol i ken yusim long lukim moa long wanpela park long moa long wanpela de.
Maski planti lain i save mekim dispela samting, Disney i tok tambu long dispela: ol dispela tiket em i bilong wanpela man na ol i no ken salim long narapela man.
Long mekim sampela kain liklik 'camping' long Grand Canyon, yu mas kisim wanpela tok orait long go long ol liklik ples longwe long siti.
Ol i putim mak long namba bilong tok orait bikos ol i laik lukautim 'canyon', na em bai i op long namba 1 de bilong mun long ol lain i ken makim spes bilong ol long i go, foapela mun bipo long mun we 'canyon' bai i op.
Olsem na, tok orait bilong i go long ol liklik ples we i stap longwe long siti long mun Mei bai i redi long de namba 1 bilong mun Jenueri.
Spes bilong i stap long ol ples we planti manmeri i save laikim, i save pulap hariap long namba wan de ol i open long ol manmeri long makim spes, dispela em ol kain ples olsem Bright Angel Campground we i stap sait long Phantom Ranch.
I gat mak bilong namba bilong tok orait we ol i ken givim long ol lain we i wokabaut i go insait long ofis bilong ol na mekim rikwes, na ol bai givim spes long husat ol lain i kam pas.
Go long Southern Africa long kar em i wanpela we bilong lukim olgeta naispela samting bilong dispela rijen na tu long kisim ol narapela rot na go long ol ples we ol turis i save go long em.
Dispela em i yu ken mekim wantaim wanpela nomol kar taim yu mekim gut plen, tasol i gutpela moa long yuim 4x4 kar na planti ol hap em yu ken go long en wantaim wanpela 'high wheel base' 4x4.
Taim yu mekim plen yu mas tingim olsem maski Southern Africa i stap gut ol narapela kantri i stap klostu long en em ol i no stap gut.
Kost na nid bilong i gat wanpela visa em i save senis long wanpela kantri i go long narapela na dispela em bai bihainim wanem kantri yu kam long en.
Wanwan kantru tu i gat ol narakain lo bilong em yet long wanem ol samting bilong imejensi (emergency) yu ken karim insait long kar.
Victoria Falls em i wanpela taun long hap wes bilong Zimbabwe, kalapim boda long Livinstone Zambia, na klostu long Botswana.
Dispela taun em i stap arere tasol long 'falls', na ol i save pulim planti turis, tasol dispela ples em i gutpela long ol lain i painim 'adventure' na ol lain i laik lukim ol samting long i stap longpela taim.
Long taim bilong ren (Novemba i go long Mas), vmak bilong wara bai i go antap na Falls bai i luk bikpela moa.
Yu bai wet sapos yu wokabaut long bris o wokabaut long ol liklik rot we i stap klostu long Falls.
Tasol narapela sait, em i bikos mak bilong wara em i bikpela tru olsem na yu bai no inap long lukim Falls—bikos sais bilong wara i blokim ples bilong lukluk!
Tomb of Tutankhamun (KV62). KV62 em i wanpela 'tomb' bilong Valley we planti lain tru i save long en, em i wanklain olsem piksa bilong Howard Carter taim em i painim dispela 'tomb' bilong yangpela king i stap gut tru long 1922.
Taim yu skelim wantaim ol narapela 'tomb' bilong king na kwin, dispela 'tomb' bilong Tutankhamun em planti lain bai i no gat tingting long go lukim bikos sais bilong em i liklik na em i no gat planti bilas.
Wanpela man o meri we i gat intres long lukim evidens (evidence) bilong bagarap long 'mummy' long taim ol i laik traim long rausim em long kofin bai i no inap amamas biks het na solda (shoulder) i stap ples klia.
Ol naispela kago we i stap long ol 'tomb' i no stap moa. tasol ol i putim ol long Egyptian Museum long Cairo.
Ol visita (visiter) we i no gat inap taim bilong raun i ken spendim taim bilong ol long sampela narapela hap.
Phnom Krom, em i stap 12 km 'southwest' long Siem Reap. Tempel i stap antap long liklik maunten em ol i bin wokim long pinis bilong '9th century', long taim King Yasovarman i stap olsem king.
Dispela ples we i no gat lait insait long tempel na naispela hap bilong lukluk antap long raunwara Tonle Sap i mekim dispela wok we yu mekim long klaimim maunten em i no lus nating.
Wanpela raun i go long dispela hap em yu ken bungim i go wantaim wanpela raun long bot i go long raunwara.
Angkor Pass em yu bai nidim long i go insait long tempel olsem na no ken lus tingtin long bringim paspot (passport) i go wantaim yu taim yu golong Tonle Sap.
Jerusalem em i kapitol na bikpela siti tru bilong Israel, maski planti narapela kantri na United Nations i no luksave long Israel olsem kapitol bilong em.
Dispela siti bilong bipo i stap long Judean Hills me i gat wanpela narapela kain histori (history) bilong em yet we i go bak long planti tausen yia.
Dispela siti em i holi long tripela lotu we i save bilip long wanpela God - Judaism, Christianity na Islam, na em i save stp olsem senta bilong lotu, bilip, na kalsa.
Bikos long impoten mining bilong dispela siti long sait bilong lotu, na ol hap we i stap long eria bilong Old City, Jerusalem em i wanpela hap we i save pulim planti turis.
Jerusalem i gat planti ples bilong histori, kalsa na akeoloji (archeology), wantaim planti hap bilong baim samting, baim kaikai, na 'restaurant'.
Lo bilong Ecuador i tok olsem ol sitisen bilong Cuba i mas kisim wanpela pas we i askim ol long go long Ecuador bipo long ol i ken yusim ol intanesinel eapot o ol 'frontier admission points' long kam long em.
Dispela leta em Ecuadorian Ministry of Foreign Affairs i mas tok orait long em, na em i mas bihainim sampela samting.
Ol dispela samting we ol i mas mekim em i bilong mekim wanpela gutpela balens i kamap long namba bilong ol manmeri i go i kam long dispela tupela kantri.
Ol sitisen bilong Cuba husat i holim 'US green card' em ol i mas go long wanpela Ecuadorian Consulate long kisim wanpela pepa i tok olsem ol i no gat nid long i gat wanpela pas i askim ol long i go.
Paspot (passport) bilong yu em i mas 'valid' long 6-pela mun o moa long de we yu bai travel. Yu bai nidim wanpela 'round/onward' tiket long soim hamas taim yu bai stap long hap.
Ol 'tour' i go long dispela hap em i no bikpela mani long ol bikpela grup, olsem na sapos yu go yu yet o wantaim wanpela pren, traim long bungim ol narapela manmeri na kamapim wanpela grup we o gat foapela o sikspela lain long kisim wanpela gutpela reit (rate).
Tasol, dispela em wanpela samting we yu no ken wari long en, bikos ol turis em ol i save bungim ol wantaim long pulapim ol kar.
Em i luk olsem wanpela rot bilong trikim ol manmeri long bilip olsem ol i mas baim moa mani.
Sanap longpela moa long hap not bilong Machu Picchu em wanpela longpela maunten, planti taim em i save stap baksait long ol foto bilong ol bilding bilong bipo.
Em i luk olsem wanpela hat long klaimim taim yu stap daunbilo, na em i sap na i hat long go antap, tasol wanpela man o meri we i strong i ken i go antap long kain taim olsem 45 minit.
Ol i putim ol ston step long rot bilong wokabaut, na long ol hap we i sap moa i gat ol 'steel cable' bilong givim sapot bilong holim han.
Yumi tok olsem pinis, tasol yu mas save olsem yu bai sotwin, lukaut gut long ol ples we i sap, lukaut moa yet long taim ples i wet, em i ken kamapim birua hariap.
I gat wanpela hul bilong ston i stap klostu long antap we yu mas go insait long en, em i sotpela na i gat liklik spes bilong 'squeeze' na i go insait.
Long lukim ol ples na animal bilong Galapago em i gutpela moa long rong long bot, wankain olsem Charles Darwin i bin mekim long 1835.
Moa long 60-pela 'cruise ship' i save go long ol wara bilongt Galapagos ‑ stat long sais bilong 8-pela pasindia i go long sais bilong 100-pela pasindia.
Planti manmeri i save makim ples bilong ol bipo yet (bikos ol bot i save pulap long taim we planti manmeri i save laikim).
Yu mas sekim gut olsem dispela 'agent' we yu tokim em long makim spes em i wanpela man o meri we i gat planti save long Galapagos na ol kainkain sip.
Dispela em bai mekim na ol intres bilong yu o ol sampela samting we yu no inap long em ol i makim gut wanpela sip long inapim ol dispela nid.
Bipo long ol lain Spain i kam kamap long '16th century', ol Inca i bin bosim 'nothern' Chile taim ol aspela lain Araucanians (Mapuche) i stap long 'central' na 'southern' Chile.
Ol Mapuche em ol laspela tumbuna bilong ol asples lain bilong America, we i no kamap olsem pat bilong ol lain i kam aninit long Spain na i save tok ples Spanish i go inap bihain long Chile i kisim indipendens (independence).
Maski ol Chile i tokaut olsem ol indipenden long 1810 (namel long Napoleonis woa i mekim ol Spain i no gat wanpela gavman long sampela yia), ol i no winim Spain i go inap 1818.
Dominican Republic (Tok Ples bilong Spain: República Dominicana) em i wanpela kantri bilong Caribbean we i stap insait long hap ist bilong ailan Hispaniola, na i serim dispela ailan wantaim kantri Haiti
Dispela kantri i gat ol nambis we i gat waitpela wesan na ol maunten, na tu em i gat olpela siti tru long Americas i stap long en. Nau, dispela siti i stap insait long Santo Domingo.
Dispela ailan em ol Tainos na Caribes em ol namba wan lain husat i bin i kam na sindaun long em. Ol Caribes em ol lain we i save tok ples Arawaken na ol i bin kam long yia 10,000 BCE.
Bihain long sampela yia long taim we ol eksplora (explorer) bilong Europe i kam, ol lain bilong Spain i bin daunim namba bilong ol manmeri long Tainos i go daun olgeta.
Fray Bartolomé de la Casas (Tratado de las Indias) i bin tok olsem namel long 1942 na 1498 ol lain bilong Spain we i kam na bosim dispela hap i bin kilim 100,000 Taínos manmeri.
Jardín de la Unión. Dispela spes we ol i bin bildim olsem wanpela ples bilong bung bilong wanpela konven (convent) bilong '17th century', em Templo de San Diego i wanpela bilding tasol we i sanap yet.
Nau em i stap olsem wanpela bikpela 'plaza', na olgeta taim i save i gat planti samting i kamap long hap, long de na nait.
I gat sampela 'restaurant' i raunim dispela gaden, na long ol avinun na nait i save i gat ol fri konset (concert) we ol i save givim long wanpela liklik haus we i stap namel long dispela ples.
Callejon del Beso (Alley of the Kiss). Tupela 'balcony' we i gat 69 'centimeter' spes i stap namel long tupela em i ples bilong wanpela 'love legend'.
Sapos yu givim sampela 'penny' sampela pikinin bai tokim yu dispela stori.
Bowen Island em i wanpela ailan we planti lain i save long en long kisim wanpela raun long de o wanpela wiken raun na ol i save givim 'kayaking', 'hiking', ol stua, 'restaurant', na moa.
Dispela trupela komuniti we i stap long Howe Sound autsait tasol long Vancouver, na em i isi long go long en long wanpela 'water taxi' we i save lusim Granville Island ilong 'downtown' Vancouver.
Long ol lain husat i save amamas long raun raun, wanpela wokabaut i go antap long ples bilong Sea to Sky em bai inapim laik bilong yu.
Whistler (1.5 aua draiv lusim Vancouver) em i ekspensif (expensive), tasol planti lain i save long en bikos long 2010 Winter Olympics.
Long taim bilong winta (winter), amamas wantaim sampela nambawan ples bilong ski long North America, na long sama (summer) traim sampela trupela 'mountain biking'.
Yu mas kisim tok orait bipo long yu go long hap. Yu mas i gat tok orait long stap long nait long Sirena.
Sierna em i wanpela 'ranger station' we i save givim ples bilong slip na kaikai wantaim 'camping'. La Loena, San Pedrillo, na Los Patos i save givim 'camping' tasol na i o gat sevis bilong givim kaikai.
Em i isi long kisim ol tok orait bilong go long park long Ranger Station long Puerto Jiménez, tasol ol i no save yusim ol 'credit card'.
Park Service (MINAE) i no save givim ol tok orait bilong go long park wanpela mun bipo long taim we yu bai go long park.
CafeNet El Sol i save givim wanpela 'reservation service' long wanpela prais bilong US$30, o $10 long ol 'one-day pass'; ol tok save i stap long Corcovado pes bilong ol.
Ol Cook Islands em ol wanpela ailan kantri long we i save wok bung wantaim New Zealand, na em i stap long Polynesa, long namel bilong South Pacific Ocean.
Em i wanpela grup ailan wantaim 15-pela ailan we i slip antap long 2.2 milien km2 bilong solwara.
Wantaim wankain 'time zone' olsem Hawaii, ol dispela ailan em sampela taim ol i save kolim ol olsem "'Hawaii down under'".
Maski em i liklik, em i mekim sampela ol lain we i bin go lukim Hawaii bipo long em i kamap olsem wanpela steit (state) na i no gat ol bikpela hotel bilong turis na ol narapela divelopmen.
Cooks Island i no gat wanpela siti, tasol em i gat 15-pela kainkain ailan. Ol bikpela ailan em Rarotonga na Aitutaki.
Long ol divelop kantri tude, pasin bilong givim wanpela 'deluxe bed' na brekfas em ol i mekim i go kamap olsem wanpela kain 'art-form'.
Long ol lain we i save givim nambawan sevis, B&Bs i save resis long tupela bikpela samting: 'bedding' na brekfas (breakfast).
Olsem na, long ol nambawan institusen wanpela bai painim ol naispela 'bedding' tru, ating wanpela 'quilt' we ol wokim long han o wanpela 'antique' bed.
Brekfas (breakfast) em bai gat ol naispela kaikai bilong dispela sisen (season) o spesol kaikai bilong dispela hotel.
Ples bilong sindaun em ol bai bilasim olsem wanpela bilding bilng bipo wantaim ol 'antique' bilas, gras ol i katim gut na wanpela 'swimming pool'.
Kisim kar bilong yu na go long wanpela longpela 'road trip' em i isi long mekim na em bai mekim yu pilim nais.
I no kain olsem ol bikpela kar, yu bai save pinis long dravim kar bilong yu na yu save long wanem samting em i no inap long mekim.
Sanapim wanpela haus sek long banis bilong sampela lain o insait long wanpela taun i ken mekim ol manmeri kam lukluk o toktok long yu.
Long mekim sotpela tok, yusim kar bilong yu yet wanpela gutpela rot bilong go graun long rot, tasol em i no wanpela gutpela we bilong mekim "'camp'".
'Car camping' em i isi long mekim sapos yu gat wanpela bikpela 'minivan', SUV, Sedan o Station Wagon we i gat sit bilong putim go daun.
Sampela hotel i gat wanpela 'heritage' i kam long taim bilong ol 'steam railways' na 'ocean liners'; bipo long Second World War, long '19th' o stat bilong '20th century'.
Ol dispela hotel em ol ples we ol maniman na bikman bilong dispela taim i save stap long en, na planti taim ol save gat naispela kaikai na gutpela ektiviti bilong mekim long nait.
Dispela ol bilas bilong bipo, na ol i no yusim ol samting bilong tude, na kain olpela na naispela kondisen bilong ol samting bilong bipo em i pat bilong stail bilong ol.
Maski ol i privet propeti bilong sampela lain, ol i ken kisim ol bikman bilong kantri na ol narapela impoten manmeri taim ol i kam.
Wanpela travela (traveller) we i gat planti mani i ken tingting long raun long olgeta hap bilong graun, na i stap long planti bilong ol dispela kain hotel.
Wanpela 'hospitality exchange network' em i wanpela oganaisesen we i save konektim ol travela wantaim ol lokel manmeri long siti we ol bai i go na raun long en.
Long joinim wanpela kain 'network' yu bai nid long pulapim wanpela 'online form'; maski sampela 'network' bai laikim sampela moa dokumen bilong soim.
Ol bai givim wanpela list bilong ol 'host'long intanet/bilong printim, sampela wantaim 'reference' na 'review' we ol narapela travela (traveller) i givim.
Couchsurfing i bin stat long Jenueri 2004 bihain long wanpela 'computer programmer' Casey Fenton i pasin balus i go long Iceland long liklik prais, tasol em i no gat ples long i stap.
Em i imeilim ol sumatin long lokel univesiti na kisim bikpela namba bilong ol lain i laik givim em haus long stap.
Ol 'hostel' em i bilong ol yanpela manmeri – wanpela 'guest' bilong en em bai stap long mak bilong ol twentipela krismas – tasol yu ken painim ol olpela travela tu i stap long hap.
Ol famili wantaim ol pikinini i no save stap long 'hostel', tasol sampela 'hostel' i save larim ol i stap long ol praivet rum.
Dispela siti bilong Beijing long China em bai kamap olsem 'host city' bilong Olympic Winter Games long 2022, dispela bai i mekim em i kamap olsem namba wan siti bilong kamap 'host' bilong winta (winter) na sama (summer) Olympics.
Beijing bai hostim (host) 'opening' na 'closing' seremoni na ol 'indoor ice events'.
Ol narapela 'skiing events' bai kamap long Taizicheng ski eria long Zhangjiakou, kain olsem 220 km (140 'miles') long Beijing.
Planti bilong ol dispela tempel i gat wanpela Annual bikde we i stat long Novemba na i pinis long Mid of May, we i save senis senis bihain kalenda bilong wanwan tempel long olgeta yia.
Planti bilong bikde bilong tempel em ol i save amamasim olsem pat bilong 'anniversary' bilong tempel o bon de bilong wanpela god o wanpela bikpela samting bilong dispela tempel.
Ol bikde bilong tempel long Kerala em ol i narakain na yu bai laik long lukim, ol i save wokabaut wantaim ol elefen, ol lain bilong pilai musik long tempel na ol narapela samting bilong amamasim dispela de,
World's Fair (narapela nem we planti lain i save long en em World Exposition, o Expo) em i wanpela intanesinel festivel bilong 'art' na 'science'.
Ol kantri we i stap insait long dispela festivel na i soim ol samting bilong ol long 'art' na 'edukesen long ol bilding bilong ol long soim ol hevi i kamap long wol o kalsa na histori bilong kantri bilong ol.
nternational Horticultural Expositions em ol bung bilong soim flawa, ol 'botanical garden' na ol narapela samting long sait bilong ol plent (plant).
Maski ol i tok olsem em i ken kamap long olgeta yia (sapos ol i no kamap long ol narapela narapela kantri), tru tru ol i no save kamap long narapela narapela kantri.
Ol dispela samting i save stap long kain mak olsem tripela na sikspela mun, na ol save holim ol long ol ples we i liklik moa long 50 'hectare'.
I gat planti kainkain fomet (format) bilong film we ol i bin yusim long ol yia i go pinis. Stendet 35 mm film (36 by 24 negatif) em planti lain tru i save long en.
Ol i ken senisim em isi taim em i pinis, na em i save givim 'resolution' we i klostu wankain olsem 'resolution' bilong DSLR bilong tude.
Sampela 'medium‑format' film kamera i save yusim wanpela '6 by 6 cm' fomet, tru tru em i '56 by 56 mm' negatif.
Dispela i save givim 'resolution' we i kain olsem foapela taim moa long wanpela '35 mm' negatif (3136 mm2 versus 864).
Ol wel animal em ol hatpela samting long ol 'photographer' long kisim, na ol i nidim 'good luck', pasin bilong stap isi na wet, ekspiriens na gutpela ikwipmen (equipment).
'Wildlife photography' em wanpela samting we mipela i no save tingim hatwok i stap baksait long dispela, tasol wankain ol olgeta narapela foto, wanpela piksa em i inap long tausenpela wod.
'Wildlife photography' em i nidim wanpela longpela 'telephoto lens', tasol long ol narapela samting olsem ol grup pisin o wanpela liklik animal em bai i nidim ol narapela 'lens'.
Planti ol narakain animal em i hat long painim ol, na sampela taim sampela park i gat ol lo bilong kisim foto sapos yu bai mekim mani long dispela foto.
Ol wel animal i ken sem o i ken kros. Envairomen i ken kol, hot, o i no isi long stap long en.
Olgeta hap bilong graun i gat moa long 5,000 kainkain tok ples, twentipela bilong ol dispela tok ples i gat 50 milien o moa manmeri i save yusim.
Ol toktok ol i raitim em planti taim em i isi moa long save long en na i no ol toktok we ol i tok long maus. Dispela em i tru long ol adres, we i hat moa long kolim na narapela bai i klia long en.
Planti manmeri insait long wanpela kantri i save gut tru long English, na moa yet em yu ken lukim olsem i gat liklik save bilong dispela tok ples i stap ‑ long ol yangpela manmeri.
Tingim, sapos yu inap, wanpela Mancunian, Bostonian, Jamaican na Sydneysider i sindaun raunim wanpela tebol na kaikai nait kaikai long wanpela 'restaurant' long Toronto.
Ol i wok long stori long wanpela narapela long ol stori bilong ol taun bilong ol, na ol bai toktok long ol nek na hap tok we i bilong taun bilong ol yet.
Baim sampela kaikai long ol maket em i rot we i no i yusim liklik mani tru long kisim kaikai. Sapos i no gat ples bilong kuk, orait ol kaikai we yu ken baim em bai i no inap planti.
Namba bilong kaikai we i redi long kaikai i wok long i go antap long sekseen bilong kaikai we i redi na i stap. Sampela i save i gat 'micowave oven' o sampela narapela rot bilong hotim kaikai.
Insait long sampela kantri o sampela stoa i gat wanpela 'restaurant' i stap, na em i no 'restaurant' tru tru na ol prais bilong em i no antap tumas.
Mekim na karim kopi bilong ol polisi bilong yu na kontek infomesen bilong 'insurer' bilong yu wantaim yu.
Ol bai nid soim imeil adres bilong 'insurer' bilong ol na intanesinel fon namba long kisim tok save/atoraisesen long mekim ol 'claims'.
Yu mas i gat wanpela narapela kopi insait long beg bilong yu na 'online' (salim imeil long yu yet wantaim 'attachment', ol putim long "'cloud'").
Sapos yu raun wantaim wanpela 'laptop' o 'tablet', putim wanpela kopi insait long 'memory' o 'disc' (we yu no inap nidim intanet long kisim).
Na tu, givim kopi bilong polisi/kontek long ol pren we i travel wantaim yu na ol famili o pren long haus we i wanbel long helpim yu.
'Moose' (narapela nem bilong en em 'elk) em ol i no save pait wantaim fos, tasol ol i save banisim ol yet long samting we ol i ting olsem i ken bagarapim ol.
Taim ol manmeri i ting olsem ol 'moose' i no inap long kamapim birua, ol i ken i go klostu tumas na putim ol yet long han bilong birua.
Dringim bia long sampela taim. Bia i save wanwan man o meri i kainkain pasin, na em i impoten olsem yu mas save long mak bilong yu.
Ol samting we i ken kamap bihain bikos long pasin bilong dring bia tumas em 'liver' i bagarap na aipas na dai. Mak bilong birua i kamap long pasin bilong dring em i ken i go antap moa taim yumi dring bia we ol i no mekim long stretpela rot.
Ol 'spirit' we lo i tok tambu long en i gat ol kainakin samting insait long en wanpela em 'methanol', dispela i ken kamapim aipas na dai maski yu dring liklik tasol.
Ol aiglas em ol i liklik mani long wanpela narapela kantri, ol i save liklik mani long ol kantri we i save kisim liklik man na kost bilong wok leba (labour) em i daunbilo.
Tingting long kisim wanpela 'eye exam' long haus, yu mas mekim olsem sapos insuren (insurance) i no karampim em, na bringim 'prescription' i go long hap bilong baim aiglas.
Ol ekspensif 'brand‑name' bilong freim (frame) we i stap long ol dispela eria i ken i gat tupela kain problem; sampela ol i ken kopi tasol na i no prodak tru, na ol dispela we ol i importim (imported) em ol bai moa ekspensif long aiglas we ol i wokim yet long kantri.
Kofi em i wanpela bilong ol samting we ol manmeri bilong graun i save salim na baim, na yu ken painim kainkain bilong em long rijen bilong yu.
Maski long dispela, i gat ol kainkain we bilong dringim kofi long olgeta hap bilong graun we yu ken eksperiensim.
Canyoning (o: 'canyoneering') em i toktok long go long aninit bilong wanpela 'canyon', we i drai o i pulap long wara.
'Canyoning' em i bungim pasin bilong 'swimming', 'climbing' na 'jumping'‑‑tasol em i no nidim treining (training) o bodi we i fit long stat (taim yu skelim em wantaim eksmapel, 'climbing', 'scuba diving' o 'alpine skiing').
'Hiking' em i wanpela ektiviti bilong mekim long autsait we yu bai wokabaut long envairomen, planti taim long ol rot bilong wokabaut.
'Day hiking' em i gat ol mak bilong wokabaut we i aninit long wanpela 'mile' na i go inap long mak bilong wokabaut we wanpela i ken mekim long wanpela de.
Long wanpela 'hike' long wanpela isipela rot em i no gat nid long redi, na wanpela man o meri we i stap helti i ken amamas long wokabaut long en.
Ol famili we i gat ol liklik pikinini i nid long redi gut moa, tasol wanpela de autsait em i isi long mekim wantaim ol bebi na ol 'pre-school' pikinini.
Long intanesinel level, i gat kain olsem 200-pela 'running tour' oganaisesen. Planti bilong ol i save operet long ol yet.
Dispela Go Running Tours, we i kisim ples bilong Global Running Tours i save bungim planti bilong ol 'sightrunning provider' long foapela kontinen (continent).
Em i bin stat long Barcelona's Running Tours Barcelona na Copenhagen's Running Copenhagen, Running Tours Prague we i stap long Prague na ol narapela i hariap long joinim em.
I gat planti samting yu mas tingim pastaim na bihain yu travel i go long sampela hap.
Taim yu travel, yu mas save olsem ol samting i no inap long wankain olsem "ples bilong yu". Ol pasin bilong ol, ol lo, kaikai, rot bilong kar, ples bilong i slip, ol stendet, tok ples na kain olsem bai senis long wanem ples yu stap long en.
Dispela em i samting we yu bai nid long putim insait long het bilong yu, long mekim na yu bai i no inap long amamas o les long pasin bilong ol lokel long mekim samting.
Dispela ol 'travel agency' em ol i bin i stap stat long '19th century'. Wanpela 'travel agent' em i wanpela gutpela rot bilong wanpela raun we i go moa long mak bilong raun long bus, lukim kalsa, tok ples o 'low-income country'.
Maski planti bilong ol 'agency' i wanbel long mekim planti bilong ol 'booking' we planti lain i save mekim, planti 'agent' i save wok long wanpela kain travel, mak bilong mani o ples.
Em i gutpela long yusim wanpela 'agent' husat i save mekim 'booking' long ol wankain raun olsem raun bilong yu.
Lukluk long wanem ol raun ol 'agent' i wok long mekim promosen long en, maski em long wanpela websait o long wanpela windua bilong stoa.
Sapos yu laik long lukim olgeta hap bilong graun long liklik mani, baim wanem samting yu nidim, o salensim yu yet, i gat sampela rot bilong mekim olsem.
Long bikpela rot bilong lukim samting, ol i kam aninit long tupela grup: Yu ken wok taim yu raun o traim na daunim mak bilong mani yu spendim. Dispela hap toktok bai lukluk long pasin bilong daunim mak bilong mani yu spendim.
Long ol lain i sekrifaisim ol gutpela samting, taim na pasin bilong bihain plen na daunim mak bilong mani i go daun klostu long jiro, lukim 'minimum budget travel'.
Dispela tok skul i no min olsem ol travela bai i no inap long stil, go insait long banis we i gat tok tambu long en, salim samting we lo i tok tambu long en, askim long samting, o yusim ol narapela lain long kisim ol samting we ol i laikim.
Wanpela 'immigration checkpoint' em i namba wan stop taim yu kam daun long wanpela balus, sip, ol narapela trenspot (transport).
Long sampela ples bilong krosim boda ol i save mekim ol trein inspeksen long trein we i wok long ron na yu mas i gat wanpela 'valid ID' wantaim yu taim yu kalap long wanpela bilong ol dispela trein.
Long ol 'sleeper train' bilong nait, 'conductor' i ken kolektim paspot (passport) olsem na yu ken slip gut na ol i no inap distebim yu.
'Registration' wanpela samting yu mas mekim insait long wok bilong 'visa'. Insait long sampela kantri, yu mas 'register' olsem yu i stap na adres we yu bai stap long en wantaim ol lokel atoriti.
Long mekim dispela yu bai pulapim wanpela pepa wantaim ol lokel polis o go lukim ol ofis bilong 'immigration'.
Long planti kantri we i gat dispela kain lo, ol lokel hotel bai stretim displela 'registration' long yu (yu mas askim ol).
Long narapela taim, ol lain we i stap autsait long ol ples we ol turis i save stap long en em ol i nid long mekim dispela 'registration'. Tasol, dispela i mekim na lo bai i no inap klia, olsem na yu mas painimaut pastaim.
'Architecture' em i wok bilong disainim na konstraktim ol bilding. 'Architecture' bilong wanpela ples i save kamap olsem samting we i save pulim ol turis i go long em.
Planti bilding em ol i nais tru long lukluk long en na piksa bilong ol taim yu stap antap long wanpela longpela bilding o wanpela gutpela posisen long windua em i ken nais tumas.
'Architecture' i save bungim ol narapela eria bilong wok kain olsem 'urban planning', 'civil engineering', 'decorative arts', 'interior desigen' na 'landscape design'.
Ol taun bilong en i stap longwe tru, yu no inap long painim planti samting i kamap long nait sapos yu no raun i go long Albuquerque o Santa Fe.
Tasol, klostu olgeta bilong ol 'casino' i stap long list i stap antap i save sevim (serve) ol dring, na sampela bilong ol i save bringim ol 'entertainment brand' (ol dispela 'brand' we i stap raunim Albuquerque na Santa Fe).
Lukaut: ol liklik 'bar' bilong taun em ol i no gutpela ples bilong ol lain long autait long i go long en.
Wanpela samting em i olsem, 'northern' New Mexico i gat bikpela problem wantaim pasin bilong dring bia na draiv, na namba bilong ol draiva we i save dring na draiv i save go antap taim yu go klostu long ol 'bar' bilong ol liklik taun.
Ol peinting (painting) we ol lain i no laikim o ol raiting (writing) we i no gutpela em ol i save kolim olsem 'graffiti'.
Maski em i wanpela samting bilong bipo yet, planti manmeri i save ting olsem em i samting we ol yanpela i save mekim taim ol laim bagarap samting bilong pablik na praivet propeti taim ol i yusim 'spray paint'.
Tasol, nau i gat ol 'graffiti artist', 'graffiti events' na "'legal" walls'. Ol 'graffiti painting' bilong ol dispela lain em i save soim ol 'artwork' na i no ol samting we lo i tambu long em.
Pasin bilong tromoi 'boomerang' em i wanpela samting we planti turis i save lainim.
Sapos yu laik lainim long tromoi wanpela 'boomerang' we i kam bek long han bilong yu, yu mas sekim na lukim olsem yu gat wanpela gutpela 'boomerang' we i ken tanim i kam bek.
Planti ol 'boomerang' i stap long Australia em o i no inap long kam bek. Em i gutpela long ol lain i wok long stat long lainim long no ken traim tromoi long taim bilong win
Wanpela Hangi Meal em ol i save kukim insait long wanpela hotpela hol long graun.
Dispela hol em ol i save hotim wantaim hotpela ston bilong wanpela paia, ol long sampela ples we i gat hot i save kam aninit long graun.
Planti taim ol i save yusim 'hangi' long kukim wanpela kaikai bilong avinun long paia.
Sampela ples long Rotorua i save givim 'geothermal hangi', na ol narapela 'hangi' em ol lain i ken traim long Christchurch, Wellington na narapela hap.
MetroRail i gat tupela level long ol trein bilong i go i kam long wok na raun long Cape Town: MetroPlus (em ol i save kolim olsem First Class) na Metro (ol i save kolim Third Class).
MetroPlus em i gutpela moa na i no gat planti manmeri, tasol em i moa ekspensif moa, tasol em i liklik mani moa long ol nomol tiket bilong ol trein i save ron aninit long graun long Europe.
Olgeta train i gat MetroPlus na Metro 'coaches'; MetroPlus 'coaches' em ol i save stap long baksait long trein klostu long Cape Town.
Ol lain i save karim bek bilong ol narapela ‑ No ken lusim ai long bek bilong yu, bikpela moa em taim yu long lusim wanpela intanesinel boda na i go long hapsait.
Yu ken painimaut olsem ol i yusim yu long karim drag (drug) taim yu no save, dispela em bai mekim yu i stap insait long bikpela trabel.
Dispela em yu bai sanap long lain, bikos ol bai i no inap tok save na yusim ol dok bilong smelim drag (drug).
Sampela kantri i gat bikpela panismen maski em i namba wan taim ol lain i brukim lo; ol dispela kain panismen em man bai go long kalabus long moa long 10-pela yia o dai.
Ol bek we no gat man i was long ol em ol lain i ken stilim na tu, em i ken mekim ol atoriti i tingting planti olsem sampela lain i lusim bom insait long dispela bek.
Long haus, bikos yu save stap wantaim ol dispela lokel jem (germ), i gat bikpela sans olsem yu kamap 'immune' long ol.
Tasol long ol narapela hap bilng graun, long ples we ol bekteria (bacteria) i nupela long yu, i gat bikpela sans olsem yu bai bungim sampela hevi.
Na tu, long ol ples we i hot ol bekteria (bacteria) i ken gro hariap moa na stap longpela taim autsait long bodi.
Olsem na o wip (whip) bilong Delhi Belly, Pharaoh's Curse, Montezuma's Revenge, na ol planti pren bilong ol.
Wankain olsem ol problem bilong pulim win long ol ples kol, problem bilong bel rop long ol hotpela ples em i save kamap na planti taim em i save mekim man i les tasol em i no inap kamapim bikpela bagarap.
Sapos yu wok long travel i go long wanprla kantri we i wok long divelop yet long namba wan taim – o long wanpeal nupela hap bilong graun – no ken ting olsem yu no inap long kisim 'culture shock'.
Ol nupela samting insait long wanpela kantri we i wok long divelop yet i bin daunim planti bilong ol gutpela travela (traveler), long wanem ol i nid long mekim planti liklik senis long kalsa na ol dispela liklik senis i bung wantaim na i kamap olsem bikpela samting tumas.
Bikpela moa em long ol de we yu stat, tingim long amamasim yu yet long ol ' Western-style' na -kwaliti hotel, na ol sevis bilong mekim yu lainim long stap long dispela hap.
No ken slip long wanpela matres o wanpela samting yu putim long graun long ol eria we yu no klia gut long ol lokel animal na binatang.
Sapos yu bai go autsait na mekim kem, bringim wanpela bet bilong kem o wanpela 'hammock' long mekim yu i stap longwe long ol snek, 'scorpion' na kain olsem.
Pulapim haus bilong yu wantaim wanpela naispela kofi long moning na sampela 'chamomile' ti bilong rileks (relax) long nait.
Taim yu stap tasol long haus na holide, yu gat taim long mekim yu yet amamas na kisim sampela taim long mekim wanpela naispela ti o kofi.
Sapos yu pilim olsem yu laik traim sampela nupela samting, kisim dispela taim ling mekim jus o mekim 'smoothies'.
ating yu bai painim wanpela isipela dring we yu ken mekim long brekfas (breakfast) taim yu go bek long 'daily routine' bilong yu.
Sapos yu stap long wanpela siti we i gat kainkain kalsa bilong dring, go long ol 'bar', o 'pub' we stap klostu na yu no save go long em planti taim.
Long ol lain we i no klia long hap tok we ol medikel lain i save yusim, dispela tupela hap tok 'infectious' na 'contagious' i gat narapela narapela mining.
Wanpela sik we i isi tru long spred (spread) em sik we wanpela 'pathogen' i kamapim, kain olsem wanpela vaires, bekteria, fangi (fungi) o ol narapela parasait (parasite).
Wanpela 'contagious' sik em i wanpela sik we i isi tru long kalap i go long narapela man o meri taim yu stap klostu long wanpela man o meri i gat dispela sik.
Planti gavman i tok olsem olgeta visita em kam long kantri bilong ol, ol i lusim wanpela kantri i mas kisim sut marasin bilong banisim ol long ol kainkain sik.
Ol dispela samting we lo i tok long mekim em i senisim bihainim wanem kantri wanpela travela i go long em pinis o i laik go long en.
Wanpela bilong ol gutpela samting long Charlotte, North Carolina, em i olsem i gat planti kwaliti ektiviti bilong ol famili.
Planti taim oll lain i save stap long dispela eria i tok olsem 'family-friendliness' em i wanpela bilong ol nambawan as tingting bilong ol long muv i go long hap, na ol visita i save lukim olsem em i isi long amamas wantaim ol pikinini long hap.
Long 20-pela yia i go pinis, mak bilong ol samting bilong mekim wantaim ol pikinini long Uptown Charlotte em i go antap tru.
Ol famili long Charlotte i no save yusim ol teksi, maski ol i ken yusim ol long mekim sampela samting.
I gat ekstra (extra) kost bilong i gat moa long 2-pela pasindia, olsem na dispela i mekim em i kamap moa ekspensif.
Antarctica em i kol ples we i winim ol kol ples long olgeta hap bilong graun na em i stap long South Pole.
Em i bikpela mani long ol turis long i go na lukim dispela ples. Bodi bilong ol turis i mas fit long i go long dispela hap na ol i ken i go long taim bilong sama long Novemba i go long Febueri, na ol i ken i go long Peninsula, Islands na Ross Sea.
Sampela tausen wokmanmeri i save stap hia long sama (summer). Ol i save stap long kain olsem foapela 'dozen' senta long ol dispela eria, liklik namba bilong ol wokmanmeri tasol i save stap long taim bilong winta (winter).
Insait long Antarctica em ples i flet nating na i gat 2-3 kilomita bilong ais i stap.
Wanwan taim i save i gat balus i go long insait bilong Antarctica long ol lain bilong klaimim maunten o bilong i go long Pole. I gat bikpela 'base' i stap long Pole.
South Pole Traverse (o Highway) em i wanpela 1600 km rot we i stat long McMurdo Station long Ross Sea na i go long Pole.
Sno bilong em i gat ol hol i go insait long graun na i gat ol plak i makim ol dispela hol. Ol spesol trakta (tractor) tasol i ken ron antap long em na pulim ol plang we i gat saplai na 'fuel' i stap antap.
Ol i no save muv hariap olsem na dispela rot i kisim longpela taim long tanim na raunim Transantarctic Mountains long kam long ol ples antap.
Nambawan samtinbg we i save kamapim ol eksiden long winta (winter) em rot we i welwel, 'pavements' (rot bilong wokabaut long sait), na bikpela moa em ol step.
Long 'minimum' mak, yu bai nidim ol su we i gat ol gutpela aninit bilong em. Ol su bilong sama (summer) em ol i save welwel long ais na sno (snow), maski sampela 'boot' bilong winta (winter) tu i no gutpela.
Peten i mas dip (deep) inap, 5 mm (1/5 inch) o moa, na meteriel em i mas 'soft' inap taim em i stap insait long ol kol tempritsa (temperature).
Sampela 'bbot' i gat 'stud' na i gat ikwipmen wei gat moa 'stud' long en bilong yusim long ol kondisen we i welwel, na em i gutpela long planti su na 'boot', na long ol 'heel' bilong su o 'heel' na aninit bilong su wantaim.
Ol 'heel' em ol i mas sotpela na i op. Wesan, karanas o sol ('calcium chloride') em planti taim ol i sace tromoi long rot na liklik han rot bilong mekim ol kar na manmeri i no ken wel.
Ol 'avalanche' em ol i no samting we i no nomol; ol sap maunten i ken holim sampela sno tasol, moa sno bai kam daun olsem 'avalanche'.
Problem em i olsem sno em i 'sticky', olsem na em i nidim sampela samting long mekim em i kam daun, na taim sampela sno i kamdaun dispela i ken mekim na olgeta sno i kam daun.
Sampela taim, nambawan samting we i mekim dispela em i san we i mekim sno i hat, sampela taim em sampela moa sno i pundaun, na sampela taim em ol narapela samting, bikpela moa em ol manmeri.
Wanpela 'tornado' em i wanpela longpela win wei gat 'low-pressure air', we i save pulim ol win i stap long sait sait na karim i go antap.
Ol i save kamapim 'high winds' (planti taim em i 100-200 'mile'/'hour') na i ken apim ol hevipela samting i go antap long win, na karim ol i go taim 'tornado' i muv.
Ol i stat taim ol 'funnel' i kam daun long ol klaut bilong win na ren, na i kamap ol "'tornado" taim ol i tasim graun.
Personal VPN (virtual private network) 'provider' em i nambawan we bilong abrusim 'censorship' bilong gavman na 'commercial IP-geofiltering'.
Ol i antap moa long ol 'web proxies' bikos long sampela as. Ol i ken senisim 'route' bilong olgeta 'internet traffic', i no http tasol.
Planti taim ol i save givim 'higher bandwidth' na gutpela kwailiti sevis. Ol i 'encrypted' olsem na em i hat long ol lain i 'spy' long ol.
Ol nius kampani i save giaman long wok bilong dispela, ol i save tok olsem dispela em long "stopim 'piracy'".
Tru tru, ol 'region codes' i no senisim wanpela samting long pasin bilong brukim lo na mekim kopi; wanapela ' bit-for-bit' kopi i ken pilai gut long wanpela divai (device) wankain olsem 'original' kopi.
Tru tru wok bilong en em long givim ol kamapi moa kontrol long maket bilong ol; as tingting bilong en em long wokim moa mani.
Bikos ol kol (call) i save go long intanet, yu no nid long yusim wanpela fon kampani we i stap long ples yu stap long en o i stap long ples we yu go long en.
I no gat wanpela lo we i tok olsem yu niod long kisim wanpela lokel namba long komunit we yu stap insait long en, yu ken kisim wanpela 'satellite Internet connection' long 'wilds of Chicken, long Alaska na makim wanpela namba wei tok olsem yu stap long ples bilong san long Arizona.
Planti taim, yu bai wanpela 'global number' long em yet we bai larim ol PSTN fon i ringim yu. Wanem hap dispela namba i kam long en bai mekim sampela senis i kamap long ol lain i ringim yu.
Ol 'real-time text translator apps' – em ol aplikesen we i inap long mekim 'automatic' trenslesen bilong ol hap toktok long wanpela tok ples i no long narapela.
Sampela bilong ol aplikesen insait long dispela grup i ken mekim trenslesen long narapela tok long 'signs' o ol narapela samting we 'user' i poinim smatfon i go long en.
Ol 'translation engine' i kamap gutpela moa moa yet, na ol i save givim ol stretpela trenslesen (na wanwan taim tasol em ol toktok we i no gat mining), tasol yu mas lukaut bikos, ol i ken mekim bikpela asua na tanim olgeta toktok kranki.
Wanpela bilong ol nambawan 'app' insait long dispela grup em Google Translate, we i save mekim ol 'offline' trenslesen taim em i daunlodim olgeta 'language data' we em i nidim.
Pasin bilong yusim ol 'GPS navigation app' long smatfon bilong yu em i isipela we na gutpela we bilong painim wanem hap yu laik go long en taim yu stap autsait long kantri bilong yu.
Em i ken seivim mani bilong baim wanpela nupela mep (map) taim yu yusim wanpela GPS, o wanpela 'standalone' GPS divais (device)o rentim wanpela long wanpela 'car rental company'.
Sapos yu no gat wanpela 'data connection' long fon bilong yu, o taim fon bilong yu i stap 'out of range', pefomens bilong em bai i no inap long wok gut o i no stap.
Olgeta kona stoa i pulap wantaim ol kainkain 'pre-paid' fon kad we yu ken yusim long ol 'pay phone' o long ol telefon.
Maski planti bilong ol dispela kad em i gutpela long ring long olgeta hap, sampela i save givim spesol reit (rate) long ring i go long ol kantri i stap insait long wanpela grup.
Long kisim ol dispela sevis planti taim em yu bai ringim wanpela 'toll-free' telefon namba we yu ken ring long planti fon na i no gat sas bilong em.
Ol rul (rule) bilong 'regular photography' em yu ken yusim long 'video recording', na dispela em i gutpela moa.
Sapos yu kisim foto bilong wanpela samting we i tambu long kisim foto long en, orait yu ken tingting long kisim video bilong em.
Sapos yu yusim wanpela 'drone', sekim gut long wanem samting yu ken kisim foto long en na wanem ol tok orait pepa o narapela laisens em yu mas kisim long mekim dispela.
Flaim wanpela 'drone' klostu long wanpela eapot o antap long wanpela bikpela lain manmeri em i no gutpela, maski lo i no tok tambu long en long eria bilong yu.
Tude raun long balus em wanwan taim tasol i save baim tiket stret long 'airline' na i no mekim 'search' na skelim ol prais.
Sampela taim dispela seim (same) ron bilong balus i ken i gat narapela narapela prais long kainkain 'aregator' na em bai gutpwla long mekim 'search' long websait bilong dispela balus kampani bipo long mekim 'booking'.
Maski yu bai no inap long nidim wanpela 'visa' long mekim ol sotpela visit long sampela kantri olsem wanpela turis o go long mekim wok bisnis, taim yu go olsem wanpela intanesinel sumating em yu bai stap longpela taim moa long sapos yu go olsem wanpela turis nating.
Planti taim, pasin bilong stap long wanpela narapela kantri long longpela taim em yu bai nid long kisim wanpela visa pastaim.
Ol visa bilong ol sumatin i gat kainkain rikwaimen na rot bilong mekim aplikesen na em i no wankain olsem ol nomol turis o bisnis visa.
Long planti kantri, yu bai nid long i gat wanpela leta i kam long dispela institusen we yu bai stadi long en, na tu yu bai nidim evidens bilong mani yu gat lontg en long sapotim yu yet long wanpela yia bilong kos bilong yu.
Sekim wantaim dispela institusen, na tu sekim 'immigration department' bilong kantri yu laik stadi long en long kisim moa infomesen long ol rikwaimen.
Tasol sapos yu wanpela 'diplomat', pasin bilong wok long narapela kantri em i min olsem yu bai nid long givim 'income tax' long kantri yu stap long en.
Straksa bilong 'income tax' em i narakain long narapela narapela kantri, na reit (rate) bilong takis na 'brackets' em i narakain narakain long wanwan kantri.
Long sampela 'federal' kantri, kain olsem United States na Canada, 'income tax' em i 'federal' level na lokel level wantaim i save kisim, olsem na ol reit (rate) na 'bracket' i ken senis long wanpela rijen i go long narapela.
Maski 'immigration check' em i no save stap o i no save kamap taim yu kam bek long kantri bilong yu, 'customs control' em i ken hat wok liklik.
Yu mas lukim olsem yu save long wanem samting yu ken o i no inap long bringim i go insait long kantri na tokaut sapos mak bilong samting yu bringim em i go antap moa long wanem lo i tok orait long en.
Isipela we bilong statim bisnis bilong 'travel writing' em long stretim pasin bilong yu long rait taim yu statim wanpela 'travel blog' websait.
Taim yu kamap gutpela long mekim 'formatting' na 'editing' long web, orait bihain, yu ken kamapim websait bilong yu yet.
Pasin bilong mekim volentia wok taim yu travel em i wanpela gutpela we long mekim sampela gutpela senis, tasol em i no wansait we yu tasol i givim samting.
Pasin bilong i stap na mekim wok volentia long narapela kantri em i wanpela gutpela we bilong save long narapela kalsa, bungim nupela manmeri, na lainim sampela nupela samting long yu yet, na kisim sampela gutpela tingting na lainim sampela nupela samting.
Em i gutpela we bilong yusim gut bajet (budget) na mekim yu i ken i stpa longpela taim long wanpela hap bikos planti ol wok volentia i save givim rum na kaikai na wanpela liklik pe.
Ol Viking i yusim ol wara bilong Russia long go bek long Black Sea na Caspian Sea. Ol hap bilong ol dispela rot bilong travel long wara em ol lain i ken yusim yet. Sekim sapos i gat nid long kisim spesol tok orait, dispela em i hat long kisim.
White Sea–Baltic Canal i konektim Arctic Ocean i go long Baltic Sea, long Lake Onega, Lake Ladoga na Saint Petersburg, bikpela moa em ol wara na raunwara i konektim.
Lake Onega i konekt tu i go long Volga, olsem na long kam olsem long Caspian Sea insait long Russia em i isi long mekim.
Yu mas save olsem taim yu go long ol 'marina' olgeta samting bai kamap ples klia. Yu bai bungim ol narapela lain i save kalap long bot na ol bai serim infomesen wantaim yu.
Yu bai putim ol tok save long helpim yu laik givim, wokabaut i go i kam long ol 'dock', go toktok long lain na klinim ol 'yatch' bilong ol, traim long toktok wantaim ol 'sailor' long ol 'bar, na kain olsem.
Traim long toktok long planti manmeri we yu inap long toktok long en. Bihain long sampela taim olgeta lain bai save long yu na bai givim sampela tok save long yu long wanem ol bot i wok long painim wokman.
Yu mas makim Frequent Flyer 'airline' bilong yu gut.
Maski yu ting olsem em i isi long joinim 'airline' we yu save flai planti taim long en, yu mas save olsem ol samting we ol i save givim em i narakain narakain na ol 'frequent flyer points' we ol i save givim aninit long narapela 'airline' em i gutpela moa long wankain 'alliance'.
Ol 'airline' kain olsem Emirates, Etihad Airways, Qatar Airways & Turkish Airlines i mekim sevis bilong ol i go long Africa, na ol i givim ol koneksen i go long planti bikpela siti bilong Africa long gutpela prais moa long ol 'airlines' bilong Europe.
Turkish Airlines i save flai i go long 39-pela ples insait long 30 kantri insait long Africa stat long 2014 i kam inap nau.
Sapos yu gat sampela moa taim bilong travel, sekim hamas totol bilong raun i go long Africa na hamas totol bilong raun long olgeta hap bilong graun.
No ken lus tingting long putim narapela kost bilong ol narapela visa, 'departure taxes', trenspot, na kain olsem long olgeta ol ples autsait long Africa.
Sapos yu laik flai raun long wol long Southern Hemisphere, namba bilong ol balus i save flai na ol ples bilong i go long en em i no planti bikos i no gat ol 'transoceanic routes'.
No gat 'airline alliance' i karamapim olgeta tripela 'oceanic crossing' insait long Southern Hemisphere (na SkyTeam i no karampaim wanpela bilong ol dispela 'crossing').
Tasol, Star Alliance i save karamapim olgeta samting, wanpela samting tasol em i no karamapim em 'eastern' South Pacific long Santiago de Chile i go long Tahiti, dispela em i wanpela LATAM Oneworld flight.
Dispela 'flight' em i no wanpela tasol sapos yu laik lusim South Pacific na 'west coast' bilong South America. (lukim infomesen i stap daunbilo)
Long 1994, ol Armenian Nagorno-Karabakh rijen bilong Azerbaijan i statim woa agensim ol Azeris.
Armenia i sanap baksait long ol, na ol i kamap wantaim nupela 'republic'. Tasol, ol i no kamap olsem wanpela kantri ‑ Armenia tu ‑ i no luksave long ol olsem ol i wanpela kantri.
Ol tok pait long dispela rijen i kontinu long bagarapim ol rilesensip namel long Armenia na Azerbaijan.
Canal District (Dutch: Grachtengordel) em wanpela '17 centruy' distrik we planti lain i save long en na em i raunim Binnenstad long Amsterdam.
Olgeta hap bilong dispela distrik em ol i bin makim olsem wanpela UNESCO World Heritage Site bikos long narakain histori na kalsa bilong em, na kost bilong ol propeti bilong en em i wanpela bilong ol propeti we i bikpela mani tru long em.
Cinque Terre, dispela em i min olsem Five Lands, em o gat faivpela liklik ples we i stap klostu long solwara na nem bilong ol em Riomaggiore, Manarola, Corniglia, Vernazza na Monterosso we i stap long Liguria rijen bilong Italy.
Ol i stap long list bilong UNESCO World Heritage.
Long planti 'century' i go pinis, ol manmeri i bin bildim ol fletpela eria long ol ples we i no stret, ol ples we i sanap i go antap i go long 'cliff' we i lukluk i go long solwara.
Wanpela hap bilong samting we i naispela long en em i olsem em i no gat divelopmen long sait bilong bisnis, Ol liklik rot, trein (train) na bot i konketim ol liklik ples, na ol kar i no inap stap long autsait na i go long ol.
Ol 'variety' bilong French we ol i yusim long Belgium na Switzerland i narakain liklik long French we ol yusim long France, maski ol i wankain inap na ol lain long wanpela i ken harim ol lain long narapela 'variety' i toktok.
Bikpela moa, sistem bilong namba insait long Belgium na Switerland we i save yusim French em i narakain long French we ol i yusim long France, na we ol i kolik sampela wod em i narakain liklik.
Maski long dispela, olgeta lain long Belgium na Switzerland we i save yusim French i save lainim 'standard French' insait long skul, olsem na ol bai i inap long save maski yu yusim namba sistem bilong 'standard French'.

Ol wol na ruf bilong ol ‘ice cave’ i ken pundaun na i ken pasim ol ‘crack’.

NextGen em i wanpela sistem we FAA i tok olsem em bai larim ol balus long flai long ol sotpela rot na seivim (save) planti milien galen (gallon) bilong 'fuel' long olgeta yia na daunim mak bilong 'carbon' we i save go long 'air'.

Wanpela stadi we ol i pablisim (publish) long Fonde insait long wanpela jenel (journal) ol i kolim Science i givim infomesen long wanpela nupela 'specie' bilong pisin we i staplong Galapagos Islands bilong Ecuador.
Ol lain i mekim risets long Princeton University long United States na Uppsala University long Sweden i mekim ripot long wanpela nupela 'specie' we i kamap insait long tupela generesen (generation), tasol ol i ting long dispela proses (process) i kisim longpela taim moa, em i kamap bikos long 'breeding' i kamap namel long Darwin finch bilong dispela eria, Geospiza fortes, na cactus finch we i kam long narapela eria, Geospiza conirostris.
Gol em ol i ken mekim i go kama kainkain seip (shape). Na ol i ken rolim em na kamapim ol liklik liklik seip (shape).
Ol i ken pulim em na mekim em i kamap wanpela liklik bun waia, we ol i ken tanim tanim na pasim. Ol i ken paitim em long hama o rolim na kamapim ol 'sheets'.
Ol i ken mekim em i kama bun na liklik nogut tru na stikim (stick) em i go long ol narapela metel (metal). Sampela taim ol i ken mekim em i kama bun nogut tru na yusim em long bilasim ol piksa we ol peintim (paint) long han na insait long buk we ol i kolim "illuminated manuscripts".
Dispela em ol kolim pH bilong kemikel (chemical). Yu ken mekim wanpela 'indicator' wantaim retpela jus bilong kabis.
Kala bilong jus bilong kabis i save sensim bihainim hamas 'acid' o 'basic' (alkaline) i stap long dispela kemikel.
Mak bilong Hydrogen (dispela H insait long pH) 'ion' insait long kemikel (chemical) we ol i testim bai soim level bilong pH.
Ol 'ions' bilong Hydrogen em ol 'proton' we ol i bin rausim ol 'electron' bilong ol (bikos ol Hydrogen 'atom' i gat wanpela 'proton' na wanpela 'electron').
Miksim tupela drai pauda wantaim na bihain, wantaim han we i klin na wet, skwisim (squeeze) ol na mekim wanpela bal.
Dispela wara i stap long han bilong yu bai i 'react' wantaim ol 'layer' we i stap autsait, we bai i pilim narakain na kamapim wanpela kain sel.
Ol siti bilong Harappa na Mohenjo-daro i gat wanpela toilet we i yusim wara long klostu olgeta haus, naol i join i go long wanpela narapela kain 'sewage system'.
Ol samting bilong bipo we i soim ol dispela 'sewage system' em ol i bin painim ol long ol haus bilong ol siti bilong Minoan bilong Crete na Santorini long Greece.
I gat ol toilet bilong bipotaim tru long Egypt, Persia na China. Long hap bilong ol Rome, ol toilet em ol i stap olsem hap bilong ol pablik haus bilong waswas we ol man na meri i save bung wantaim.
Taim yu ringim sampela lain we i stap tausen 'mile' longwe, yu wok long yusim wanpela 'satellite'.
Dispela 'satellite' long 'space' i kisim dispela kol (call) na salim em i kam daun bek gen, wantu tru.
Dispela 'satellite' em wanpela 'rocket' i bin salim i go long 'space'. Ol saintis i yusim ol 'telescope' long 'space' bikos 'atmosphere' bilong Earth i save tanim sampela bilong ol lait bilong yumi na hau yumi lukim ol samting.
Ol i save yusim wanpela jaient 'rocket' we longpela bilong em i winim 100 'feet' long putim wanpela 'telescope' long 'space'.
Dispela wil (wheel) i senisim graun long kainkain we. Bikpela samting tru we wil i mekim long yumi em i givim yumi isipela 'transportation' we i save muv hariap moa.
Em i givim yumi trein (train), kar, ma planti narapela masin bilong 'transportation'.
Aninit long ol em ol namel sais pusi we i save kaikai ol namel sais abus stat long rebit (rabbit) i go long entelop (antelope) na dia (deer).
Las tru, i gat planti liklik pusi (wantaim ol dispela we yumi save lukautim long haus) we i save kaikai ol liklik abus kain olsem ol insek (insect), rat, palai, na pisin.
Sikret (secret) bilong hau ol i save stap gut em i dispela samting ol i kolim 'niche', wanpela spesol wok wanwan pusi i save mekim na em i no resis wantaim narapela.
Ol laion em ol pusi we i save laik long stap wantaim ol narapela pusi, na ol i save stap wantaim long ol bikpela grup we ol i kolim ol 'pride'.
Ol 'pride' i save i gat wanpela i go long mak bilong tripela man, wantaim kain olsem tetipela meri na pikinini.
Ol meri em ol i kam long wanpela famili, kain olsem wanpela bikpela famili bilong ol sista na ol pikinini meri bilong ol.
Ol 'pride' bilong ol laion i save ekt long wankain we olsem ol 'pack' bilong ol wulf o dok, ol dispela animal we i wankain long ol laion (tasol i no ol narapela bikpela pusi) long pasin, na tu ol i save kamapim bikpela birua long ol narapela animal we ol i save kaikai.
Wanpela gutpela 'athlete', taiga i ken klaim (em i no save klaim gut tumas), swim, kalap long bikpela mak na pulim ol samting wantaim strong we i faivpela taim moa long strong bilong man.
Taiga em i stap insait long seim (same) grup (Genus Panthera) olsem ol laion, 'leopards', na 'jaguars'. Ol dispela foapela pusi em ol tasol i ken 'roar'.
'Roar' bilong taiga em i wankaim olsem 'full-voiced roar' bilong wanpela laion, tasol em i klostu i laik wankain olsem wanpela sentens bilong man i pulim win taim em kros na singaut.
Ol 'ocelot' i save laik long kaikai ol liklik animal. Ol i save ketsim ol manki (monkey), snek, rat na ol pisin sapos ol i inap long ketsim. Klostu olgeta animal we ol 'ocelot' i save painim em ol i liklik sais moa long em.
Ol saintis i ting olsem ol 'ocelot' i save bihainim na painim ol narapela animal long kaikai (traim long kaikai) taim ol i smelim samting, ol i kisim smel bilong ol long wanem hap ol i bin i stap long em long graun.
Ol i ken lukluk gut tru long tudak wantaim 'night vision', na tu, ol i save muv isi tru. Ol 'ocelot' i save painim kaikai bilong ol taim ol i hait wantaim ol samting i stap long envairomen na kalap antap long animal we ol i laik ketsim.
Taim wanpela liklik grup bilong ol animal (wanpela liklik namba) i lusim bikpela populesen (population) we ol i kam long en (sapos ol i muv i go antap long wanpela maunten o wanpela liklik wara, o saps ol i muv i go long wanpela nupela ailan na ol i painim hat long i go bek) ol bai lukim olsem ol i stap long wanpela narapela envairomen we i no wankain olsem bipo.
Displela nupela envairomen i gat ol kainkain risos na ol kainkain kompetisen, olsem na dispela nupela populesen (population) bai nidim ol narapela pasin long kamap strong moa long mak we ol i bin stap long en bipo.
Dispela narapela populesen i no senis, tasol ol i nid long mekim ol wankain senis long envairomen bilong ol olsem bipo.
Bihain long sampela taim, dispela nupela populesen i stat long mekim senis na lainim long stap long nupela envairomen bilong ol, ol i stat long luk narakain liklik long narapela populesen.
I go i go, na bihain long sampela tausen o milien yia, dispela tupela populesen bai luk narakain olgeta bai ol lain i no tok olsem ol i wanpela 'specie'.
Mipela i save kolim dispela proses (process) 'speciation', dispela em i min olsem kamapim nupela 'specie'. 'Speciation' em i wanpela samting we yumi i no inap long abrusim na em i wanpela impoten pat bilong 'evolution'.
Ol plent (plant) i save mekim 'oxygen' we yumi ol manmeri i save pulim win long en, na ol i save kisim 'carbon dioxide' we yumi ol manmeri i save rausim i kam autsait long bodi bilong yumi (dispela em, taim win we yumi i pulim i go insait i kam autsait).
Ol plent (plant) i save mekim kaikai bilong ol long san taim 'photosynthesis' i kamap. Ol i save givim seid (shade).
Yumi save mekim ol haus bilong yumi long ol plent (plant) na yumi save mekim ol klos bilong yumi long ol plent. Planti bilong ol kaikai we yumi save kaikai em ol plent. Sapos no gat plent, ol animal bai i no inap long stap laip.
Ol mosasaurus i bin i stap olsem nambawan wel animal long dispela taim, no gat narapela animal i inap long kaikaim ol, olsem na ol i no pret long wanpela samting. Ol i save pret long narapela mosasaurus tasol.
Maus bilong em i gat moa long 70-pela tit we i sap olsem resa, wantaim wanpela narapela lain tit we i stap long ruf bilong maus. Dispela em i min olsem wanem samting em i bungim bai i no inap long ranawe.
Yumi no inap long save, tasol ating em i gat fok tang. Em i save kaikai trausel, bikpela fis, ol narapela mosasaurus, na ating em i save kaikai ol manmeri tu.
Em i save kaikai olgeta samting we i go insait long wara; maski wanpela jaient dainaso kain olsem T. rex bai i no inap long em.
Maski planti bilong ol kaiki bilong ol em mipela i ken save, ol Rom i gat ol kaikai we yumi i no save long en o ol save yusim long taim bilong bikpela bung kaikai, wanpela em wel pik, 'peacock', 'snail', na wanpela kain rat ol i kolim 'dormouse'.
Wanpela narapela samting we i narakain em i olsem taim ol manmeri we i no gat planti samting i kaikai kaiakia bilong ol taim ol i sindaun long ol sia, ol maniman i save laik long i gat ol bikpela bung kaikai we ol i save slip long sait bilong ol na kaikai.
Ol lain bilong bipo long Rom i no bin i gat kaikai we i kam long America o Asia we nau ol i stap long Europe long sampela handret yia bihain.
Wanpela eksampel em olsem, ol i no gat kon, o tomato, o potato, o kakau, na no gat wanpela bilong ol lain bilong bipo long Rom i bin teistim wanpela 'turkey'.
Ol lain long Babylon i bildim wanpela namba wan tempel long wanwan god bilong ol we ol i save mekim olsem dispela em i haus bilong dispela god.
Ol manmeri bai bringim ol samting bilong mekim ofa i go long ol god na ol pris bai traim long inapim samting we ol god i nidim taim ol i mekim ol seremoni (ceremony) na ol bikpela bung bilong lotu.
Wanwan tempel i gat wanpela ples bilong sindaun autsait na i gat ples insait we ol pris tasol i ken i go insait.
Sampela taim ol spesel taua we seip (shape) bilong ol i olsem ol 'pyramid', na ol i kolim ol 'ziggurats', em ol i save bildim olsem pat bilong ol tempel.
Antap long dispela taua em sampela spesol ples bilong dispela god i stap.
Long ol ples we i hot long Middle East, haus em i no impoten.
Planti samting long laip bilong ol Hebrew famili i save kamap autsait long haus.
Ol meri i save kukim kaikai autsait long sait bilong haus; ol stoa em ol tebol we i op na i lukluk i go long rot. Ol i save yusim ol ston long bildim ol haus.
I bin no gat ol bikpela bus insait long graun bilong ol Canaan, olsem na plang em i ekspensif (expensive) tumas.
I no gat planti lain i sindaun long Greenland. Long ol tumbuna stori bilong ol Norway, ol i tok olsem Erik the Red em ol i bin rausim em long Iceland bikos em i bin kilim wanpela man, na taim em i travel i go long wes, em i painim Greenland na em i givim dispela nem long en.
Tasol maski em i painim dispela ples, i gat ol Eskimo i bin i stap pinis long hap long dispela taim.
Maski wanwan kantri em i bin 'Scandinavian', i gat planti samting i narakain namel long ol manmeri, ol king, ol kastom na histori bilong Denmark, Sweden, Norway na Iceland.
Sapos yu bin lukim muvi National Treasure, yu bai ting olsem ol i raitim wanpela 'treasure map' long baksait bilong Declaration of Independence pepa.
Tasol, dispela em i no tru. Maski i gat samting we ol i raitim long baksait bilong wanpela dokumen, dispela em i no wanpela 'treasure map'.
Ol i raitim ol dispela hap tok long baksait bilong Declaration of Independence pepa "Original Declaration of Independence dated 4th July 1776". Dispela hap tok i stap long aninit bilong dispela dokumen, na em i stap 'upside down'.
