Taim no gat man i save long husat i raitim ol dispela hap tok, ol i save olsem taim em i nupela yet, dispela bikpela 'parchment' dokumen (sais bilong en, em 29¾ 'inches' na 24½ 'inches') em ol i bin rolim bai em i ken stap long storej (storage).
Olsem na, em i luk olsem dispela hap tok ol i bin raitim bihain bai em i ken i stap olsem wanpela 'label'.
Ol D-Day 'landings' na ol narapela pait i bin mekim hap not bilong France i kamap fri, tasol hap saut i no bin kamap fri yet.
Dipela hap em ol "Vichy" French i bin bosim. Ol dispela lain ol French manmeri husat i bin mekim 'peace' wantaim ol German long 1940 na i wok wantaim ol lain i kam long kisim kantri bilong ol na ol i no pait agensim ol.
Long 15 August 1940, ol Allies i holimpasim hap saut bilong France, the pait em ol i bin kolim "Operation Dragoon".
Insait long tupela wik tasol ol soldia bilong America na ol Free French i mekim hap saut bilong France i kamap fri na ol i wok long i go long Germany.
Wanpela 'civilization' em i wanpela kalsa we wanpela bikpela lain manmeri husat i save stap wantaim na wok wantaim i serim, em i wanpela 'society'.
Dispela hap tok 'civilization' em i kam long wanpela tok Latin 'civilis', em i min olsem 'civil', na em i wankain olsem narapela tok Latin 'civis', mining bilong en em 'citizen', na 'civitas', mining bilong en em siti o 'city-state', na dispela tu em i toktok long sais bilong 'society'.
Ol 'city-states' em ol samting we i save kamapim wanpela kantri. Insait long wanpela 'civilizational culture' em ol lain i save givim save bilong ol i go long sampela 'generation', wanpela kain 'footprint' bilong kalsa we i save stap na rot bilong givim save long ol narapela.
Planti taim ol liklik kalsa i save pinis hariap na i no save lusim evidens (evidence) bilong histori bilong ol na ol savemanmeri i no save lukim ol olsem ol i 'civilization' tru tru.
Long taim bilong Revolutionary War, pastaim ol tetinpela 'states' i kamapim wanpela 'central government' we i no strong—we Congress em i wanpela komponen (component) tasol—aninit long Articles of Confederation.
Congress i no gat pawa long makim na kisim takis, na, bikos i bin no gat 'national executive' o 'judiciary', em i save yusim ol 'state authorities', husat i no save wok wantaim em long planti taim, long mekim ol manmeri i bihainim ol 'act' bilong em.
Na tu, em i no gat atoriti long senisim ol 'tax law' na ol 'tariff' namel long ol 'state'.
Ol 'Article' i nidim ol lain long tok orait long olgeta 'state' bipo long ol i ken mekim senis na ol 'state' i kisim 'central government' olsem na ol lain we ol i makim i no save stap.
'National football' bilong Italy, wantaim 'national football' tim bilong Germany em tupela namba tu tim we i gutpela tru insait long olgeta hap bilong graun na ol i bin sempion bilong FIFA World Cup long 2006.
Ol 'sport' we planti manmeri i save long en em 'football', 'basketball', 'volleyball', 'water-polo', 'fencing', 'rugby', 'cycling', 'ice hockey', 'roller hockey' na 'F1 motor racing'.
Ol 'winter sport' em planti lain long ol 'Northern regions' i save long en, na ol lain long Italy i save pilai insait long ol intanesinel geim (game) na ol Olympic events.
Japan i gat 7,000 ailan (bikpela ailan tru em i Honshu), na dispela i mekim Japan i kamalpl olsem namba 7 bikpela ailan insait long olgeta hap bilong graun.
Bikos long grup bilong ol ailan we Japan i gat, ol laini save kolim Japan olsem, long sait bilong 'geography', em i wanpela "'archipelago'"
Stat bilong Taiwan i kamap long '15th century' taim ol 'sailor' bilong Europe i abrusim em na i rekodim nem bilong em olsem Ilha Formosa, o naispela ailan.
Long 1624, Dutch East India Company i wokim wanpela senta bilong ol long 'southwestern' Taiwan, dispela i statim wanpela senis we i kamap long pasin bilong wokim 'grain' taim ol i kisim ol wokman bilong China long wok long ol rais na suga plentesen (plantation) bilong em.
Long 1683, ol soldia bilong Qing dynasty (1644-1912) i holimpasim na kisim 'western' na 'northern' nambis eria bilong Taiwan na tokaut olsem Taiwan em i wanpela provins bilong Qing Empire long 1885.
Long 1895, bihain long em i lusim pait insait long First Sino-Japanese War (1894-1895), Qing gavman i sainim Treaty of Shimonoseki, insait long dispela em i givim pawa bilong Taiwan i go long Japan, husat i bosim dispela ailan i go inap long 1945.
Machu Picchu i gat tripela bikpela straksa (structure), nem bilong ol em Intihuatana, Temple of the Sun, na Room of the Three Windows.
Planti bilong ol bilding we i stap long arere bilong dispela straka (structure) em ol i bin bildim gen long helpim ol turis long save wanem kain we dispela straksa i bin luk long taim bipo.
Long 1976, teti pesen (percent) bilong Machu Picchu em ol i bin bildim bek gen na ol i wok long stretim yet i kam inap tude.
Eksampel, 'still image photography' fomet (format) we planti lain i save long en em i 35mm, we i nambawan sais bilong 'film' bihain long taim bilong 'analog film'.
Ol i wokim em yet long tude, tasol impoten moa em i olsem 'aspect ratio' bilong en em ol 'digital camera image senor' fomet (format) i kisim na yusim.
Ol 35mm fomet (format) em ol, i ken mekim ol lain i paul, ol i gat 36mm long 'width' na 24mm long 'height'.
'Aspect ratio' bilong dispela fomet (format) (ol i divaidim (divide) em wantaim twelv long kisim wanpela liklik 'whole-number ratio') na ol i tok dispela 'ratio' em i 3:2.
Planti ol fomet (format) we ol lain i save yusim (eksampel, APS famili bilong ol fomet) em i wankain o klostu wankain olsem dispela 'aspect ratio'.
Dispela 'rule of thrids' we planti lain i save bagarapim na tok pilai long en em i wanpela isipela 'guideline' we kamapim gutpela foto na i mekim na i gat sampela oda insait long wanpela piksa.
Em i tok olsem gutpela ples bilong wanpela sabjek (subject) long i stap long taim bilong kisim foto em long ples we ol lain i brukim piksa i go long tripela hap 'vertically' na 'horizontally' (lukim eksampel).
Long dispela taim, Katolik Sios i bin i gat planti mani na pawa, olsem na ol i skelim em gut tru.
Moa long wan tausen yia, dispela lotu bilong ol Kristen i bin bungim ol kantri bilong Europe wantaim, maski ol i gat wanwan tok ples na kastom bilong ol yet.
Dispela bikpela pawa bilong em i kamapim senis long olgeta manmeri. Stat long king na i go daun long ol manmeri nating we i no gat nem na namba.
Wanpela bilong ol bikpela bilip bilong ol Kristen em i olsem ol i mas yusim gut mani na kago bilong ol long helpim ol narapela we i gat pen na hevi o i no gat mani na kaikai. Ol i bilip olsem mani bilong sios em i bilong mekim dispela wok.
Rom i bin go pas long lukautim wok bilong sios long tausen yia na planti pawa na moni i stap long Rom. Dispela i mekim na planti manmeri i wok long i gat tupela tingting sapos em i inapim dispela bilip, o nogat.
Bihain tasol long pait i stat, Britain i mekim wanpela 'naval blockade' long Germany.
Dispela plen bilong ol em i wok gut, ol i stopim impoten saplai (supply) i go long militeri (military) na ol manmeri, maski dispela 'blokade' i brukim intanesinel lo we i bin kamap aninit long ol agrimen bilong tupela 'century' i go pinis.
Britain i putim ol bom aninit long ol intanesinel wara long stopim ol sip long i go insait long bikpela seksen bilong solwara, dispela i kamapim birua tu long ol sip bilong ol narapela lain we i no stap insait long dispela pait.
Bikos i no gat bekim i kamap long dispela 'tactic', Germany i ting olsem wankain samting bai i kamap long ol 'submarine' bilong em.
Long ol yia bilong 1920, pasin bilong bikpela namba bilong ol sitisen (citizen) na ol kantri em long kisim bel isi na wanbel na stap ol yet.
Ol kantri i lukim pinis ol pen na hevi na kranki pasin bilong woa we i kamap insait long World War I, ol kantri i laik long abrusim dispela kain samting long kamap gen long bihaintaim.
Long 1884, Telsa i muv i go long United States of America long wok wantaim Edison Company long New York City.
Em i kamap long US wantaim 4 cents, wanpela 'poetry' buk, na wanpela leta bilong rekomendesen i kam long Charles Batchelor (meneja bilong em long wok em i bin mekim bipo) i go long Thomas Edison.
Ancient China i gat wanpela narakain we bilong soim ol kainkain time; wanwan 'stage' bilong China o wanwan famili we i holim pawa em i wanpela 'dynasty'.
Na tu, namel long wanwan 'dynasty' i gat taim we ol provins i stap ol yet. Wanpela bilong ol dispela taim we planti lain i save long en em taim bilong Three Kingdom we i stap long 60-pela yia namel long Han na Jin Dynasty.
Long ol dispela ol taim bikpela pait i kamap namel long ol planti bilong ol famili we i gat nem na namba i pait long sia king.
Three Kingdoms em i wanpela bilong ol taim bilong pait insait long histori bilong Ancient China we planti tausen manmeri i dai taim ol pait long sindaun long nambawan sia insait long 'grand palace' long Xi’an.
I gat planti ol samting i kamap long 'society' na 'politics' kain olsem pasin bilong yusim 'metric system'. na senis long 'absolutism' i go long 'republicanism', na pasin bilong 'nationalism' na bilip long kantri em i samting bilong ol manmeri na i no bilong wanpela man tasol we i bosim ol.
Na tu, bihain long Revolution ol wok i op long olgeta man long larim ol man i gat driman na i save wok hat long mekim ol gutpela wok we ol i laik long mekim.
Dispela em i wankain long ol militeri (military) bikos nau ol i no kisim 'rank' we i bihainim 'class' bilong famili bilong ol, tasol ol bai i kisim 'rank' we i bihainim pasin bilong ol na wanem samting ol i inap long mekim.
French Revolution i kirapim tingting bilong planti ol narapela 'working class' manmeri long ol narapela kantri long statim ol 'revolution' bilong ol yet.
Muhammad i gat intres long ol samting we i bikpela moa long ol samting bilong dispela laip. Em i save go long wanpela hul bilong ston we ol i kolim olsem “Hira'” long Mountain of “Noor” (lait) long i stap na tingting.
Dispela hul bilong ston, we i stap yet, i save givim klia piksa long ol bilip bilong Muhammad.
Em i stap antap long wanpela bilong ol maunten long hap not bilong Mecca, dispela hul bilong ston em i stap hait long olgeta hap bilong graun.
Tru tru, em i no isi long painim em o save sapos em i stap. Taim yu stap insait long dispela hul bilong ston, em yu stap longwe olgeta long ol narapela samting.
Yu no inap long lukim wanpela narapela samting tasol skai we i klia, i luk nais na i stap antap na planti maunten i raunim em. Yu no inap long lukim o harim ol samting bilong dispela graun taim yu stap insait long dispela hul bilong ston.
'Great Pyramid' long Giza em i wanpela bilong ol 'seven wonders' we i sanap yet long tude.
Ol lain Egypt i bildim long 'third century' BCE, Great Pyramid em i wanpela bilong ol bikpela pyramid straksa we ol i wokim long givim ona long wanpela Pharaoh we i dai pinis.
 Giza Plateau, o "Giza Necropolis" insait long Valley of the Dead bilong Egypt i gat sampela pyramid (bikpela tru long olgeta em 'great pyramid'), sampela liklik 'tomb', sampela tempel, na 'great Sphinx'.
'Great pyramid' em ol i bin wokim long givim ona long Pharaoh Khufu, na planti ol liklik pyramid, ol 'tomb', na tempel em ol i wok long givim ona long ol meri na famili memba bilong Khufu.
Dispela "'up bow" mark' i luk olsem wanpela V na dispela "'down bow mark'" i luk olsem wanpela 'staple' o wanpela 'square' i no gat aninit sait bilong em.
'Up' em i min olsem yu mas stat long 'tip' na pusim 'bow', na 'down' em i min olsem yu mas stat long 'frog' (dispela em i ples we han bilong yu i holim 'bow') na pulim dispela 'bow'.
Wanpela 'up-bow' em i save kamapim wanpela saun we i 'soft' moa, na wanpela 'down-bow' em i wanpela saun we i strong moa na i gat moa fos.
Yu kem mekim ol mak bilong yu yet wantaim pensil, tasol tingim ol 'bowing marks' we ol i printim pinis em i gat as na ol i stap, olsem na yu mas rispektim ol.
Long namba 6 de bilong Oktoba 1789 ol maket meri i mekim King Louis XVI, Queen Marie Antoinette na tupela liklik pikinini bilong ol (Marie Therese we i gat 11-pela krismas na Louis-Charles we i gat 4-pela krismas) na susa bilong King, Madam Elizabeth, i go bek long Paris taim ol i stap long Versailles.
Insait long wanpela karis, ol i ron i go bek long Paris taim ol bikpela lain manmeri i belhat na i raunim ol na i wok long singaut na mekim ol kainkain toktok bilong pretim King na Queen.
Ol dipela bikpela lain manmeri we i belhat na i stap i fosim King na Queen long larim ol windua bilong karis bilong ol i op na i stap.
Wanpela taim wanpela man insait long ol bikpela lain manmeri i apim na soim het bilong wanpela 'royal guard' we ol i bin kilim long Versailles long fran bilong Queen na em i pret nogut tru.
Mani bilong woa we U.S i kamapim taim em i laik holimpasim na kisim Philippines em ol manmeri long Filipino yet i baim.
Ol i fosim ol long baim takis i go long 'colonial regime' bilong U.S long givim mani i go long ol 'expenditure' na 'interest' long ol 'bond' we ol yusim aninit long nem bilong gavman bilong Philipines insait long ol benk (bank) bilong Wall Street.
Em i tru olsem, ol bikpela win mani we i kamap taim o i bagarapim ol Filipino manmeri em bai kamapim ol win mani bilong U.S long bosim ol narapela hap bilong graun.
Long klia gut long ol Templars yumi mas klia gut long stori i stap baksait we i mekim ol i kamapim dispela grup.
Dispela taim we ol samting i kamap em ol i save kolim olsem High Middle Ages dispela taim insait long histori bilong Europe long 11th, 12th na '13th century' (AD 1000–1300).
Bipo long High Middle Ages i bin gat Early Middle Ages na bihain long en i bin gat Late Middle Ages, dispela taim em i pinis long kain taim olsem 1500.
'Technological determinism' em i wanpela hap tok we i gat planti kainkain tingting we ol manmeri i save prektisim, stat long 'technology push' o 'technological imperative' i go long wanpela tingting we i tok olsem pasin bilong ol manmeri bilong graun em long bihainim ol lo bilong sains na kamapim ol teknoloji we i save bihainim ol dispela lo bilong sains.
Planti bilong ol tingting long mining bilong 'technological determinism' i gat tupela bikpela tingting insait long ol: wanpela em i olsem divelopmen bilong teknoloji i bihainim wanpela rot we kalsa na politiks i no inap long senisim, na narapela em i olsem teknoloji i kamapim "senis" long ol komuniti bikos dispela ol pasin na tingting em ol manmeri i bon wantaim na teknoloji i no kamapim.
Eksampel em, yumi i ken tok olsem kar i mekim na ol manmeri i kamapim ol rot.
Tasol, wanpela rot we i go long olgeta hap bilong kantri em bai i westim mani bikos i gat sampela kar tasol, olsem na ol nupela rot bilong wokim kar i kamap bilong daunim prais bilong kar.
Taim planti manmeri i gat kar, planti eksiden i ken kamap long ol rot, dispela bai i mekim na ol lain bai i kamapim ol nupela teknik insait long heltkea long stretim ol bagarap long bodi.
Romanticicm i bin gat wanpela bikpela hap tingting bilong 'cultural determinism' insait long em, dispela tingting em i kam long 'writer' olsem Goethe, Fichte, na Schlegel.
Long sait bilong Romanticisim, ples we ol man i kam long en i save mekim ol i gat wanpela kain pasin, na bihain long sampela taim ol kastom na ol kalsa we i go wantaim ples we ol i stap long en i save kamap, na ol dispela, bai soim wanem pasin em i pasin bilong ol manmeri long dispela ples, dispela em i gutpela moa long ol lo we ol lain i kisim nating long narapela hap na i kam yusim.
Long dispela rot, Paris i kamap olsem nambawan ples bilong ol kainkain stail bilong klos long dispela graun long tude, tasol Constantinople em i stap olsem nambawan siti bilong kainkain stail klos long taim bilong 'middle ages' long Europe.
Planti lain manmeri i save long em bikos em i asples bilong gutpela laipstail na em i bin stat long 400 A.D na pinis long kain taim olsem 1100 A.D.
Long 'twelfth century', velu (value) bilong em i go daun bikos ol Crusaders i bin kam bek na ol i karim ol presen kain olsem ol silk na spais. Velu bilong ol dispela samting i antap moa long velu bilong ol samting we i stap long ol maket bilong ol Byzantine.
Long dispela taim, ol i kisim dispela nem 'Fashion Capital' long siti Constantinople na givim i go long siti Paris.
Gothic style i kamap bikpela long taim namel long '10th - 11th century' na '14 century'.
Pastaim dispela dres i bihainim stail bilong Byzantine kalsa bilong is.
Tasol, bikos pasin bilong salim toktok i go i kam i save kisim taim, ol stail bilong wes bai stap bihain long 25 i go long 30-pela yia.
taim i go long pinis bilong ol Middle Ages 'western' Europe i stat long kamapim ol stail bilong ol yet. Wanpela bilong ol bikpela divelopmen we i kamap long dispela taim bikos long ol 'crusades' em ol manmeri i stat long yusim ol baten long pasim ol klos.
'Subistence agriculture' em i agrikalsa (agriculture) we ol lain i mekim long kamapim kaikai long mak bilong famili bilong ol.
'Subsistence agriculture' em i wanpela sistem we i no yusim planti samting, i no yusim marasin, i yusim sit we ol i kisim long kaikai we i gro long dispela rijen na ol i bungim dispela ol pasin wantaim pasin bilong mekim 'crop rotation' o ol narapela isipela teknik (technique) bilong mekim kaikai i kamap planti.
Bipo planti fama (farmer) i save mekim 'subsistence agriculture' na dispela pasin em i stap yet long planti kantri we i no divelop yet.
Ol 'subculture' i save mekim ol lain i gat wankain tingting na i pilim olsem ol stendet bilong 'society' i no bilong ol na taim ol i bung wantaim ol i kamapim wanpela 'identity' bilong ol yet.
Ol 'subculture' em ol i ken narakain narakain bikos long krismas, ples ol lain i kam long en, level bilong ol insait long komuniti, ples ol i stap long en, na 'gender' bilong ol.
Ol samting we i mekim ol 'subculture' i narakain narakain em i ken tok ples, samting we i nais, lotu, politiks, 'sexual', ples, o ol dispela samting i bung wantaim.
Ol memba bilong wanpela 'subculture' i ken soim olsem ol i memba bilong em taim ol i yusim wanpela kain stail, kain olsem klos ol i werim, pasin ol i gat long en, na toktok ol i yusim.
Wanpela bilong ol metod (method) we planti lain i save yusim long soim olsem 'socialization' em i impoten em ol i save yusim stori bilong ol pikinini we i bin 'socialized' bikos ol papamama i no bisi long ol, ol samting nogut i kamap long laip bilong ol, o ol lain i mekim nogut long ol taim ol i wok long gro.
Dispela kain ol pikinini em ol i save kolim ol olsem "'feral" o wel pikinini. Sampela 'feral' pikinini em sampela lain (planti taim em i papamam bilong ol yet) i save mekim ol i stap long haus tasol; long sampela taim ol papamama i no bisi long dispela pikinini bikos em i gat samting i rong long het bilong em o long bodi bilong em.
Ol 'feral' pikinini em ol sampela bikpela bagarap o 'trauma' i bin kamap long ol bipo long ol i ranawe o papamama i no bisi long ol.
Ol narapela 'feral' pikinini em ol lain i tok olsem ol animal long bus i lukautim ol; sampela em ol lain i tok olsem ol i stap ol yet long bus.
Taim ol animal i lukautim ol dispela pikinini, ol dispela 'feral' pikinini save soim ol pasin (we ol inap long mek) we i wankain olsem pasin bilong dispela animal we i lukautim ol, kain olsem pret o i no save wanem samting bilong mekim taim em i stap wantaim ol narapela manmeri.
Maski, 'project based learning' i mekim pasin bilong lainim samting i kamap isi moa na i kirapim intres (interest), 'scaffolding' em i mekim moa samting.
'Scaffolding' em i no wanpela metod (method) bilong lainim samting tasol em i wanpela helpim we i save givim sapot long ol wanwan sumatin husat i wok long lainim wanpela nupela samting kain olsem yusim wanpela nupela komputa o statim wanpela nupela projek (project).
Ol 'scaffold' em ol i ken kamap long komputa o em i ken tru insait long klasrum, narapela we bilong tok em i olsem, wanpela tisa em wanpela 'scaffold', tasol wanpela 'paperclip man' insait long Microsoft Office em tu i wanpela 'scaffold'.
Ol 'scaffold' long komputa em ol i stap insait long ol 'software' na wok bilong ol em long askim kwesten, tok save long wanem samting bilong mekim, na tok klia long ol rot bilong mekim samting we i hat long ol sumatin long mekim long save bilong ol yet.
Ol i save putim ol pikinini long Foster Care bikos long kainkain samting na em i ken 'neglect', i go long 'abuse', na pasin bilong fosim pikinini long mekim samting bilong kisim mani.
No gat wanpela pikinini i mas stap insait long wanpela envairomen we i no gutpela long ol, i no lukautim ol, na i givim save long ol, tasol ol i save stap insait long kain envairomen olsem.
Mipela i lukim Foster Care System olsem wanpela ples we i seif long ol dispela pikinini.
'Foster Care System' bilong mipela em i sapos long givim ol ples we i seif long ol pikinini long i stap, lain we i ken laikim ol na lukautim ol, gutpela helt kea (health care).
Ol 'foster care' i sapos long givim olgeta samting we ol i no bin gat long haus we ol i kisim ol long en.
Intanet i save bungim ol pasin bilong toktok long wanwan man o meri wantaim ol pasin bilong toktok long planti manmeri.
Dispela ol pasin bilong intanet i save givim nupela save long wanem we yumi ken yusim ‌intanet na kisim amamas.
Eksampel em, “'learning” and “socialization'” em ol impoten motivesen (motivation) we i save mekim ol manmeri i laik long yusim intanet (James et al., 1995).
“'Personal involvement'” na “'continuing relationship'” em Eighmey and McCord (1998) i bin luksave olsem ol nupela samting we i kirapim bel bilong yumi long yusim intanet taim ol i mekim stadi long pasin bilong ol manmeri long ol websait.
Pasin bilong yusim vidio rekoding i mekim na ol saveman i painimaut long ol impoten samting long sait bilong mining bilong 'micro-expression', ol muvmen bilong pes we i save kamap insait long sampela 'millisecond'.
Bikpela moa, ol i tok olsem yumi i ken painimaut sapos wanpela man o meri i giaman taim yumi painimaut mining bilong 'micro-expression' bilong em long stretpela we.
Oliver Sacks, insait long pepa we em i raitim The President's Speech, em i soim hau olsem manmeri i no inap long klia gut long mining bilong toktok bikos ol i gat sampela bagarap i kamap long brein (brain) bilong ol tasol ol i klia stret sapos man em i tok tru.
Em i tok tu olsem ol dispela kain save bilong man long lukim mining bilong pasin bilong ol man em ol animal tu i gat kain olsem ol dok we yumi save lukautim long haus.
Ol risets i kamap long 'Twentieth century' i bin soim olsem i gat tupela 'pool' bilong 'genetic variation': wanpela em i hait na wanpela em i stap ples klia.
'Mutation' i save mekim nupela 'genetic variation' i kamap, na 'selection' i save rausim em long 'pool' bilong 'expressed variation'.
'Segregation' na 'recombination' i save mekim dispela 'variation' i go i kam namel long tupela 'pool' insait long wanwan 'generation'.
Long 'savaana', em i hat long wanpela 'primate' we i gat wanpela 'digestive system' kain olsem bilong ol man long inapim ol 'amino-acid' long ol plent (plant) i stap long hap.
Na moa yet, sapos ol i no inap long mekim dispela ol bikpela samting i ken kamap: 'growth depression', 'malnutrition', na bikpela tru em i dai.
Dispela plent (plant) we i stap long dispela hap em ol 'protein' i save stap insait long ol lip na ol bin bilong en, tasol dispela em i hat long ol bel bilong ol 'primate' olsem mipela long brukim i go daun na ol i mas kukim ol pastaim.
Narapela samting, em animal kaikai (ol anis, ol 'termite', na kiau) em ol i isi long kaikai, na tu ol i givim bikpela mak bilong ol 'protein' we i gat olgeta ol 'amino acid' we bodi i nidim.
Taim yumi skelim olgeta samting, yumi mas no ken kirap nogut sapos ol tumbuna bilong ol i stretim ol "problem bilong 'protein'" bilong ol long wankain we olsem ol 'chimps' long 'savanna' i save mekim long tude.
'Sleep interruption' em i pasin bilong kirap namel long slip na go bek long slip sotpela taim bihain (10–60 minit).
Dispela em yu ken mekim taim yu yusim wanpela 'quiet alarm clock' long mekim yu i kirap isi isi na i no kirapim yu wantu.
Sapos yu lukim olsem yu mekim 'reset' long kilok namel long slip bilong yu, yu ken putim em long narapela sait bilong rum, dispela em bai mekim yu i kirap long bed long i go ofim em.
Narapela opsen (option) bilong 'biorhythm-based' em bai yu dringim planti wara (kain olsem wara o ti, wanpela 'diuretic') bipo long yu slip, dispela bai fosim yu long kirap na i go pispis.
Mak bilong bel isi i stap insait long wanpela man i gat koneksen (connection) tasol em i oposit (opposite) long mak bilong hevi we i stap insait long bodi na spirit bilong wanpela man.
Taim hevi em i liklik, bai i gat moa positif fos bilong laip i stap. Olgeta man i gat strong long painim bel isi tru na amamas.
Olgeta lain i ken kisim 'enlightenment'. Wanpela samting tasol we i sanap namel long dispela as tingting em hevi na 'negativity' bilong yumi yet.
Tibetan Buddhism em i bihainim ol samting we Buddha i tisim, tasol ol i mekim em i go bikpela moa wantaim 'mahayana path of love' na tu wantaim planti ol teknik (technique) bilong Indian Yoga.
Insait long as tingting bilong em Tibetan Buddhism em i isi tru. Em i gat Kundalini Yoga, 'meditation' and the rot bilong 'all-embracing love'.
Wantaim Kundalini Yoga dispela Kundalini energy ('enlightenment energy') em i save kirap insait long 'yoga postures', eksesais bilong pulim win, ol 'mantra' na 'visualizations'.
Nambawan samting insait long 'Tibetan meditation' em Deity Yoga. Insait long 'visualization' bilong ol kainkain god ol rot bilong eneji i kamap klin, ol 'chakra' i kamap ektif (active) na 'enlightenment' bilong tingting i kamap.
Germany em i stap olsem birua bilong planti lain long World War 2, dispela i mekim na wok bung i kamap namel long USSR na USA. Taim woa i pinis, bam i kamap namel long ol sistem, ol proses (process) na kalsa na dispela i mekim ol kantri i no wok wantaim.
Bihain long tupela yia long pinis bilong woa, ol lain we i bin wok wantaim i kamap olsem ol birua na Cold War i stat.
Dispela woa em bai i stap 40-pela yia na pait i kamap tru tru, long ol ami (army) we i makim ol kantri, long ol ples bilong pait long Africa i go long Asia, long Afghanistan, Cuba na planti narapela ples.
Long September 17, 1939, ol difens (defence) bilong ol Poland em i bruk, na wanpela samting tasol bilong mekim em long go bek na bung gen long 'bridgehead' bilong Romania.
Tasol, ol dispela plen (plan) i bagarap long dispela nait, moa long 800,000 soldia bilong Rrd Army bilong Soviet Union i go insait na i kamapim wanpela 'front' long Belarus na wanpela 'front' long Ukraine bihain long ol i go insait na holimpasim ol 'eastern region' bilong Poland na dispela pasin em i no bihaibim Riga Peace Treaty, Soviet-Polish Non-Aggression Pact, na ol narapela intanesinel agrimen (agreement) we i kamap namel long tupela kantri na tu, i kamap namel long planti narapela kantri.
Pasin bilong yusim sip long muvim ol samting em i nambawan we tru bilong muvim bikpela namba bilong ol kago o ol manmeri long solwara.
Wok bilong ol 'navy' em i bilong lukim olsem kantri bilong yu em i inap long muvin ol kago na manmeri, na tu, stopim ol birua long muvim ol kago na ol manmeri bilong em.
Wanpela gutpela eksampel we i kamap i no longtaim em dispela kempen (campaign) bilong North Altlantic long WWII. Ol America i wok long traim long muvim ol kago na ol man long Atlantic Ocean long helpim ol Britain.
Long wankain taim, 'navy' bilong Germany, i yusim ol U-boat, na i wok long traim long stopim dispela long kamap.
Sapos ol Allies i no mekim samting ol i bin mekim, Germany ating bai holimpasim na kisim Britain olsem em i bin mekim long olgeta hap bilong Europe.
Ol man i stat long lukautim meme long kain taim olsem 10,000 yia i go pinis long Zagros Mountains bilong Iran.
Ol kalsa bilong bipo tru na ol 'tribe' i stat long lukautim ol long mekim isi long kisim milk, gras, mit na skin bilong ol.
Ol meme bilong we ol man i save lukautim em ol i save putim ol long grup we i save raun long ol liklik maunten o ol narapela hap bilong kaikai, planti taim ol 'goatherd' i save was long ol na dispela em ol pikinini ol bikpela man we ol i save kolim olsem 'sheperd'. Ol dispela ol pasin bilong lukautim ol meme em ol i wok long yusim yet long tude.
Ol Wagonways em ol i bin bildim long England taim bipo long '16th Century'.
Maski ol 'wagonways' em ol plang we i stap sait sait long rot, ol i mekim ol hos we i pulim ol long spit moa na i pulim bikpela kago long ol rot we i no raf (rough) moa long mak bilong ol rot we i save stap long dispela de.
Ol i yusim ol 'crossties' pastaim long holim ol dispela 'track' i stap long wanpela ples. Bihain, nau, ol i luksave olsem ol dispela 'track' bai kamap gutpela moa sapos ol i gat wanpela hap ain i stap antap long ol.
Dispela pasin em planti lain i save mekim, tasol em i kamapim 'wear' long plang wil bilong ol 'wagon'.
Bihain, ol i senisim ol plang wil wantaim ain wil. Long 1767, ol i wokim ol namba wan 'full-iron rails'.
Namba wan 'transportation' em wokabaut, ol manmeri i stat long wokabaut long tupela lek tu miline yia i go pinis taim ol Homo Erectus (dispela em i min olsem 'upright man') i kamap.
Ol lain i stap pastaim, ol Australopithecus i no wokabut long tupela lek olgeta taim.
Pasin bilong wokabaut long tupela lek em ol i painim long fosil (fossil) bilong ol Australopithecus we i bin stap 4.2-3.9 milien yia i go pinis, tasol ol Sahelanthropus i bin wokabaut long tupela lek long kain taim olsem seven milien yia i go pinis.
Yumi ken stat long stap gut wantaim envairomen, yumi ken joinim wanpela 'environmental movement', na yumi ken kamap olsem 'activist' long daunim mak bilong hevi we i ken kamap long bihaintaim.
Planti taim dispela em i wankain olsem 'sympomatic treatment'. Tasol, sapos yumi i no laikim wanpela sotpela ansa, orait yumi mas painim as bilong problem, na yumi mas stopim ol.
Em i is long lukim olsem graun i senis tru bikos long ol nupela save bilong sains (science) na teknoloji (technology), na ol problem i wok long kamap bikpela bikos long planti manmeri na laipstail bilong manmeri long i gat ol kainkain bikpela samting.
Bihain long Congress i kisim dispela pepa long Julai 4, wanpela kopi we ol i raitim long han na President of Congress John Hancock na Secretary Charles Thomson tupela i sainim, ol i salim i go long wanpela 'printing shop' bilong John Dunlop we i stap klostu.
Namel long nait kain olsem 150 na 200 kopi em ol i mekim, nau ol i kolim olsem "Dunlap broadsides".
Namba wan taim ol i ritim dispela dokumen long pablik em John Nixon i ritim autsait long Independence Hall long Julai 8.
Wanpela em ol i salim i go long George Washington long Julai 6, na em i ritim long ol soldia bilong em long New York long Julai 9. Wanpela kopi i kamap long London long Ogas 10.
25-pela Dunlop broadies em ol i stap yet na ol i olpela kopi tru bilong dispela dokumen. Dispela namba wan dokumen we ol i raitim long han em i bagarap.
Planti bilong ol 'paleontologists' tude i bilip olsem wanpela grup bilong ol dainaso i stap laip yet long tude. Mipela i save kolim ol olsem pisin.
Planti manmeri i no ting olsem ol i wankain olsem ol dainaso bikos ol i gat 'feather' na ol i ken flai.
Tasol i gat planti samting long ol pisin we i luk wankain olsem ol dainaso yet.
Ol i gat lek we i gat 'scale' na 'claws', ol i save putim kiau, na ol i save wokabaut long tupela lek olsem wanpela T-Rex.
Klostu olgeta komputa we ol i yusim long tude em ol i save senisim infomesen i stap long 'code' bilong ol 'binary number'.
Wanpela 'binary number' em i ken i gat tupela velu (value), dispela em i 0 o 1, na ol dispela namba em ol i save kolim olsem ol 'binary digit' - o 'bits' long toktok bilong komputa.
'Internal poisoning' em i no inap long kamap ples klia hariap. Ol sain, kain olsem traut em ol bikpela sain taim ol lain i no inap long mekim wanpela 'diagnosis' hariap.
Ol nambawan samting we i soim olsem 'internal poisoning' i kamap em wanpela kontena bilong marasin o 'toxic chemical' bilong haus i op na i stap.
Sekim 'label' long ol 'first aid instruction' bilong dipela posin.
Dispela hap tok 'bug' em ol entomolojist (entomologist) i save yusim long toktok long dispela grup bilong ol binatang.
Dispela hap tok i kisim mining bilong em long Bed-bugs, ol dispela binatang we i save parasait long ol manmeri.
Ol Assasin-bugs na ol Bed-bugs em ol i 'nidiocolous', ol i save stap long ples we ol i bon long en o long samting we i save givim ol kaikai.
Long kainkain hap bilong United States of America, i gat kain olsem 400,000 'case' bilong Multiple Sclerosis (MS), mekim em i kamap olsem nambawan 'neurological disease' insait long ol bikpela manmeri.
MS em i wanpela sik we i save kamap long 'central nervous system', dispela sistem em brein (brain), 'spinal cord' na 'optic nerve' i kamapim.
Risets i bin painimaut olsem sans bilong ol meri long kisim MS em i tupela taim moa long ol man.
Wanpela marit i ken mekim disisen olsem em i no gutpela long ol, ol em i no gutpela long pikinini bilong ol, sapos ol i gat wanpela bebi.
Ol dispela kain marit i ken mekim disisen long putim bebi bilong ol i go long 'adoption'.
Insait long wanpela 'adoption', ol papamama we i kamapim dispela pikinini bai stopim 'right' bilong olsem ol papamama na narapela marit i ken lukautim dispela pikinini.
As tingting bilong sains (science) em long painimaut wanem we dispela graun i wok taim ol yusim ol 'scientific method'. Dispela metod (method) i save stiaim planti bilong ol 'scientific research'.
Em i no i stap em yet, 'experimentation', na wanpela 'experiment' em i wanpela 'test' ol save yusim long rausim wanpela o moa bilong ol tingting we ol i bin kamapim, pasin bilong askim ol kwesten, na mekim stadi tu i save givim stia long 'scientific research'.
Ol lain i save stadi long 'nature' na ol 'philosophy' i save lukluk long ol 'classical texts', kain olsem, Bible long tok ples Latin.
Ol samting we ol i tok orait long en em ol tingting bilong Aristotle long sains (science), wantaim saikoloji (psychology).
Taim save bilong ol Greek i go daun, West i lusim ol tingting bilong Greek long sains (science) na filosofi (philosophy).
Planti savemanmeri i lukim olsem ol 'rhythm' we i kamap long bodi na pasin bilong ol animal na manmeri i save bihainim ol 'cycle' bilong ol samting we i stap autsait long bodi na ol 'biological clock' bilong bodi.
Ol 'periodic rhythms', em ol i no kamap bikos long ol samting we i stap autsait tasol, dispela em ol lain i bin stadi na lukim olsem em i kamap long planti ol samting we i gat laip, wantaim ol 'bacteria', 'fungi', plent (plant) na animal.
Ol 'biological clock' em ol samting we i save mentenim ol yet na i save kamap ol 'electric currents' na ol i save kontinu (continue) long ron maski ol samting long autsait we i save mekim ol i ron i no stap.
'Experiment' bilong Hershey and Chase em i wanpela bilong ol samting we i tok olsem DNA em i wanpela 'genetic material'.
Hershey na Chase i bin yusim 'phages', o ol vaires (virus), long putim DNA bilong ol yet i go insait long wanpela 'bacterium'.
Ol i mekim tupela 'experiment' we tupela i makim DNA insait long 'phage' wantaim wanpela 'radioactive phosphorus' o tupela i makim 'protein' bilong 'phage' wantaim 'radioactive sulfur'.
Ol 'mutation' i ken kamapim kainkain samting na ol i save kamap bikos long wanem kain 'mutation', impoten wok bilong dispela hap 'genetic material' na sapos dispela ol 'cell' em ol 'germ-line cell'.
Ol 'mutation' we i kamap insait long ol 'germ-line cell' tasol em ol i ken i go long ol pikinini, tasol ol 'mutation' we i kamap long narapela hap i ken kamapim 'cell-death' o kensa.
'Nature-based tourism' em i save pulim ol manmeri we i intres long lukim ol eria bilong 'nature' na amamas long lukim ol ples, wantaim ol plent (plent) na animal bilong dispela eria.
Eksampel bilong ol 'on-site activity' em painim pis, kisim foto, lukim ol pisin, na raun long ol 'park' na stadim infomesen long 'ecosystem'.
Wanpela eksampel em raun, kisim foto, na kisim save long ol 'orangatuang' taim yu go long Borneo.
Olgeta moning. ol manmeri i save lusim liklik kantri taun taim ol i kalap long kar long go long ol ples bilong ol long wok na ol i save abrus ol narapela lain we ples bilong ol long wok i stap long ples we ol i lusim nau tasol na i kam.
Insait long dispela 'transport shuttle' olgeta lain i konek wantaim, na ol i sapotim wanpela 'transport system' we ol 'private car' i kamapim.
Nau sains (science) i soim olsem dispela traipela 'carbon economy' em i rausim 'biosphere' long wanpela 'stable state' we i bin sapotim ol manmeri long tupela milien yia i go pinis.
Olgeta manmeri i save stap insait long sosaiti (society) na yusim 'transportation system'. Klostu olgeta lain i save komplen long ol 'transportation system'.
Long ol 'developed country' yu bai no inap long harim wankain mak bilong komplen long kwaliti bilong wara ol bris i pundaun.
Bilong wanem na ol 'transportation system' i save kamapim ol dispela kain komplen, bilong wanem na ol i no save wok gut long olgeta de? Ol 'transportation engineer' i no save long mekim wok bilong ol? O, i gat samting we i bikpela moa i wok long kamap?
'Traffic Flow' em i stadi bilong muvmen (movement) bilong wanwan draiva na kara namel long tupela poin na wanem kain samting ol i save mekim long wanpela narapela.
Tasol, stadi bilong 'traffic flow' em i hat bikos pasin bilong draiva em wanpela i no inap long tok wanem samting bai i kamap long mak we wan handret pesen (percent) korek.
Tasol, ol draiva i save mekim pasin long mak we i 'consistent', olsem na, ol 'traffic' i save i gat sampela samting i 'consistent' long ol na dispela em ol savemanmeri i ken soim wantaim ol namba bilong 'mathematics'.
Long mekim 'traffic flow' i kamap gutpela moa, ol rilesensip i mas kamap namel long tripela bikpela samting: (1) 'flow', (2) 'density', and (3) 'velocity'.
Ol dispela rilesensip i save helpim long mekim 'planning', 'design', na 'operation' bilong ol 'roadway facilities'.
Ol insek em ol namba wan animal long stap long win. Dispela pasin bilong ol long flai i helpim ol long abrusim ol birua bilong ol na painim kaikai na pren bilong ol isi tru.
Planti ol insek i ken foldim wing bilong ol i kam pas wantaim bodi bilong ol na dispela em i gutpela samting.
Dispela i mekim na ol i gat planti liklik ples bilong hait long ol animal we i laik kaikaim ol.
Tude, ol insek (insect) we i no save foldim wing bilong ol em ol 'dragon flies' na ol 'mayflies'.
Sampela tausen yia i go pinis, wanpela man nem bilong em Aristarchus i tok olsem Solar System i save muv raunim Sun.
Ol sampela manmeri i ting olsem em i tok stret, tasol planti manmeri i bilim long oposit (opposite); ol i bilip olsem Solar System i save muv raunim Earth, wantaim Sun (na ol narapela sta tu).
Dispela em i luk olsem i stret, bikos yumi no save pilim olsem Earth i muv, a?
Amazon River em i namba tu longpela wara na namba wan bikpela wara long Earth. Em i karim wara we mak bilong em i 8-pela taim moa long namba tu bikpela wara.
Na tu, Amazon em namba wan wara we namel bilong em i bikpela tru long Earth, na mak bilong namel bilong en em i sikspela 'mile'.
20 pesen (percent) bilong wara we i save kamaut long ol wara bilong plenet (planet) i save kam long Amazon.
Bikpela Amazon River em i 6,387 km (3,980 miles). Em i save kolektim ol wara i kam long planti tausen liklik wara.
Maski ol pasin bilong mekim 'pyramid-bilding' long ston em i kontinu (continue) i go inap long pinis bilong Old Kingdom, ol i no winim sais na save bilong ol lain i wokim ol 'pyramid' bilong Giza.
Ol lain Egypt bilong New Kingdom i tingting olsem ol dispela bilding bilong ol tumbuna bilong ol em i narakain tru, long dispela taim ol dispela 'pyramid' i gat moa long tausen krismas.
Populesen (population) bilong Vatican City em i kain olsem 800. Dispela em nambawan liklik kantri tru insait long wol na kantri we i gat liklik populesen tru.
Vatican City i save yusim tok ples Italian insait long ol lo bilong em na long mekim ol 'official communication'.
Tok ples Italian em ol lain i save wok insait long steit (state) i save yusim tu long toktok long olgeta de na ol i save yusim Latin long mekim ol seremoni (ceremony) bilong lotu.
Olgeta sitisen (citizen) bilong Vatican City em ol i Roman Catholic.
Ol manmeri i bin save long ol bikpela kemikel elemen (chemical element) kain olsem gol, silva, na kopa (copper) long bipo taim, bikos ol i bin painim ol insait long envairomen long 'native form' na em i isi long painim ol wantaim ol tul (tool) bilong bipo.
Aristotle, wanpela filosofa (philosopher), i kamapim tingting olsem olgeta samting i kamap long ol wanpela o moa bilong ol foapela elemen (elements) i miks wantaim. Ol dispela elemen em graun, wara, win, na paia.
Dispela em i wankain olsem foapela 'states of matter' (na i bihainim wankain oda): strong, wara, ges (gas), na 'plasma', em i tok tu olsem ol i senis na kamapim nupela samting long mekim ol samting we yumi i lukim.
Ol 'alloy'em ol samting we i gat tupela o moa metel (metal) insait long en. No ken lus tingting olsem i gat planti elemen (element) insait long 'periodic table'.
Ol elemen (element) kain olsem 'calcium' na 'potassium' em ol i save lukim ol olsem ol metel (metal). I gat ol narapela metel tu olsem silva na gol.
Yu ken i gat ol 'alloy' we i gat ol liklik mak bilong ol elemen (element) we i no metel (metal) kain olsem 'carbon' insait long ol.
Olgeta samting insait long Universe em ol i kamap long 'matter'. Olgeta 'matter' i gat ol liklik samting insait long ol we ol i kolim 'atom'.
Ol 'atom' em ol i liklik liklik tru na trilien (trillion) bilong ol bai i inap long fit i go inap long wanpela 'full stop' long pinis bilong wanpela sentens (sentence).
Olsem na, pensil (pencil) em i bin wanpela gutpela pren bilong planti manmeri taim em i bin kamap.
Tasol, taim ol nupela rot bilong rait i kamap, pensil (pencil) i kisim wanpela posisen we i daunbilo na i no gat planti i yusim em.
Nau ol manmeri i save raitim ol tok save long ol komputa skrin (computer screen), na ol i no kam klostu long wanpela sapena (sharpener).
Yumi ken tingting long wanem samting bai i kamap long ol kibod (keyboard) taim wanpela nupela samting i kamap.
'Fission bomb' em i save wok bihainim lo we i save kisim eneji na kamapim wanpela 'nucleus' wantaim planti 'protons' na 'neutrons'.
Wankain liklik olsem yu wok long pusim wanpela hevipela samting i go antap long wanpela liklik maunten. Pasin bilong 'splitting nucleus' gen i save lusim sampela bilong ol dispela eneji.
Sampela 'atom' i gat 'unstable nuclei' na dispela em i min olsem ol i save bruk taim yu tasim liklik o i no tasim.
Antap bilong Moon em i gat ol ston na das (dust). 'Outer layer' bilong Moon em ol i kolim 'crust'.
'Crust' bilong em i kain olsem 70 km 'thick' long sait i stap klostu na 100 km 'thick' long sait i stap longwe.
Em i 'thin' moa aninit long 'maria' na 'thick' moa aninit long 'highlands'.
I luk olsem bai i gat moa 'maria' long sait i stap klostu bikos 'crust' em i 'thin' moa. Em i isi moa long 'lava' long kam antap long autsait.
Ol 'content theories' i save lukluk long painimaut wanem ol samting i save kirapim bel bilong ol manmeri o i tasim bel na tingting bilong ol.
Ol dispela 'theory' i tok olsem ol manmeri i gat sampela samting ol i nidim na laikim we i stap insait long ol taim ol i kamap bikpela.
Ol dispela 'theory' i save lukluk long wanem samting insait long sampela manmeri i save mekim ol i laikim ol samting we ol i mekim na wanem ol samting insait long envairomen (environment) bai wokim na ol i mekim wanpela samting o i no mekim wanpela samting.
Tupela 'content theory' we planti lain i save long en em Hierarchy of Needs Theory na Hertzberg's Two Factor Theory.
Sapos yumi skelim olgeta samting, tupela pasin i kamap ples klia taim ol meneja i stat long go pas long ol wanlain bilong ol. Long wanpela sait em ol i laik stap olsem “wanpela bilong ol mangi long grup” (meri long grup).
Dispela kain meneja em i save painim hat long mekim ol disisen we ol lain i no laikim, givim mekim save long ol lain i brukim lo, sekim wok pefomens (performance) bilong ol wokmanmeri, givim wok long ol wokmanmeri, na tokaut stret long ol wokmanmeri olsem ol i mekim rong.
Long narapela sait, wanpela meneja i senis i go na kamap olsem wanpela man o meri we ol lain i bo save long em na em i pilim olsem em i mas senisim olgeta samting we tim i wok long mekim na mekim olgeta samting long strong bilong ol yet.
Bihain long olgeta samting, em i wok bilong lida long mekim tim i mekim gut wok o i no mekim gut wok.
Dispela pasin i save mekim hevi i kamap namel long ol lida na ol tim.
Ol tim we i save wok wantaim long komputa i ken i gat ol wankain stendet bilong mekim gut wok wankain olsem ol tim we i save wok wantaim long ofis, tasol i gat sampela liklik samting i narakain.
Ol tim we i save wok wantaim long komputa i save wok stap olsem man o meri we i save bungim ol grup we i wok wantaim long ofis.
Ol i ken mekim samting long laik bilong ol moa long ol tim we i save wok insait long ofis taim ol bung wantaim ol narapela tim memba long taim we i gutpela long ol kainkain 'time zone' na dispela em ol lokel meneja i no inap long klia long en.
Wanpela trupela “'invisible team'” (Larson and LaFasto, 1989, p109) em i wanpela narakain samting i stap insait long ol tim we i save wok wantaim long komputa.
Dispela “'invisible team'” em i wanpela 'management team' we wanwan memba bilong tim i save ripot i go long en. Dispela 'invisible team' i save makim stendet bilong wanwan memba long bihainim.
Wai na wanpela oganaisesen bai laik long mekim wok we i save kisim planti taim? Dispela em wok bilong kamapim wanpela oganaisesen we i save lainim samting. Wanpela bilong ol as tingting bilong mekim 'organizational learning' i kamap insait long oganaisesen em pasin bilong 'innovation'.
Taim ol dipatmen bilong wanpela oganaisesen i yusim gut olgeta risos, 'creativity' na 'ingenuity' i ken kamap.
Bikos long dispela, proses (process) bilong wanpela oganaisesen long wok wantaim na daunim wanpela hatpela samting i ken kamap ol nupela narapela kain proses bilong inapim nid bilong kastoma.
Bipo long wanpela oganaisesen i ken i gat ol nupela na narapela kain we bilong mekim samting, ol lida i mas kamapim wanpela kalsa bilong kamapim ol nupela na narapela kain samting na tu, i mas i gat pasin bilong serim save na lainim samting wantaim.
Angel (2006), i tok klia long Continuum approach olsem wanpela metod (method) we ol i yusim long helpim oganaisesen i kamap long mak we i antap moa long sait bilong pefomen (performance).
Neurobiological infomesen i givim evidens (evidence) long wanpela 'theoretical approach' long investigesen bilong 'cognition'. Olsem na em i mekim eria bilong risets i kamap liklik moa na mekim em i kamap long 'exact'.
Rilesensip namel long 'brain pathology' na pasin i sapotim ol saintis insait long risets bilong ol.
Ol i save long longpela taim pinis olsem ol kainkain bagarap i kamap long brein (brain), ol 'trauma', ol 'lesion', na ol 'tumour' i ken mekim pasin i senis na kamapim senis long tingting.
Dispela ol nupela teknoloji we i kamap i helpim mipela long lukim na mekim investigesen long ol straksa (structure) na proses (process) bilong brein (brain) we mipela i no bin lukim bipo.
Dispela i save givim mipela nupela infomesen na meteriel long kamapim ol 'simulation model' we i ken helpim yumi long klia gut long ol proses (process) we i save kamap insait long tingting bilong mipela.
Maski AI em i mekim ol lain i tingim 'science fiction', AI em i kamapim wanpela impoten eria insait long 'computer science', em i save mekim wok long sait bilong pasin, lainim samting, mekim senis insait long wanpela masin.
Risets insait long AI em i wok bilong mekim masin i mekim ol wok we i save kamap olgeta taim na i nidim save bilong wanpela wok long mekim disisen.
Eksampel em kontrolim samting, plenim na makim taim bilong samting, save bilong ansarim ol kwesten bilong kastoma, na luksave long 'handwriting', vois na pes.
Dispela kain ol samting i gat wanwan eria bilong stadi bilong ol yet, na i lukluk long ol rot bilong givim ol ansa long ol problem we i save kamap long olgeta de.
Nau ol i save yusim dispela AI sistem insait long ol eria bilong 'economics', 'medecine', 'engineering' na 'military', na ol i bin yusim em long bildim sampela komputa bilong haus na 'video game software applications'.
Ol 'field trip' em ol i impoten pat bilong ol klasrum. Planti taim tisa i save laik long kisim ol sumatin bilong em i go long ol ples we ol i no inap long kalap long bas (bus) na i go.
Teknoloji (technology) i givim ansa wantaim 'field trip' we i kamap long komputa. Ol sumating i ken lukluk long ol 'museum artifact', lukim wanpela 'aquarium', ol lukluk long wanpela naispela 'art' taim ol i sindaun insait long klas.
Pasin bilong serim wanpela 'field trip' long komputa em i wanpela gutpela we tu long tingting lon wanpela raun na serim ol samting i bin kamap wantaim klas bilong bihaintaim.
Eksampel, long wanwan yia ol sumatin long Bennet School long North Carolina i save disainim wanpela websait long raun bilong ol i go long State Capital, na long wanwan yia dispela websait i kisim nupela stail, tasol ol olpela 'version' i save stap yet 'online' olsem wanpela 'scrapebook'.
Ol blog i ken kisim helpim sumatin long rait gut. Planti taim ol sumatin i statim blog bilong ol wantaim 'grammar' na 'spelling' we i no gutpela, na taim i gat lain bai i ritim ol bai i senis na i rait gut moa.
Bikos ol sumatin em ol i save mekim planti toktok sapos samting i no stret, dispela sumatin we i raitim blog bai i stat long rait gut long abrusim ol toktok we i tok olsem em no rait gut.
Na tu, 'blogging' "i save fosim ol sumatin long save moa long ol samting we i wok long kamap long komuniti we ol i stap long en." Dispela nid long inapim nid bilong ol lain i ritim blog bilong ol i mekim na ol sumatin i gat moa save na kamap 'interesting' (Toto, 2004).
'Blogging' em i wanpela tul (tool) we i save mekim ol lain i wok wantaim, na i strongim ol sumating long surikim samting ol i lainim i go autsait moa long wanem samting ol i save lainim long wanpela de insait long skul.
Yusim ol blog long gutpela na stretpela we "i ken mekim ol sumatin i ken skelim ol samting na save long wanem samting i no stret na wanem we bilong stret; taim ol wok wantaim ol meteriel long Internet, ol sumatin i ken save long wanem mak ol i stap long en taim ol skelim samting we ol narapela i raitim na tu ol i ken givim tingting bilong ol long ol samting we i wok long kamap (Oravec, 2002).
Ottawa em i kapitol bilong Canada we ol lain i save yusim tupela tok ples na em i gat ol 'art gallery' na 'museum' we i soim taim bipo na taim bilong tude long Canada.
Longwe long saut em Niagara Fall na long not em Musoka, wanplea ples we i luk nais na i gat ol narapela ples moa i stap.
Ol lain long autsait i tok olsem olgeta dispela samting na sampela moa i soim Ontario olsem em i ples we i soim tru tru kala bilong Canada.
Ol bikpela eria longwe long not em i no gat planti manmeri na sampela ples we i no gat manmeri long en.
Wanpela samting bilong skelim insait long populesen we i mekim planti lain i kirap nogut: I gat moa African American i stap long US winim namba bilong olgeta sitisen (citizen) bilong Canada.
Eastern African Islanders em ol i stap long Indian Ocean autsait long 'eastern coast' bilong Africa.
Madagascar em i wanpela bikpela tru, na em i kain olsem wanpela kontinen (continent) bilong em, taim yumi lukluk long sait bilong 'wildlife'.
Planti bilong ol liklik ailan em ol i stap olsem ol indipenden (independent) kantri, o ol i save stap olsem hap bilong France, na ol i save stap olsem ol 'luxury beach resort'.
Na tu, ol Arab i bin kisim Islam i kam long ol dispela hap, na ol i kamap olsem bikpela lotu insait long Comoros na Mayotte.
Pasin na tingting bilong ol lain long Europe na 'colonialism' i stat long '15th century', taim eksplora (explorer) bilong Portugal Vasco de Gama i painim Cape Route taim em i stap long Europe na i go long India.
Long hap not bilong rijen em Sahel i raunim, na long hap na hap wes Atlantic Ocean i raunim.
Ol meri: Em i gutpela olsem ol meri i we i go long hap i mas tok olsem ol i marit, maski ol i no marit tru tru.
Em i gutpela long werim wanpela ring (no ken werim ring we i luk ekspensif).
Ol meri i mas luksave olsem pasin bilong narapela kalsa i ken mekim na samting we ol i ting olsem haresmen (harassment) i ken kamap na planti taim ol lain ken bihaim yu, holim han bilong yu na kain olsem.
Yu mas strong na tok nogat long ol man, no ken pret long sanap strong na toktok (pasin em i pasin bilong dispela ples, em i no orait long ol i mekim olsem!).
Siti bilong Casablanca long tude em ol man Berber we i save painim pis i kamapim long '10th century' BCE, na ol Phoenicians, Romans, na Merenid i bin yusim olsem wanpela impoten port we ol i kolim Anfa.
Ol Portuguese i bin bagarapim em na bildim em gen aninit long nem Casa Branca, tasol ol i lusim dispela ples bihain long wanpela guria i kamap long 1755.
Ol 'sultan' bilong Morocco i bildim dispela siti gen olsem Daru l-Badya na ol treida (trader) bilong Spain i kolim em olsem Casablanca taim ol i mekim ol senta bilong ol long hap.
Insait long olgeta hap bilong Casablanca em i wanpela bilong ol ples we i no gat gutpela hap bilong baim ol samting.
Long olpela Medina em i isi long painim ol ples we i save salim ol samting bilong ol Morocco, kain olsem 'tagine', 'pottery', 'leather goods', 'hookahs', na ol kainkain 'geegaws', tasol olgeta dispela samting em i bilong ol turis long baim.
Goma em i wanpela siti we ol turis i save laik i go long en insait long Democratic Republic of Congo long hap ist klostu long kantri Rwanda.
Long yia 2002, hotpela paia bilong volkeno Nyiragongo i bin bagarapim Goma na karamapim planti bilong ol rot bilong dispela taun, dispela i kamap bikpela tru long namel bilong taun.
Maski Goma em seif liklik, ol turis we i go lukim ol ples autsait long Goma i mas painimaut na save gut long wanem kain pait i wok long kamap long North Kivu provins.
Dispela siti em i ples bilong i stap long en na klaimim Nyiragongo volkeno wantaim ol lain bilong painim Moutain Gorilla. Prais bilong ol dispela lain bilong painim gorila i orait moa long ol narapela insait long Africa.
Yu ken yusim boda-boda (motobaik teksi) long raun insait long Goma. Lokel prais bilong dispela em i ~500 Congolese Francs long ron long sotpela hap.
Narapela samting tu em i olsem, "Timbuktu" em i hat long go long en na ol i save yusim dispela nem olsem tok piksa bilong ol samting i narapela kain, i stap long longwe ples.
Tude, Timbuktu em i wanpela taun we i no gat planti samting, maski em i gat gutpela nem we i save pulim ol turis, na em i gat wanpela eapot.
Long 1990, ol i putim em i go long lista bilong 'world heritage sites' we i stap long mak nogut, bikos long bagarap i kamap long ol wesan bilong em long deset (desert).
Em i bin wanpela ples we PBS progrem bilong Henry Louis Gates' Wonders of the African World i mekim wanpela bikpela stop na lukluk long en.
Dispela siti em i narapela kain long olgeta narapela siti bilong kantri, bikos em i luk moa olsem ples bilong Arab na i no olsem ples bilong Africa.
Kruger National Park (KNP) i stap long hap 'north-east' bilong South Africa na i ran arere long bod bilong Mozambique long is, Zimbabwe long not, na boda long hap saut em Crocodile River.
Dispela park i karamapim 19,500 km² na em i bruk i go long 14-pela 'ecozone', wanwan bilong ol i sapotim narakain narakain 'wildlfie'.
Em i wanpela bilong ol bikpela samting we i save pulim ol turis i go long South Africa na ol i save lukim em olsem impoten samting insait long South African National Parks (SANParks).
Wankain olsem olgeta South African National Parks, i gat 'conservation' na 'entry fee' bilong wanwan de long ol park.
Em i gutpela long wanpela long baim wanpela Wild Card, we i save givim tok orait long i go insait long ol park insait long South Africa o olgeta South African National Parks.
Hong Kong Island i givim teritori (territory) bilong Hong Kong nem bilong na em i ples we planti turis i save go long en.
Ol lain bilding we i karamapim skai bilong Hong Kong em ol i bin tok olsem em i wankain olsem wanpela 'bar chart' we i sain sain na dispela sains sain em ol wara bilong Victoria i kamapim.
Long kisim ol gutpela hap bilong lukim Hong Kong, lusim ailan na go long fran bilong wara long Kowloon long hapsait.
Bikpela lain namba bilong ol divelopmen long Hong Kong Island i paspas na i stap long nambis long hap not ol graun we ol i bin kisim bek.
Dispela em i ples we ol 'coloniser' bilong British i bin kisim olsem bilong ol olsem na sapos yu laik lukim ol samting we i soim sain bilong ol 'coloniser' long bipo, dispela em i gutpela ples long stat.
Ol Sundarbans em ol nambawan bikpela 'littoral mangrove belt' long olgeta hap bilong graun, sais bilong ol em i 80 km (50 mi) i go insait long Bangladeshi na ples i stap insait tru long India longwe long nambis.
Ol i bin tokaut olsem ol Sundarbans em i wanpela UNESCO World Heritage Site. Dispela hap bilong bikbus em i stap insait long teritori (territory) bilong India we ol i kolim Sundarbans National Park.
Ol dispela bikbus em ol i no mangro na ples tais tasol — ol i gat sampela bilong laspela bikpela bikbus we i bin karamapim Gangetic plain.
Ol Sundarbans i karamapim wanpela eria mak bilong 3,850 km², na 'one-thrid' bilong en em wara/ples tais i karamapim.
Long 1966 Sundarban em i bin stap olsem ples bilong ol animal, na ol i estimetim olsem i gat 400 Royal Bengal taiga na kain olsem 30,000 'spotted deer' long dispela eria.
Ol bas (bus) i save lusim 'inter-district bus station' (we i stap long narapela sait bilong wara) long de taim, maski planti, bilong ol we i go long is na Jakar/Bumthang i save lusim stesin long namel long 06:30 na 07:30.
Bikos ol 'inter-district' bas (bus) i save pulap, em i gutpela long baim wanpela tiket sampela de bipo long taim bilong kalap long bas.
Planti ol distrik em planti ol Japanese Coaster Buses i save ron long en, na yu bai sindaun gut.
Teksi bilong serim wantaim narapela pasindia em i gutpela rot bilong sindaun gut na i go i kam hariap long ol ples i stap klostu, kain olsem Paro (Nu 150) na Punakha (Nu 200).
Oyapock River Bridge em i wanpelad 'cable-stayed bridge'. Em i stap long Oyapock River na konektim ol siti bilong Oiapoque insait long Brazil na Saint-Georges de l'Oyapock insait long French Guiana.
Tupela taua i kirap long mak bilong 83 mita, longpela bilong tupela em 378 mita na tupela i gat tupela 'lane' we i op olsem 3.50 m.
Dispela 'vertical clearance' aninit long bris em i 15 mita. Konstraksen (construction) i bin pinis long Ogas 2011, em i no op long ol kar i ron i go inap long Mas 2017.
Dispela bris em ol i makim taim bilong em long op long Septemba 2017, taim ol i pinisim ol 'customs checkpoints' bilong ol Brazil.
Ol Gurani em ol impoten as ples manmeri we i stap nau long ples we ol i kolim Eastern Paraguay, na ol i save raun na pasinim abus na tu, ol i save planim kaikai long gaden.
Chaco rijen i gat ol narapela grup bilong ol asples manmeri kain olsem ol Guaycurú na Payaguá, husat i save painim abus, pis na bungim ol kaikai ol i painim long bus.
Long '16th century' Paraguay, we ol i bin kolim "The Giant Province of the Indies", i bin kamap taim ol lain Spain i kam bosim ol asples lain.
Ol lain long Spain i stat long bosim dispela hap long mak bilong tripela 'century'.
Stat long taim ol i kamapim Asunción long 1537, Paraguay i bin larim planti bilong ol pasin na kalsa bilong ol asples grup i stap yet.
Planti lain i save long Argentina olsem em i gat wanpela bilong ol nambawan 'polo team' na ol 'polo player' long olgeta hap bilong graun.
Ol bikpela tonamen (tournament) bilong yia i save kamap long Disemba long ol 'polo fields' long Las Cañitas.
Ol liklik tonamen (tournament) na geim (game) em lain i ken lukim long hia tu long foapela taim long wanpela yia.
Long nius long ol tonamen (tournament) na wanem hap bilong baim tiket long ol polo geim (game), sekim Asociacion Argentina de Polo.
Karensi (currancy) bilong Falkland em Falkland pound (FKP) we velu bilong em i wankain olsem wanpela British pound (GBP).
Yu ken senisim mani long wanpela benk (bank) tasol insait long dispela ailan na em i stap long Stanley long narapela sait bilong FIC West store.
Yu ken yusim ol British pound long olgeta hap bilong ailan na insait long ol Stanley credit cards na tu ol yu ken yusim United States dollar.
Long ol ailan i stap autsait em ol i no inap long yusim ol 'credit cards', maski ol i ken kisim karensi (currency) bilong Britain na United States; sekim ol papa o mama bilongol stua long save wanem em ol rot bilong yusim long baim samting.
Em i klostu long hat olgeta long senisim karensi (currency) bilong Falkland autsait long ol ailan, olsem na yu mas senisim mani bipo long yu lusim dispela ailan.
Bikos Montevideo i stap saut long Equator, em i save sama (summer) long hap taim em i winta (winter) long Northern Hemisphere na bihain em i save senis gen.
Montevideo em i stap insait long 'subtropic'; insait long ol mun bilong sama (summer), tempritsa (temperature) bilong em i save stap antap long +30°C.
Long taim bilong winta (winter) ples i ken kol nogut tru: ol tempritsa (temperature) i no save go daun aninit long mak we ais i save kamap, tasol i win na wara i stap long win i save bung wantaim long mekim ples i pilim kol moa long wanem samting 'thermometer' i tok.
I no gat wanpela "taim bilong ren" na "taim bilong san": mak bilong ren i save stap klostu wankain mak long olgeta yia.
Maski planti bilong ol animal insait long park i save long lukim ol manmeri, dispela em ol wel animal na ol lain i no ken givim kaikai long ol o distebim ol.
Ol atoriti bilong park i tok olsem, ol lain i mas i stap 100yard/meter o moa longwe long ol bea na ol wulf na 25 yard/meter longwe long ol narapela wel animal!
Maski ol i luk olsem ol i stap isi, ol 'bison', 'elk', 'moose', bea, na klostu olgeta bikpela animal i ken pait.
Long olgeta yia, planti visita i save kisim bagarap long bodi bikos ol i no i stap longwe gut. Ol dispela animal i bikpela, wel, na i ken kamapim birua, olsem na givim ol spes bilong ol.
Na tu, lukaut long ol smel we i save pulim ol bea na ol narapela animal, olsem na no ken karim o kukim kaikai we i gat strongpela smel na mekim kem i stap klin.
Apia em i kapitol bilong Samoa. Dispela taun i stap long ailan bilong Upolu na i gat populese we i aninit long 40,000.
Apia em ol i bin kamapim em long 1850s na em i bin nambawan kapitol bilong Samoa stat long 1959 i kam inap nau.
Dispela 'habor' em i ples we bikpela pait i bin kamap long 1889 taim sevenpela sip bilong Germany, US, na Britain i les long lusim dispela 'habor'.
Olgeta sip em ol i bin sinlk, tasol wanpela 'British cruiser' i no sink. Klostu 200-pela laip bilong ol America na Germany i bin lus.
Long pait bilong kisim indipendens (independence) we Mau muvmen (movement) i bin oganaisim, wanpela bung i bin kamap long taun na namel long dispela ''paramount chief' Tupua Tamasese Lealofi III i bin dai.
I gat planti nambis, bikos Auckland i gat tupela basis i stap sait sait bilong em. Ol gutpela nambis we planti lain i save laikim i stap long tripela eria.
Ol nambis we i stap long North Shores (long North Habour district) em ol i stap long Pacific Ocean na i stat long Long Bay long hap not na i go long Devenport long hap saut.
Klostu olgeta bilong ol nambis em i seif long swim na planti bilong ol i gat gutpela seid (shade) bilong ol pohuukawa diwai long hait long san.
Ol nambis bilong Tamaki Drive i stap long Waitemata Harbour, long ol 'upmarket' komuniti bilong Mission Bay na St Heliers long Central Auckland.
Dispela ol gutpela nambis i save pulap wantaim ol famili na i save i gat ol gutpela stua i stap long klostu long dispela nambis. Em i seif long swim long ol dispela nambis.
Nambawan lokel bia em 'Number One', em i no wanpela narakain bia, tasol em i nais na i mekim man i pilim gut. Wanpela narapela lokel bia em i "Manta".
I gat planti French wain long dring, tasol ol wain bilong New Zealand na Australia em i isi moa long kisim ol.
Ol lokel wara long tep (tap) em i seif long dringim, tasol em isi long painim botol wara sapos yu pret long wara long tep.
'Flat white' kofi em i narakain samting long ol lain Australia. Wanpela 'short black' em i wanpela ' expresso', 'cappuccino' we i kam wantaim krim (i no 'froth'), na ol i no save mekim ti we i gat milk insait long en.
Ol 'hotpela chocolate' em i stap long stendet bilong ol Belgium. Em i bikpela man i long ol frut jus, tasol ol i nambawan.
Ol i save mekim planti raun i go long ol rip long olgeta taim insait long wanpela yia, na bagarap i kamap long bodi long ol dispela kain samting i save kamap wanwan taim tasol.
Tasol, kisim tok save bilong ol atoriti, bihainim olgeta sain, na ritim na bihainim gut ol tok lukaut.
Ol 'box jellyfish' i save kamap olgeta taim arere long nambis na arere long ol maus wara long Oktoba i go long Epril long hap nat long 1770. Sampela taim ol i ken kamap autsait long ol dispela taim.
Ol sak i stap, tasol i no save kaikai man. Planti bilong ol sak i save pret long manmeri na i save swim i go longwe.
Saltwater Crocodiles i no save stap long solwara olgeta taim, nambawan ples bilong ol long i stap em long ol maus wara we i stap long hap not long Rockhampton.
Pasin bilong makim spes bipo long travela i go long dispela ples bai mekim tingting bilong ol i stap isi olsem ol bai gat sampela hap bilong slip taim ol i kamap long hap.
Planti taim ol 'travel agent' i save wok wantaim wanwan hotel, yu bai lukim olsem yu ken yusim wanpela lokel 'agent' long makim spes bilong stap long o narapela hap, kain olsem ol 'camping ground'.
Ol 'travel agent' i save givim ol offer' we i gat brekfas (breakfast), kar bilong kisim yu i go i kam long eapot o bungim tu ol prais bilong balus tiket na prais bilong hotel.
Ol i ken mekim wanpela 'reservation' bilong yu sapos yu nidim taim long tingting long 'offer' o kisim ol narapela dokumen long go long dispela ples (eksampel, 'visa').
Sampela senis o rikwes em yu mas tokim 'travel agent' pastaim na i no go stret long hotel.
Long ol sampela bikde, bikpela namba bilong ol lain i save pilai musik i mekim kem long dispela ples, na planti bilong ol i save pilim olsem dispela em i impoten hap bilong dispela ekspiriens.
Sapos yu laik stap klostu long ol samting na lukim yu bai nid long go hariap na kisim wanpela ples bilong mekim kem klostu long musik.
Tingim olsem maski musik long ol bikpela hap bilong bikde em i pinis, i gat sampela seksen bilong bikde we ol bai pilai musik i go inap long biknait.
Sampela bikde i gat spesol eria bilong famili we i gat liklik pikinini long mekim kem bilong ol.
Sapos ol i brukim Northern Baltic long winta (winter), sekim lokesen bilong 'cabin', bikos taim em i go namel long ais em i kamap wanpela bikpela nois long ol hap we i bamim ais.
Ol 'cruise' i go long Saint Petersburg i save givim taim long raun long taun. Ol pasindia bilong 'cruise' i no nid long karim visa (lukim ol 'terms').
Ol 'casino' i save traim hat tru long yusim taim na mani we ol 'guest' i kam na spendim. I no gat windua na klok, na ol dua bilong go autsait em i save hat long painim.
Ol i save gat spesol kaikai, dring na ektiviti bilon amamas, long mekim ol 'guest' i amamas, na mekim ol i stap insait long banis.
Sampela bilong ol ples we i save givim ol fri dring we i gat 'alcohol' insait long en. Tasol, taim man i spak em i no inap long skelim gut samting, na olgeta gutpela man bilong 'gamble' i save olsem em i impoten long tingting bilong ol i mas stap stret.
Wanpela husat bai draiv long ples we i stap antap moa o antap long ol maunten i mas tingim olsem i ken i gat sno (snow), ais, o tempritsa (temperature) we i kol nogut tru.
Long ol rot we i gat sno (snow) o ais, 'friction' em i no strong na yu no inap long draiv olsem yu save draiv antap long kolta nating.
Long taim bilong 'blizzard', inap sno (snow) we i ken mekim yu i pas i ken pundaun long sotpela taim tasol.
Na tu, yu bai i no inap long lukluk gut taim sno (snow) i pundaun o blo o win i kamap wara o i kamap ais long ol windua bilong kar.
Long narapela sait bilong dispela samting, ol kondisen bilong ais na sno (snow) em i nomol long planti kantri, na ol kar i save ron i go i kam gut long olgeta de bilong yia.
Ol Safari em ating ol i nambawan samting we i save kisim ol turis i go long Africa na ol i bikpela samting long planti ol visita.
Dispela hap tok 'safari' we planti lain i save yusim em i toktok long travel long graun long lukim ol narakain animal bilong Africa, planti bilong ol em ol animal bilong 'savanna'.
Sampela ol animal, kain olsem ol elefen na 'giraffe', i save laik long kam klostu long ol kar na ol stendet ikwipmen (equipment) bai mekim yu i ken lukim ol gut.
Ol laion, 'cheetah' na 'leopard' em sampela taim ol i save sem long kam ples klia na yu bai lukim ol gut taim yu yusim ol 'binoculars'.
Wanpela 'safari' bilong wokabaut (ol i save kolim tu olsem wanpela "'bush walk'", "hiking safari", o 'going "'footing'") em i pasin bilong wokabaut, long sampela aua o long sampela de.
Paralympics bai i kamap long 24 Ogas i go long 5 Septemba 2021. Sampela ol samting bai kamap long ol narapela lokesen long ol narapela ples long Japan.
Tokyu bai kamap olsem wanpela siti tasol long Asia long hostim tupela sama (summer) Olympics, bikos em i bin hostim ol geim (game) long 1964.
Sapos yu bin makim taim bilong flai na ples bilong stap long 2020 bipo long ol i tokaut olsem ol i senisim taim, yu bai i stap long wanpela hatpela taim.
Ol polisi bilong kenselim (cancel) ol samting i no wankain, tasol stat long pinis bilong Mas planti bilong ol polisi bilong kenselim ol samting we i kamap long koronavaires i no surik i go long Julai 2020, taim ol i bin makim Olympics long kamap.
Ol i tok olsem planti bilong ol tiket bai i stap namel long ¥2,500 na ¥130,000, olsem na mak bilong wanpela nomol tiket bai i kost olsem ¥7,000.
Pasin bilong ainim (iron) ol wet klos i ken helpim ol long drai. Planti ol hotel i gat ain na bod bilong ain i stap bilong yusim, maski sapos wanpela ain i no i stap ples klia insait long rum.
Sapos wanpela ain i no i stap, o sapos yu no tingting long werim soks we ol i ainim, orait yu ken traim yusim wanpela 'hairdryer', sapos em i stap.
Yu mas lukaut long no ken larim laplap i kamap hot tumas (dispela i ken kamapim mekim klos i kamap liklik, o sapos em i hot tumas, klos bai i paia).
I gat ol kainkain we bilong mekim wara i kamap 'pure', sampela i save mekim wok bilong daunim sampela kain samting we i ken kamapim hevi.
Long sampela eria boilim wara long wanpela minit em i inap, long ol narapela eria yu bai nid long boilim wara long sampela minit.
Ol 'filter' em strong bilong wanwan i narakain, na yu mas tingting, bihaim yu mas tingting long baim wara long wanplela botol long wanpela gutpela kampani.
Ol travela i ken bungim kainkain animal bilong bagarapim klos na kaikai we ol i no klia long en insait long ples we ol i kam long en.
Ol 'pest' i ken bagarapim kaikai, mekim skin i skrap, o nogut moa ol i ken kamapim ol 'allergic reaction', spredim 'venom', o mekim sik i kalap long wanpela man i go long narapela.
Ol sik we i save kalap hariap, o ol animal we i save bagarapim ol kilim ol manmeri wantaim fos, em ol i no kam aninit long dispela nem 'pest'.
'Duty free shopping' em i sans long baim ol samting we yu no inap long baim takis na 'excises' long sampela lokesen.
Ol travela we i go long kantri we i gat bikpela takis sampela taim ol i ken seivim (save) bikpela mani, ol i ken seivim long ol prodak taim olsem ol 'alcoholic beverages' na 'tobacco'.
Dispela spes namel long Point Marion na Fairmont em i ol nambawan hatpela kondisen bilong draiv long Buffalo-Pittsburgh Highway, planti taim em i go insait long ol ples we i no gat planti lain na i stap longwe.
Sapos yu no save long draiv long ol rot autsait long siti, yu mas strongim yu yet: i gat ol ples we i sut i go daun o i kam antap, i gat ol liklik rot we i no gat spes long ron, na ol sap kona.
Ol tok save long mak bilong spit i stap daunbilo moa long ol narapela seksen — planti taim em i 35-40 mph (56-64 km/h) — na pasin bilong bihainim ol gut em i moa impoten long sakim tok.
Mipela i no save bilong wanem na ol mobail fon sevis i strong moa long hia na i no strong long planti ol narapela hap bilong dispela rot, kain olsem Pennsylvania Wilds.
Ol 'German pastry' em ol i gutpela tru, na long Bavaria, ol i gat gutpela teist na i gat kainkain, wankain olsem ol dispela bilong ol lain i stap saut, ol Austria.
I gat ol planti 'fruit pastry', na i gat ol epol we ol i wokim 'pastry' long en i save stap long olgeta taim bilong yia, na ol 'cherry pastry' na 'plum pastry' em ol i save mekim long taim bilong sama (summer).
Planti bilong ol kaikai bilong ol German i save gat ol 'almond', 'hazelnut', na ol narapela 'nut'. Ol keik (cake) we planti lain i save long en em i save go gut wantaim wanpela strongpela kap kofi.
Sapos yu laikim sampela liklik 'pastry' we i teist nais, traim dispela ol i save kolim Berliner, Pfannkuchen o Krapfen long wanwan rijen.
Wanpela 'curry' em i wanpela kaikai we i yusim ol 'herb' na 'spice', wantaim ol abus o kumu.
Wanpela 'curry' em i ken "drai" o "wet" bihainim mak bilong wara yu yusim.
Long ol rijen insait long Northern India na Pakistan, ol i save yusim 'yogurt' insait long ol 'curry'; long Southern India na sampela 'coastal' rijen bilong dispela ples, ol i save yusim milk bilong kokonas.
I gat 17,000 ailan long makim wanpela long en, kaikai bilong Indonesia em i wanpela bikpela nem we i karampaim ol kainkain kaikai we yu ken painim long olgeta hap bilong Indonesia.
Tasol, sapos yu yusim dispela tok na nating, dispela tok em bai min kaikai i kam long 'central' na 'eastern' hap bilong Java ailan.
Nau em i stap long olgeta hap bilong grup ailan, kaikai bilong Java em i gat ol 'seasoned dishes', na namba fleiva bilong kaikai bilong Java em pinat, 'chilie', suga (dispela em kokonas sugar bilong Java) na ol kainkain 'aromatic spices'.
Ol 'stirrup' em ol sapot bilong lek bilong 'rider' we i hangamap i kam daun long sait sait bilong 'saddle'.
Ol i save givim moa 'stability' long 'rider', tasol ol i ken kamapim hevi long sait bilong sefti bikos nogut lek bilong 'rider' i pas insait long ol.
Sapos wanpela 'rider' i pundaun long wanpela hos, tasol lek bilong em i pas long 'stirrup', hos i ken pulim ol taim em i ranawe. Long daunim mak bilong dispela hevi long kamap, ol 'rider' i mas mekim samting long abrusim dispela.
Namba wan, planti ol 'rider' i save werim ol 'riding boots' we i gat wanpela 'heel' na wanpela 'sole' we i 'smooth' na longpela.
Narapela samting, sampela 'saddle', dispela em ol English 'saddle', ol i gat ol 'safety bar' we i save larim 'stirrup leather' i pundaun i go daun long 'saddle' sapos wanpela 'rider' i pundaun i go baksait.
Cochamó Valley -nambawan hap bilong mekim 'climbing' long Chile, em ol kolim Yosemite of South America, em i gat ol kainkain bikpela 'granite wall' na 'crag'.
Het bilong maunten i gat ol naispela samting bilong lukim. Ol lain bilong klaim long olgeta hap bilong graun i wok long kamapim ol nupela rot namel long ol planti wol.
Ol 'downhill snowsport', we i gat 'skiing' na 'snowboarding', em ol 'sport' we planti lain i save long en na yu bai slaid (slide) i go daun long wanpela hap wantaim 'skis' o 'snowboard' we ol i pasim long lek bilong yu.
'Skiing' em i wanpela ektiviti bilong raun we ol lain i save laik long mekim, ol i kolim "'ski bums'," ol i save plenim holide bilong ol long mekim 'skiing' long wanpela lokesen.
Dispela tingting bilong 'skiing' em i bilong bipo yet – i gat ol peinting (painting) long hol bilong ston we i soim ol lain i ski long taim i go bek olsem 5000 BC!
'Downhill skiing' olsem wanpela 'sport' em i go bek long kain olsem '17th century' o moa, na long 1861 ol Norwegians i opim namba wan 'recreational ski club' long Australia.
'Backpacking by ski': Dispela ektiviti em ol i save kolim tu olsem 'backcountry ski', 'ski touring' o 'ski hiking'.
Em i wankain, tasol ol i no save bungim wantaim 'alpine styel ski touring' o 'mountaineering', dispela laspela wan em ol i save mekim long ples we i sap na i nidim 'skis' na 'boots' we i sap moa.
Tingim 'skiing route' olsem em i wankain long 'hiking route'.
Long gutpela kodisen yu bai inap long karamapim ol bikpela hap moa sapos yu ski na i no wokabaut – tasol wanwan taim yu bai kisim ol spit bilong 'cross country skiing' taim yu no karim wanpela hevipela bek long ol dispela hap bilong ski.
Europe em i wanpela kontinen (continent) we i liklik, tasol em i gat planti indipenden kantri. Planti taim, long raun i go long planti kantri em bai min olsem yu bai go insait long planti 'visa application' na 'passport control' moa long wanpela taim.
Schengen zone, em i narakain, sampela taim em i save stap olsem wanpela kantri bilong em yet.
Sapos yu stap insait long dispela 'zone', yu ken kalapim boda na yu bai i no inap go long 'passport control checkpoint' gen.
Wankain, taim yu gat wanpela Schengen visa, yu no nid long aplai long ol visa long wanwan bilong ol Schengen memba kantri, na dispela seivim taim, mani na pepawok.
I no gat wanpela bikpela tok we olgeta lain i yusim long makim wanem ol samting em ol i 'antique'. Sampela 'agency' bilong kisim takis i save tok olsem ol samting we i gat moa long 100 krismas em ol i 'antique'.
Dispela hap tok i save senis long wanwan ples, long sampela ples kain olsem North America em namba bilong krismas i no bikpela tumas tasol long Europe em bai i bikpela.
Ol 'handicraft' em ol i kolim ol olsem ol 'antique', maski ol i no gat bikpela krismas wankain olsem ol narapela samting we fektori (factory) i mekim planti long wanpela taim.
Pasin bilong lukautim 'reindeer' em i wanpela impoten wok namel long ol Sámi na kalsa bilong dispela wok em i impoten tu long ol narapela lain we i gat narapela wok insait long komuniti bilong ol.
Bipo, i no olgeta Sámi i bin stap insait long wok bilong lukautim planti lain 'reindeer', tasol ol i stap long painim pis, painim abus na kain olsem, planti bilong ol i save gat 'reindeer' bilong karim kago.
Tude planti Sámi i mekim ol wok bilong tude. Wok bilong givim sevis long turis em i save wanpela impoten rot bilong kisim mani long ol Sápmi, long Sámi eria.
Maski planti lain i save yusim, bikpela moa namel long ol lain we i bilong Romani, dispela hap tok "Gypsy" em i no gutpela tok bikos ol i save yusim long toktok long ol negatif samting na ol rong tingting long Romani manmeri.
Sapos kantri we yu bai go long en em ol lain i tok save long sampela samting we yu mas lukaut long en, sampela senis bai kamap long 'travel health insurance' o 'trip cancellation insurance' bilong yu.
Na tu, yu ken kisim tok save i kam long gavman na i no bilong yu yet, tasol tok save bilong ol em i bilong ol sitisen (citizen) bilong ol.
Wanpela eksampel, ol sitisen bilong America long Middle East em ol bai i stap long narapela we long ol lain long Europe na ol Arab.
Ol 'advisory' em ol sotpela tok save long ol samting i kamap insait long politiks bilong wanpela kantri.
Ol tingting i stap long dispela tok save em ol i raitim hariap, i no gat planti infomesen na ol i mekim ol samting i kamap olsem i no gat planti samting i stap insait long en sapos yu skelim wantaim ol infomesen i stap long narapela hap.
Weda (weather) nogut em i wanpela tok we i no tok klia tumas long ol weda we i ken kamapim bagarap, distebim laip bilong ol manmeri, mekim man i dai.
Ol weda (weather) nogut i ken kamap long kainkain hap bilong dispela graun, na i gat kainkain, dispela em bai bihainim ples, envairomen, na ol kondisen bilong 'atmosphere'.
Ol 'high winds', 'excessive precipitation', na 'wildfire' em ol sampela samtinng i ken kamap bikos long weda (weather) nogut, wankain tu em ol 'thunderstorm', 'tornado', 'waterspout', na 'cyclone'.
Ol weda (weather) nogut bilong wanwan rijen o sisen em ol 'blizzard', 'snowstorm', 'ice storm', na 'dust storm'.
I gat strongpela tok save i go long ol travela long save long ol weda (weather) we i save kamap long ol eria bikos ol bai mekim senis i kamap long ol plen bilong ol travela.
