Husat lain i mekim plen long go long wanpela kantri we woa i save kamap lng en i mas kisim treining (training) i kam long ol profesenol.
Wanpela 'search' long Internet long 'Hostile environment course' bai inap long givim adres bilong wanpela lokel kampani.
Wanpela kos bai karampaim ol samting we mipela i toktok long hia na bai givim moa infomesen, wantaim sampela ekspiriens.
Wanpela kos bai stap long 2-5-pela de na bai i gat 'role play', planti 'first aid' na sampela treining bilong ol samting bilong pait.
Ol buk na megasin we i toktok long pasin bilong stap long ples nating i save stap long planti hap, tasol i no gat planti pablikesen we i save toktok long ol 'war zone'.
Ol lain bilong travel we i plen long go mekim 'sex reassignment surgery' long narapela kantri i mas ol 'valid documents' bilong ol long yusim taim ol i kam bek.
Pasin bilong wanwan gavman long givim ol paspot (passport) we ol i no makim (X) long man o meri o givim ol dokumen long soim senis long nem na man i go long meri o meri i go long man em i narakain narakain long wanwan gavman.
Pasin bilong gavman bilong narapela kantri long luksave long ol dispela dokumen em i narakain narakain tu.
Pasin bilong sekuriti long sekim ol manmeri long ol 'checkpoint' i wok long kamap nogut moa bihain long Septemba 11, 2001.
Ol lain i laik senisim 'gender' bilong ol i no ken ting olsem ol bai go aninit long 'scanner' na 'privacy' bilong ol bai i stap hait.
Ol 'rip currents' em ol tait bilong solwara we i bruk long nambis na i wok long kam bek, planti taim long wanpela rip o kain samting olsem.
Bikos long 'underwater typology' wara we i kam bek em i bung long ol ples we i dip, na wanpela 'fast current' i go long dispela hap we i dip i ken kamap long hap.
Planti dai i save kamap bikos ol manmeri i pilim tait long traim long swim i kam bek agensim 'current', na dispela em i hat long mekim.
Taim yu kam autsait long 'current', pasin bilong swim i go bek em bai i no inap hat long mekim.
Traim long swim i go long wanpela hap we 'current' i no pulim bek gen o, bihainim mak bilong yu long swim na saposl i gat lain i lukim yu, yu ken tingting long wet long ol lain i ken seivim (save) yu.
'Re-entry shock' i save kamap hariap moa long 'culture shock' (i no gat 'honeymoon phase'), na em i save stap longpela taim na em i ken kamap long mak we i bikpela moa long 'culture shock'.
Ol travela husat i no save painim hat long lainim long stap long nupela kalsa i save painim hat long lainim gen hau long i stap long kalsa bilong ol yet.
Taim yu stap long narapela kantri na kam bek long haus bilong yu, yu senisim pasin bilong yu long bihainim nupela kalsa na yu lusim sampela bilong ol pasin bilong kalsa bilong yu yet.
Taim yu bin i go long narapela kantri long namba wan taim tru, yu bin isi na traim long lainim samting, yu save olsem ol travela i stap long narapela kantri i mas senisim tingting na pasin bilong ol.
Planti manmeri i no ting olsem pasin bilong i stap isi na lainim samting em impoten long ol travela (traveller) taim ol i kam bek gen long haus bilong ol.
'Pyramid sound and light show' em i wanpela samting we ol pikinini i save laikim na em i stap long dispela eria.
Yu ken lukim ol 'pyramid' long tudak na yu ken lukim ol tu bipo long 'show' i stat.
Olgeta taim yu bai harim saun bilong ol turis na ol lain bilong salim samting. Dispela stori bilong saun na lait em i wankain tru olsem wanpela stori buk.
'Spinx' em i stap long baksait na em i stap olsem man i wok long autim stori.
Ol wanwan hap bilong stori em ol i soim antap long o 'pyramid' na ol i save mekim lait i kamap long ol kainkain 'pyramid'.
South Shetland Islands, em ol i bin painim em long 1819, na moa long wanpela kantri i bin kisim em na em i gat planti senta, sikstinpela i bin ektif (active) yet long yia 2020.
Dispela grup ailan i stap 120 km not long Peninsula. Nambawan bikpela ailan em King George Island we i gat ol man i stap long Villa Las Estrellas.
Ol narapela em Livingston Island, na Deception we 'flooded caldera' bilong volkeno we i ektif (active) yet i save givim wanpela kain lukluk bilong dispela basis.
Ellsworth Land em i rijen we i stap long saut bilong Peninsula, na Bellingshausen Sea i raunim em.
Ol maunten bilong Peninsula long hia i bungim wantaim ol graun i stap antap, na bihain em i stap ples klia gen na i kamapim 360 km sen (chain) bilong Ellsworth Mountains we Minnesota Glacier i brukim i go long tupela hap.
Hap not bilong Sentinel Range i gat ol longpela maunten tru bilong Antarctica, Vinson Massif, na Mount Vinson we longpela bilong em i 4892 m.
Long ol ples we i stap longwe, we i no gat 'cell phone coverage', em yu ken yusim wanpela 'satellite phone' tasol.
Wanpela 'satellite phone' em i no inap long kisim ples bilong wanpela mobail fon, bikos yu bai nid long sanap autsait na yu mas lukim olsem 'satellite' i stap ples klia na yu ken ring.
Dispela sevis em planti taim ol sip i save yusim, na ol 'pleasure craft', wantaim ol 'expedition' husat i gat nid long yusim 'remote data' na 'remote voice'.
Lokel 'telephone service provider' bilong yu bai inap long givim moa infomesen long yu long hau yu ken konekt long dispela sevis.
Wanpela samting we planti manmeri husat i wok long mekim plen long i gat 'gap-year' i wok long mekim em long travel na lainim samting.
Dispela em i planti ol lain i lusim skul i wok long mekim, dispela em i mekim ol i kisim wanpela yia long malolo bipo long ol i go long univesiti, na ol i no stopim skul bilong ol.
Planti taim, pasin bilong enrol na go long wanpela 'gap-year course' long narapela kantru em i ken mekim ol sans bilong yu long muv i go long bikpela skul long kantri bilong yu yet i go antap.
Planti taim bai i gat skul fi long enrol long ol dispela edukesen progrem.
Finland em i wanpela gutpela kantri bilong raun long bot. Dispela "'Ples bilong tausen raunwara'" i gat planti tausen ailen insait long ol raunwara na long ol solwara.
Long ol liklik ailan na ol raunwara, yu bai no inap nidim wanpela 'yatch'.
Ol liklik ailan long solwara na nambawan bikpela raunwara i inap long wanpela 'yatch' o liklik bot o 'kayak' we i ken givim ol narapela we bilong kisim amamas.
'Boating' o pasin bilong raun long bot em i wanpela samting we olgeta manmeri long Finland i save laik long mekim. Ol i gat planti bot, wanpela bot em i inap long 7-pela o 8-pela manmeri.
Dispela em i wankain long Norway, Sweden na New Zealand, tasol em i narakain liklik (eksampel long Netherlands, dispela namba em i 40).
Planti bilong ol Baltic Cruises i save larim ol lain i stap longpela taim long St. Petersburg, Russia.
Dispela em i min olsem yu ken lukim siti we i gat histori bilong en long sampela de taim yu kam bek long nait na slip long sip.
Sapos yu go sua long sait bilong wara wantaim ol 'shipboard excursion' yu bai no gat nid long i gat wanpela narapela visa (dispela em i stat long 2009).
Sampela bilong ol 'cruise' i save tok olsem ol i karim ol lain i go long Berlin, Germany insait long ol 'brochure' bilong ol. Olsem yu ken lukim long mep (map) i stap antap Berlin i no stap klostu long solwara na wanpela visit long siti em i no stap insait long prais bilong 'cruise'.
Pasin bilong flai long balus em i ken wanpela ekspiriens wei mekim ol manmeri i gat kainkain krismas na i kam long kainkain ples i pret, bikpela moa em sapos ol i no bin flai bipo o i bin stap insait long wanpela samting nogut we i kamap long balus bipo.
Em i no samting bilong sem long en: em i no narakain long ol narapela samting ol manmeri i save pret long em na ol narapela samting ol planti manmeri i save les long en.
Long sampela manmeri, pasin bilong klia gut long wanem wanpela balus i save wok na wanem samting i save kamap taim balus i ron i ken helpim ol long daunim ol pret we i save kamap long ol samting we ol i no save long en o ol i pilim olsem ol i no kontrolim.
Ol 'courier' kampani em ol i save baim ol gut long bringim ol samting hariap. Planti taim, em i impoten long mekim dispela wantaim ol dokumen bilong bisnis, ol 'merchandise' o 'spare parts' long mekim wanpela ripea (repair) hariap.
Long wanpela 'route', ol bikpela kampani i gat ol balus bilong ol yet, tasol long ol narapela 'route' na long ol liklik bisnis i bin i gat wanpela problem.
Sapos ol i salim samting long kago balus, long sampela 'route' em bai kisim planti de long go insait long 'unloading' na 'customs'.
Wanpela we tasol bilong salim samting hariap em long salim em olsem wanpela 'checked luggage', Ol lo bilong 'airline' bai i no inap long ol bek we i no gat pasindia, na dispela hap em yu bai helpim.
Isipela we bilong ron long balus insait long namba wan klas o bisnis klas em long yusim bikpela mani long kisim dispela naispela sevis (o, i gutpela moa, larim kampani bilong yu i yusim dispela mani long yu).
Tasol, dispela i no save kam long liklik prais: planti taim, yu ken baim prais we i go antap foapela taim moa long prais bilong ekonomi klas long kisim bisnis klas tiket, na yu bai baim prais we i go antap 11-pela taim moa long kisim tiket bilong namba wan klas.
I no gat as bilong askim long diskaun prais long bisnis klas o namba wan klas long ol 'direct flights', long wanpela ples i go long narapela ples.
Ol balus kampani i save gut tru olsem i gat wanpela grup bilong ron long balus we i save laik long baim bikpela mani long i go hariap long wanpela hap na kisim gutpela sevis insait long balus, olsem na ol i save sasim dispela kain prais.
Kapitol bilong Moldova em Chişinău. Lokel tok ples bilong dispela ples em Romanian, tasol ol i save yusim Russian long planti hap.
Moldova em i wanpela 'republic' we i gat kainkain hauslain we i bin kisim taim nogut long kros na pait i kamap namel long ol hauslain.
Long 1994, dispela kros na pait i bin mekim na wanpela kantri ol i kolim Transnistria Republic i kamap long 'eastern' Moldova, we i gat gavman na karensi (currency) bilong em yet, tasol ol i no luksave long em olsem wanpela UN memba kantri.
Ol stretim bek gen ol 'economic link' namel long dispela tupela hap bilong Moldova maski ol toktok bilong politiks i no kamap gut.
Nambawan lotu long Moldova em Orthodox Christian.
Izmir em i namba tri bikpela siti insait long Turkey wantaim wanpela populesen long kain olsem 3.7 milien, namba tu bikpela port bihainim long Istanbul, na em i wanpela bikpela senta bilong trenspot (transport).
Bipo em i bin wanpela siti ol i kolim Smyrna, nau em i kamap olsem siti bilong tude, em i divelop pinis, na planti wok bisnis i save kamap long en, em i stap raunim wanpela basis na ol maunten i raunim em.
Ol bikpela rot, ol bilding i gat glas long fran na ol stoa bilong tude em ol i gat ol 'red-tiled roof' we i tredisinel, '18th century' maket, na ol olpela 'mosque' na sios, tasol dispela siti em olsem wanpela siti bilong Mediterranean Europe na i no Turkey bilong bipo.
Dispela liklik ples Haldarsvík em yu ken stap long em na lukluk i go long ailan bilong Eysturoy we i stap klostu na em i gat wanpela narapela kain sios we seip (shape) bilong em i olsem 'octagon'.
Long arere bilong dispela sios, i gat ol narapela kain stetu (statue) bilong ol balus pisin we ol i wokim long 'marble' na i stap antap long sampela ston.
Yu bai no inap westim taim bilong yu long wokabaut hap aua i go long dispela liklik ples we i gat ol narapela kain samting.
Long hap not na i stap long ples we isi long go long en em dispela ol i kolim Sintra we i gat histori na i nais tru na planti ol lain long narapela kantri i save long en taim ol ritim toktok bilong Lord Byron long ol naispela samting i stap long em.
Scotturb Bus 403 i save ron olgeta taim i go long Sintra, na stop long Cabo da Roca.
Na tu long hap not yu ken go Sanctuary of Our Lady of Fatima (Shrine), wanpela ples we olgeta lain i save long en bikos long ol stori bilong Maria mama bilong Jisas i kamap long en.
Plis tingim olsem yu bai lukim wanpela bikpela matmat we ol i planim planti lain long en, tu dispela ples em i gat bikpela mining long planti manmeri long dispela graun.
I gat planti manmeri i stap laip yet husat i bin stap long dispela taim, na planti lain moa husat i gat ol lain we ol laikim i bin dai o ol i bin wok go na dai long hap, ol Jew na ol lain i no Jew wantaim.
Plis soim bikpela rispek long dispela ples. No ken mekim ol tok pilai long Holocaust o Nazis.
No ken bagarapim dispela ples taim yu put mak ol skrapim 'graffiti' i go insait long ol samting.
Ol nambawan tok ples bilong Barcelona em Catalan na Spanish. Klostu hap namba bilong ol lain i stap long hap i save tok ples Catalan, bikpela namba moa i save long em, na klostu olgeta lain i save long Spanish.
Tasol, planti bilong ol sain i tok long tok ples Catalan tasol bikos lo i tok olsem em i nambawan bikpela tok ples bilong dispela hap.
Tasol, ol i save yusim tok ples Spanish long ol pablik trenspot na ol narapela hap.
Ol tok save insait long Metro em ol i save mekim long tok ples Catalan tasol, tasol ol samting we ol i no plen long mekim em wanpela 'automatic' sistem i save mekim dispela tok save long ol kainkain tok ples olsem Spanish, English, French, Arabic na Japanese.
Ol lain long Paris i gat nem long soim pasin we i no gutpela kain olsem tingim ol yet, i no mekim gutpela pasin, ting olsem ol i impoten moa long ol narapela.
 Maski dispela em i wanpela 'stereotype' we i no stret, nambawan we long stap long Paris em long mekim ol gutpela pasin, ekt olsem wanpela man o meri husat i "bien élevé" (papamama bilong em i skulim em gut). Em bai mekim isi long i go i kam long Paris.
Ol pasin bilong ol lain long Paris bai senis hariap tru sapos yu soim sampela gutpela pasin.
Plitvice Lakes nesinel park em i gat planti bikpela diwai, planti bilong ol dispela diwai em 'beech', 'spruce', na ol 'fir' diwai, na em i gat miks Alpine na Mediterranean plent (plant).
Em i gat kainkain ol plent (plant), bikos long kainkain 'microclimate' bilong en, ol kainkain graun na level bilong graun em i stap long en.
Dispela eria em i ples bilong ol kainkain animal na pisin.
Ol animal we i no stap long planti hap kain olsem 'European brown bear', 'wolf', 'owl', 'lynx', 'wild cat', na 'capercaillie' i stap long hap, wantaim ol narapela animal we i stap long planti hap.
Taim yu go lukim ol 'monastery', ol meri i mas werim ol sket we i karamapim ni (knee) na tu, ol i mas karamapim ol solda (shoulder) bilong ol.
Planti bilong ol 'monastery' i save givim ol laplap long ol meri we i no redi na i kam, tasol sapos yu bringim laplap bilong yu, gutpela moa long bringim wanpela we i gat ol brait (bright) kala, yu bai kisim wanpela smail long wanpela 'monk' o wanpela 'nun' long dua bilong go insait.
Wankain taim yu, ol man i mas werim ol trausers we i karamapim ni (knee).
Dispela tu em ol i boroim (borrow) long ol trausers i stap long dua bilong i go insait, tasol dispela klos em ol i no save wasim bihain long wanpela meri i werim olsem yu bai no inap pilim gut long werimg ol dispela sket. Long ol man em wanpela sais i ken inapim olgeta man!
'Majorcan cuisine', kain olsem ol wankain eria insait long Mediterranean, i save yusim bret, ol gaden kaikai na mit (planti taim em mit bilong pik), na i save yusim 'olive oil' long olgeta samting.
Wanpela kaikai bilong avinun we planti lain i save laikim, em ol i save laikim long mekim long taim bilong sama (summer), em i Pa amb Oli: Bret wantaim 'olive oil', tomato, na wanem samting i stap bilong givim fleiva kain olsem 'cheese', tuna pis na kain olsem.
Olgeta 'noun', we i stap wantaim dispela wod Sie bilong yu, ol i save stat wantaim wanpela kapitol leta, maski em i stap insait long namel bilong sentens (sentence).
Dispela em i impoten we bilong luksave long wanem em ol 'verb' na wanem em ol 'object'.
Na tu, em i save mekim pasin bilong rit i isi moa, maski pasin bilong rait em i hap liklik taim yu laik painimaut sapos wanpela 'verb' o 'adjective' em ol i yusim insait long 'substantivized form' bilong em.
'Pronunciation' em i tok ples Italian bikos planti bilong ol wod em ol i save kolim olsem hau ol i raitim.
Ol leta bilong tingim em 'c' na 'g', bikos 'pronunciation' bilong ol i save senis bihainim 'vowel' we i kam bihain long ol.
Na tu, yu mas sekim olsem yu kolim 'r' na 'rr' narakain: 'caro' em i min olsem dia, na 'carro' em i min olsem 'chariot'.
Perian tok ples em i isi na grama (grammar) bilong em i isi long bihainim.
Olsem na, taim yu ritim dispela 'grammar primer' em bai helpim yu tru long grama (grammar) bilong tok ples Persia na yu ken save gut long ol hap toktok.
Em i klia tru olsem, sapos yu save long wanpela Romance tok ples, em bai isi moa long yu long lainim Portuguese.
Tasol, ol manmeri husat i save liklik log Spanish i ken ting olsem Portuguese em i klostu wankain olsem Spanish na i no gat nid long stadi long em.
Ol 'observatory' bilong taim bipo em ol i no yusim moa long tude, na nau ol i stap olsem ol 'museum', o ples bilong edukesen.
'Light pollution' i no bin wanpela problem long mak we em i stap long en tude, ol i save stap long ol siti o long ol skul, na i isi long go long en na i no olsem ol dispela we ol i bildim long tude.
Planti ol 'research telescope' em ol i bikpela fesiliti (facilty) we i stap long ol longwe ples long ol gutpela 'atmospheric condition'.
Pasin bilong lukluk long 'cherry blossom', we ol i kolim olsem hanami, em i pat bilong kalsa bilong Japanese stat long '8th century' na i kam.
Dispela pasin em i kam long Chain we ol i save lukluk long ol 'plum blossom'.
Long Japan, empera (emperor) i save holim ol pati bilong ol namba wan 'cherry blossom' pati bilong em yet na ol memba bilong 'aristocracy' long Imperial Court.
Ol plent (plant) i save luk nais tru insait long wel envaironmen bilong ol, olsem an no ken traim long rausim "wanpela tasol" na kisim olsem ‘specimen’.
Sapos yu go long wanpela gaden we ol i stretim bilong ol lalin i kam na lukim, pasin bilong kolektim ol "'specimen’" bai mekim na ol i rausim yu, na ol i no inap toktok planti.
Singapore em i seif tru na isi long i go i kam, na yu ken baim kainkain samting taim yu kamap long hap.
Tasol bikos em i stap long "‘high tropics’" sampela ‘degree’ not long ‘equator’ yu bai nid long stap insait long hot (olgeta taim) na strongpela san (taim san i klia, dispela i no save kamap planti taim).
Na tu, i gat sampela bas (bus) i save go long hap not long Hebron, dispela em i ples we ol i planim ol papa bilong bilip insait long Baibel Abraham, Isaac, Jacob, na ol meri bilong ol.
Sekim sapos ol bas (bus) yu tingting long kisim em bai go insait long Hebron na i no go klostu long setelmen (settlement) bilong ol Jewish long Kiryat Arba.
Ol wara we i stap insait long ples em ol gutpela samting bilong mekim holide long en.
Eksampel, taim yu go lukim ol kasol (castle) insait long Loire Valley, Rhine valley o kisim wanpela ‘cruise’ i go long ol naispela siti long Danube o ‘boating’ long Erie Canal.
Na tu, ol i save makim ol ‘route’ we planti lain i save go wokabaut o ‘cycling’ long em.
Krismas em i wanpela bilong ol impoten holide bilong Christianity, na ol i save amamasim dispela de olsem bonde bilong Jisas.
Planti bilong ol pasin we ol lain i save mekim long dispela holide em ol lain i no Kristen na ol kantri we i no Kristen kantri i save bihainim long olgeta hap bilong graun.
I gat tredisen (tradition) i bilong no ken slip long Easter nait na stap long wanpela ples klia long lukim san i kirap.
I gat ol Kristen bilip we i toktok long dispela tredisen (tradition), tasol em i wankain olsem tredisen bilong Spring na Fertility bipo long taim bilong Kristen bilip.
Ol sios we i save bihainim pasin bilong lotu long bipo i save holim wanpela Easter Vigil long Sarere nai long Easter wiken, i gat ol manmeri bilong lotu i save i kam bung na ol i save mekim selebresen (celebration) long biknait i pinis na moning i kamap long amamas long Krais i kirap long dai.
Olgeta animal we i kam kamap long ailen i kam long hia taim ol i swim, flai o trip antap long wara.
Bikos long longpela distens (distance) long kontinen (continent) ol 'mammal' i no inap long mekim longpela wokabaut na dispela i mekim 'giant tortoise' i kamap olsem nambawan animal bilong kaikai gras insait long Galapagos.
Taim ol man i kam long Galapagos, planti 'mammal' we ol i bin kisim i kam em meme, hos, kau, rat, pusi na dok.
Sapos yu go lukim Arctic o Antarctic eria long taim bilong winta (winter) yu bai lukim 'polar night', dispela em i min olsem san i no inap kirap long 'horizon'.
Dispela em i gutpela sans bilong lukim Aurora borealis, taim skai bai tudak long klostu olgeta aua long kilok.
Bikos ol dispela eria i no gat planti manmeri, planti taim 'light pollution' em bai i no wanpela problem, yu bai inap long lukim ol sta.
Japanese kalsa bilong wok em i gat oda bilong em na em i moa fomol (formal) long we ol Westerner i save long en.
Ol 'suit' em ol stendet bisnis klos, na ol wanwok i save kolim wanpela narapela long nem bilong famili bilong ol o ol taitol bilong ol long wok.
Gutpela sindaun insait long wok ples em i bikpela samting, na ol i laikim grup wok na i no pasin bilong tok amamas long samting we wanpela wokman i mekim.
Ol woklain i mas kisim tok orait long ol lain i antap long ol bipo long ol i mekim wanpela disisen, na ol i mas harim tok stia bilong ol lain we ol i wok aninit long en na ol i no ken askim kwesten.
